 om namaḥ saṃvid vapuṣe śivāya atha īśvara pratyabhijñā vimarśinī nirābhāsāt pūrṇāt aham iti purā bhāsayati yad  dvi śākhām āśāste tadanu ca vibhaṅktum nija kalām sva rūpāt unmeṣa prasaraṇa nimeṣa sthiti juṣas tad advaitam vande parama śiva śakti ātma nikhilam śrotraiyambaka sat vaṃśa madhya mukta āmaya sthiteḥ śrosoma ānanda nāthasya vijñāna pratibimbakam anuttara ananya sākṣi pum artha upāyam abhyadhāt  īśvara pratyabhijñā ākhyam yaḥ śāstram yad su nirmalam tad praśiṣyaḥ karomi etām tad sūtra vivṛtim laghum buddhvā abhinavaguptaḥ  aham śrīmat lakṣmaṇa guptatas vṛttyā tātparyam ṭīkayā tad vicāraḥ sūtreṣu eteṣu granthakāreṇa dṛbdham tasmāt sūtra artham manda buddhīn pratīttham samyak vyākhyāsye pratyabhijñā viviktyai sarvatra alpa matau yad vā kutra api su mahā dhiyi na vā anyatra api tu sva ātmani eṣā syāt upakāriṇī granthakāraḥ aparokṣam ātma dṛṣṭa śaktikām parameśvara tanmaya tām paratra saṃcikramayiṣuḥ sva tādātmya samarpaṇa pūrvam avighnena tad sampattim manyamānaḥ parameśvara utkarṣa prahvata aparāmarśa śeṣa tayā parameśvara tādātmya yogya tā āpādana buddhyā prayojanam āsūtrayatiḥ iha prameśvaram prati yā iyam kāya vāc manasām tad eka viṣaya tā niyojanā lakṣaṇā prahvatā sā namaskārasya arthaḥ sā ca tathā kartum ucitā prāmāṇikasya bhavati yadi sarvatas  namaskaraṇīyasya utkarṣam paśyet  anyathā yuktim aparāmṛśataḥ aparama arthe api namaskāra udyatasya sāṃsārika jana madhya pāti tvam eva yathā uktam na vindanti param devam vidyā rāgeṇa rañjitāḥ iti tāvati hi māyīya aśuddha vidyā rāga kalā saṃcāryamāṇasya paśu tvam eva itara apekṣayā tu katipaya adhva uttīrṇa tayā samutkarṣaḥ  api syāt  tad uktam kasya nāma karaṇaiḥ akṛtrimaiḥ paśyataḥ tava vibhūtimakṣatām vibhramāt avarataḥ  api jāyate tvām vyudasya vara da stuti spṛhā iti śrīmat vidyā adhipatinā etaḥ ca āgama kāṇḍe nirūpayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt  nikhila utkarṣa parāmarśanam api tatra svīkāryam yadi api āyāta dṛḍha īśvara śaktipātasya svayam eva iyam iyatī paramaśiva bhūmiḥ abhyeti hṛdaya gocaram na tu atra svātmīyaḥ puruṣakāraḥ kaḥ  api nirvahati sarvasya tasya māyā maya tvena andhatamasa prakhyasya āmāyīyam śuddha prakāśam sva pratidvandvinam prati upāyat|anupapatteḥ vajigamiṣayā niḥśeṣa utkarṣa viśeṣa abhidhīyi jayati ādi śabda anuvedhena parāmarśanīyam iti namaskāre ākṣepyaḥ jaya pada udīraṇe api tādṛśa samutkarṣa atiśaya śālini sva ātmānam aprahvīkurvāṇasya taṭa sthasya paramanātma upakāri tvam iti samutkarṣa viśeṣa ākṣipta eva namaskāraḥ  avaśyam abhyantarī kāryaḥ iti anayā yuktyā jaya namaskāra ekatara prakrame anyatarasya artha ākṣipta tā avaśyam aṅgīkartavyā vandana namana smaraṇa pradhyāna prabhṛtīnām api namaskāra jayati artha mātra parama artha tvāt  iyam eva vartanī atra ayam punar grantha kṛtā tādṛś  prakrama āśritaḥ yatra dvayam api idam sva śabda parāmṛṣṭam eva etad ca padārtha vyākhyāna avasara eva prakaṭībhaviṣyati sva śabda parāmarśaḥ ca sarva jana hita tvāt yukti yuktaḥ sa hi sarvasya eva jhaṭiti hṛdayaṃgamaḥ artha ākṣiptaḥ tu katicid eva prati sva pratibhā udita vāc tattva avamarśa asaṃbhavāt vāc tattva avamarśa śūnyasya ca prakāśasya aprakāśa kalpa tvāt etad ca sphuṭībhaviṣyati abhiprāyeṇa prasiddha jaya namaḥ prabhṛti śabda śaṭyāna āśleṣeṇa imām saraṇim anusarasi sma granthakāraḥ iha yad yad kim cana sphurati tad tad vakṣyamāṇa īśvara rūpa sva ātma prathā mātram tatra tu upāya upeya bhāva prabhṛtiḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  api yathāprakāśam parama artha bhūta  eva prakāśasya anapahnavanīya tvāt  yad āha bhaṭṭativākara vatsaḥ  viveka añjane prakāśa śva eva bhāvānām ityādi na śāpa uktyā vilīyate iti antam tatra tu kārya kāraṇa bhāve api kvacid  paripūrṇa svātantrya lakṣaṇa māheśvarī ana antarīyaka tā kroḍīkṛta ananta śakti cakra cumbita bhāva bhāvita prathā antara vyacadhānam cakāsti sa tu māyīya tvena sthāpayiṣyate jaḍa cetana ādyava antara bheda śata saṃbhinnaḥ ca asau tad kṛtaḥ ca sarvaḥ  ayam niṣpādya niṣpādaka bhāva jñāpya jñāpaka bhāva aṃvabhāsaḥ  loka vyavahāra rūpaḥ yatra tu śuddha sva ātma rūpa prathā ātmaka anuttara śakti śāli nirargalasva ātma prakāśa eva māyīya prathā antara vyavadhāna vandhyaḥ  nibandhanam tatra tasya eva bhagavataḥ kāraṇa tvam eṣa ca anugraha lakṣaṇaḥ  antyaḥ pañcamaḥ pārameśvaraḥ kṛtya viśeṣaḥ para puruṣa artha prāpakaḥ tad nibandhana tvāt  parama artha mokṣasya anyatratyaḥ  hi apavargaḥ kutaścid muktiḥ na sarvata iti niḥśreyasa ābhāsa iti vakṣyāmaḥ sa ca ayam dvitīyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  laukika anvaya vyatireka siddha prasiddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva vilakṣaṇa tvāt sphuṭena rūpeṇa asaṃcetyamānaḥ kādācid ka vastu sadbhāva unneya parama arthaḥ ati durghaṭa kāritva lakṣaṇa aiśvarya vijṛmbhā bhāvita adbhuta bhāvaḥ prathama koṭi saṃbhāvanā śūnya kālika ākāra sva prakāśa āvaraṇa nirākaraṇa manoratha śata duṣprāpa iti evaṃprakāraḥ katham ā dyotaka nipāta sahitena nirūpitaḥ akathaṃcit iti kenacid ca prakāreṇa parameśvara abhinna guru caraṇa samārādhanena parameśvara ghaṭitena eva yathā uktam saṃbandhaḥ  atīva durghaṭaḥ iti ‘a āsādya iti ā samantāt  paripūrṇa rūpa tayā sādayitvā sva ātma upabhoga yogya tām nirargalām gamayitvā iyatā vidita vedya tvena para arthe śāstra karaṇe adhikāraḥ  darśitaḥ anyathā pratāraka tā mātram eva syāt  paurvakālyena sāmanantaryam atra vivakṣitam anyathā tu āsādana tāratamya prāptau māyīya mala kalāpa saṃskāra prakṣaye katham para upadeśaḥ śakya kriyaḥ saṃbhavanti hi māyā garbha adhikāriṇaḥ  viṣṇu viriṃca ādyāḥ tad uttīrṇā api mahāmāyā adhikṛtāḥ śuddha aśuddhā mantra tad īśa tad maheśa ātmānaḥ śuddhā api śrī sadāśiva prabhṛtayaḥ te tu yadīya aiśvarya vipruḍbhiḥ īśvarībhūtāḥ sa bhagavān anavacchinna prakāśa ānanda rūpa svātantrya parama arthaḥ  maheśvaraḥ tasya adāsyam iti anena tad pratyabhijña upapādanasya mahā phala tvam āsūtrayati dīyate asmai svāminā sarvam yathā abhilaṣitam iti dāsaḥ tasya bhāva iti anena parameśvara rūpa svātantrya pātra tā uktā ‘janasya iti yaḥ kaścid  jāyamānaḥ tasya iti anena adhikāri viṣayaḥ  na atra kaścid niyama iti darśayati yasya yasya hi idam svarūpa prathanam tasya tasya mahā phalam prathanasya eva parama artha phala tvāt tasya ca pratibandhaka saṃmataiḥ apratibandhanīya tvāt na hi prathitam aprathitam iti nyāyāt  tad uktam na iha abhikrama nāśaḥ  asti pratyavāyaḥ  na vidyate su alpam api asya darmasya trāyte mahataḥ  bhayāt  iti parama guru pādaiḥ api śiva dṛṣṭau eka vāram pramāṇena śāstrāt vā guru vākyataḥ jñāte śiva tve sarva sthe pratipattyā dṛḍha ātmanā karaṇena na asti kṛtyam kvāpi bhāvanayā api vā sakṛt jhāte suvarṇe kim satyatā karaṇa ādinā sarvadā pitṛmātra ādi tulya dārḍyena satyatā iti janasya anavarata janana maraṇa pīḍitasya iti anena kṛpā āspadatayā upakaraṇīya tvam āha api śabdaḥ sva ātmanaḥ tad abhinnatām āviṣkurvan pūrṇa tvena sva ātmani para artha saṃpatti atirikta prayojana antara avakāśam parākaroti para arthaḥ ca prayojanam bhavati eva tad lakṣaṇa tvāt na hi ayam daiva śāpaḥ sva artha eva prayojanam na para artha iti tasya api atad lakṣaṇa tve sati aprayojana tvāt  saṃpādya tvena abhisaṃhitam yad  mukhya tayā tatas  eva kriyāsu prayojakam tad prayojanam ata eva bheda āde api īśvarasya sṛṣṭi ādi karaṇe para artha eva prayojanam iti darśayitum nyāya nirmāṇa vedhasā nirūpitam yam artham adhikṛtya puruṣaḥ pravartate tad  prayojanam iti icchan iti icchā viṣayīkṛtasya phalasya pravṛttaḥ  hetu tvam śatrā darśayati icchā śaktiḥ ca uttarottaram ucchūna svabhāva tayā kriyāśakti paryantībhavati iti darśayiṣyāmaḥ upaśabdaḥ samīpa arthaḥ tena janasya parameśvara dharma samīpa tā karaṇam atra phalam ata eva āha samasta iti parameśvara tāla ābhe hi samastāḥ saṃpadaḥ tad niḥṣyanda mayyaḥ saṃpannā eva rohaṇa lābhe ratna saṃpada iva pramuṣitasva ātma parama arthasya hi kim anyena labdhena labdha tad parama arthasya api tad anyat  na asti yad  vāñchanīyam yad uktam grantha kṛtā evaḥ bhakti lakṣmī samṛddhānām kim anyat upayācitam enayā vā daridrāṇām kim anyat upayācitam iti evam ṣaṣṭhī samāsena prayojanam uktam bahubrīhiṇā tu upāyaḥ sūcyate samastasya bhāva abhāva rūpasya bāhya abhyantarasya nīla sukha ādeḥ yā saṃpad  saṃpattiḥ siddhiḥ tathātva prakāśaḥ tasyāḥ samyak  avāptiḥ vimarśa rūḍhiḥ sā eva hetuḥ yasyām tad pratyabhijñāyām tathā hi sphuṭatara bhāsa samāna nīla sukha ādi pramā anu eṣaṇa dvāreṇa eva pāramārthika pramātṛ lābha iha upadiśyate yad āha anyatraḥ idam iti asya vicchinna vimarśasya kṛtārtha tā yā sva svarūpe viśrāntiḥ vimarśaḥ saḥ  aham iti ayam iti tathā tatra eva prakāśasya ātma viśrāntiḥ ahaṃbhāvaḥ  hi kīrtitaḥ uktā ca sā eva viśrāntiḥ sarva apekṣā nirodhataḥ svātantryam atha kartṛ tvam mukhyam īśvara tā api ca iti iyatā ca upāye ati durghaṭatva āśaṅkā parākṛtā yad ante nirūpayiṣyati su ghaṭa eṣa mārgaḥ  navaḥ iti tamya maheśvarasya pratyabhijñā pratīpam ātma abhimukhyena jñānam prakāśaḥ pratyabhijñā pratīpam iti sva ātma avabhāsaḥ  hi na ananubhūta pūrvaḥ avicchinna prakāśa tvāt  tasya sa tu tad śaktyā eva vicchinna iva vikalpita iva lakṣyate iti vakṣyate pratyabhijñā ca bhāta bhāsamāna rūpa anusaṃdhāna ātmikā sa eva ayam caitra iti pratisaṃdhānena abhimukhībhūte vastuni jñānam loke api etad putra evaṃguṇa evaṃrūpaka iti evam vā antatas api sāmānya ātmanā vā jñātasya punar abhimukhībhāva avasare pratisaṃdhi prāṇitam eva jñānam pratyabhijñā iti vyavahriyate nṛpam prati pratyabhijñāpitaḥ ayam iti ādau iha api prasiddha purāṇa siddhānta āgama anumāna ādi vidita pūrṇa śakti svabhāve īśvare sati sva ātmani abhimukhībhūte tad pratisaṃdhānena jñānam udeti nūnam sa eva īśvaraḥ aham iti tām enām upapādayāmi iti upapattiḥ saṃbhavaḥ tām saṃbhavantīm tad samartha ācaraṇena prayojaka vyāpāreṇa saṃpādayāmi tathā hi saṃbhavati tāvat  asau avicchinna prakāśa tvāt  nirodhaka abhimata māyā śakti samapasāraṇa mātram eva tu tatra upapādanam pratyabhijñā upapattau sva para vibhāga abhāve tad apekṣam kartṛ abhiprāya ādi asaṃbhāvyam iti para smaipada prayogaḥ ittham ca atra śloke yojanā maheśvarasya dāsyam samasta saṃpad lābha hetum kathaṃcid  āsādya janasya api kathaṃcid  tad pratyabhijñām āsādya prāpayya upakāram samasta saṃpad lābha hetu bhūtam maheśvara dāsya ātmakam icchan tām eva samasta saṃpad samavāpti hetukām tad pratyabhijñām upapādayāmi āsādya iti āvṛtti yojane dvau ṇicau iyati ca vyākhyāne vṛtti kṛtā bharaḥ na kṛtaḥ tātparyavyākhyānāt yad uktam saṃvṛta sautra nirdeśa vivṛti mātra vyāpārāyām iti ṭīkākāreṇa api vṛtti mātram vyākhyātum udyatena na idam spṛṣṭam asmākam tu sūtra vyākhyāna eva udyama iti vibhajya vyākhyātam evam sarvatra evam anena ślokena abhidheyam prayojanam tad prayojanam tad prayojanam adhikāri nirūpaṇam guru parva kramaḥ saṃbandha iti darśitam tathā hi samasta saṃpad lakṣaṇaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ  yaḥ arthaḥ pūrvam puṇya pāpa ādau saṃsāra mūla kāraṇe hetuḥ sa eva pratyabhijñāyate anayā iti karaṇa vyutpattyā upāyaḥ iha loka uttara mārgam prati nirṇītaḥ iti ati durghaṭa kāritva lakṣaṇam aiśvaryam mārgaḥ  nava iti śākhā ante nirūpayiṣyamāṇam sūcayatā upāyaḥ darśitaḥ abhidheya tvena ata eva tathā hi jaḍa bhūtānām iti upakrama pūrvakam śloka antaram bhaviṣyati prayojanam ca pratyabhijñā upāya jñānam tasya prayojanam pratyabhijñānam tasya api prayojanam samasta saṃpad lakṣaṇa pāramaiśvarya eka rūpa rathanam tatas  param na asti eva tasya sarva paryanta phala tvāt aṃśa aṃśikayā api yad uktam mayā eva stotre phalam kriyāṇām athavā vidhīnām paryantatas tvad maya tā eva deva pahlepsavaḥ  ye punar atra teṣām mūḍhā sthitiḥ syāt anavasthayā eva iti etad  vakṣyati tad atra nidadhat padam iti pāda dvayena janasya iti anena adhikārī darśitaḥ yad  nigamayiṣyati aniśam āviśan iti kathaṃcid  iti anena guru parva kramaḥ vakṣyati mahā gurubhiḥ ucyate sma śiva dṛṣṭi śāstre yathā iti evam pratyabhijñātavya samasta vastu saṃgrahaṇena idam vākyam uddeśa rūpam pratijñā piṇḍa ātmakam ca madhya granthaḥ tu hetu ādi nirūpakaḥ iti prakaṭitaḥ  mayā iti ca antyaślokaḥ  nigamana granthaḥ iti evam pañca avayava ātmakam idam śāstram para vyutpatti phalam naiyāyika kramasya eva māyā pade pāramārthika tvam iti granthakāra abhiprāyaḥ kriyā saṃbandha sāmānya ityādiṣu uddeśeṣu prakaṭībhaviṣyati iti tāvat  granthasya tātparyam su janaḥ ca laukikeśvara paricita īśvara viṣaye janam anujīvi guṇa saṃpannam prakāśayati jana viṣaye ca abhigāmikā ādi guṇa saṃpannam īśvaram prakāśayati iti iyā anarthaḥ sāmānyena ṣaṣṭhosamāsena darśitaḥ tasya pratyabhijñā iti etad śloka ākarṇana samaye ca śiṣyāṇām etad artha saṃkramaṇa krameṇa parameśvara tādātmyam eva upajāyate tāvat  tathā hi janasya iti ākarṇanāt  vayam te janana maraṇa pīḍitā aparyupasta vṛttayaḥ ca asmāka mayam upakāram icchan maheśvarasya dāsyam āsādya samasta saṃpad samavāpti hetum tad pratyabhijñām upapādayati tatas ca tad pratyabhijñām evaṃbhūtām vayam prāptā eva iti ittham eva hi adhikāriṇi śāstra arthasya bimba pratibimbavat  saṃkrāntiḥ loḍliṅā ādīnām viṣayībhavati prathama puruṣa artha uttama puruṣa arthe paryasyati na tu tāṭasthyena adhikārī anadhi kāriṇoḥ pratipattau viśeṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt  ārogya kāmāḥ śivām sevantām sevadhvam iti vā vākya arthasya sevāmahai iti evaṃrūpeṇa adhikāriṇi dvitīyā kakṣyā saṃkrāntau tṛṭīya kakṣyām eva bhāvi koṭi patitām api puruṣa artha saṃpattim akāla kalita svarūpa anupraveśena sva ātmīkṛtām abhimanyamāne tatas  eva vitata saṃvid sundara parām arśaḥ  pūrṇa tā abhimāna pratilambhāt  anyasya tu anevaṃrūpa tvena eva anadhikāritā tāṭasthya prāṇā iti tadā āstām avāntaram etad  ati gahanam ca iti sthitam etad  etena ślokena īśvara sāṃmukhyam vineyānām prayojana ādi pratipādanam ca kriyate iti ananta bhāva saṃbhāra bhāsane spandanam param upoddhātāyate yasya tam stumaḥ sarvadā śivam nanu īśvarasya siddhiḥ eva kartavyā kā iyam siddhiḥ na tāvat  utpattiḥ nitya tvāt  na api īśvara siddhi kāra ādayaḥ tasya upapattim vidadhate jñaptiḥ siddhiḥ iti ced  anavacchinna prakāśasya pramāṇa vyāpāra upādheya prakāśa ātmaka siddhi anupayoga eva nanu anavacchinnaḥ tadīyaḥ prakāśa iti katham etad  nīla sukha ādi prakāśe hi tad prakāśaḥ kutas  tad aprakāśe api supta mūrchā ādau nitarām sva prakāśe api vā īśvare pramātḥṇām kim vṛttam yena teṣām pramāṇa vyāpāra anupayoga iti āśaṅkya āha iha ka īśvare kīdṛśe kīdṛśena pramāṇena asti iti jñāna lakṣaṇām siddhim na asti iti jñāna lakṣaṇam vā niṣedham kuryāt  pramātā iti ced  sa eva kaḥ deha ādiḥ jaḍaḥ uta tad anyaḥ  vā kaścid  ātma ādi śabda vācyaḥ saḥ api sva prakāśa svabhāvaḥ  vā na vā deha ādiḥ jaḍaḥ iti ced  sa eva sva ātmani asiddhaḥ paratra kām siddhim kuryāt  ātmā api asvaprakāśaḥ  jaḍa eva tad tulya yogakṣemaḥ sva prakāśa svabhāvaḥ iti ced  kīdṛśena svena rūpeṇa bhāti yadi pariniṣṭhita saṃvid mātra rūpeṇa tadā saṃvidām bhedanam bheditānām ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam na syāt  tena svatantra sva prakāśa ātma tayā tāvat  sa bhāsate bheditānām ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam na syāt  tena svatantra sva prakāśa ātma tayā tāvat  sa bhāsate tathā abhāsamānaḥ ca kīdṛśam īśvaram sādhayet  niṣedhet  vā kartṛ jñātṛ svabhāvam iti ced  nanu sa pramātā eva tathābhūtaḥ iti kaḥ anyaḥ saḥ nanu sarva kartṛtva sarvajña tve pramātuḥ na staḥ na khalu sarva śabda arthaḥ  jñātṛ kartṛ tvayoḥ svarūpam bhinatti bheda darśane api īśvara jñāna cikīrṣā yajña ādeḥ nityasya viṣayeṇa akāraṇa bhūtena anādheya atiśaya tvāt  prakāśam ānatā ānayanam eva viṣaya tvam iti ced  aprakāśa svabhāvasya tathātvam anucitam iti vakṣyāmaḥ prakāśamāna svabhāva tve viṣayaḥ api sarva ātmanā prakāśa eva nimagna iti prakāśaḥ prakāśate iti etāvat mātra paramārtha tve kaḥ sarvajñā sarvajña vibhāgaḥ pramāṇam api evam siddhatva asiddha tvābhyām paryanuyojyam evam siddhiḥ api tasmāt  viṣaya abhimatam vastu śarīra tayā gṛhītvā tāvat  nirbhāsamāna ātmā eva prakāśate viccheda śūnyaḥ suṣuptam api prati prakāśata eva anyathā smṛtyayogāt  prakāśasya ca nitya tvāt  viccheda hetoḥ abhāvena anya pramātṛ apekṣayā ca prakāśamāna tvāt  sva para pramātṛ vibhāgasya tad sṛṣṭasya māyīya tvena vakṣyamāṇa tvāt  sa ca ayam svatantraḥ svātantryam ca asya abhede bhedanam bhedite ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam iti bahu prakāram vakṣyāmaḥ etad eva asya pārameśvaryam mukhyam ānanda mayam rūpam iti pūrvam upāttam kartari iti tad eva tu svātantryam vibhajya vaktum jñātari iti pañcāt nirdiṣṭam jñāna pallava svabhāvā eva hi kriyā iti vakṣyate tena sarva kriyā svatantre sarva śaktike iti yāvat  uktam bhavet  tāvat eva kartari jñātari iti iyam eva ca saṃvid svabhāva tā saṃvid iti tu ucyamānā vikalpya tvena prameya tām spṛśantaḥ  sṛṣṭa tvāt  na parama artha saṃvid  iti vakṣyāmaḥ kartā jñātā ca maheśvara iti abhidhāne api sa eva prakāra āpatet  iti yathā yathā prameya bhūmikā pāda na nyakkāra kalaṅka parihāraḥ śakyaḥ tathā tathā yāvat gati yatitavyam iti bhūta vibhaktyā nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ upadeśa avasare hi sarva ātmanā tāvat  sā prameya tā asya parihartum aśakyā sva ātmani iti svasmin anapāyi rūpe svabhāve iti anena vaiśeṣika ādi abhimata jaḍa ātma vāda nirāsaḥ ādi siddhe iti avicchinna prakāśe iti arthaḥ maheśvare iti etad eva māheśvarya yad  anavacchinna parkāśa tvena jñātṛ kartṛtva dhārā upārohaḥ ajaḍa ātmā iti yasya tu vaiśeṣika ādeḥ jaḍa ātmā sa siddhim karotu īśvara viṣayām anyaḥ tu sāṃkhya ādi niṣedham sāṃkhyaḥ api viṣaya avabhāsana rūpam jñānam buddhi dharmam icchan ātmānam vastu tas  jaḍam eva upaiti na ca jaḍa ātmā sva ātmani api durlabha prakāśa svātantrya leśaḥ kiṃcid  sādhayitum niṣeddhum vā prabhaviṣṇuḥ pāṣāṇa iva na ca ajaḍa ātmanaḥ api etad  ucitam tathā hi sa sva ātmani siddhim ittham kuryāt  yadi asya saḥ abhinava tvena bhāsamānaḥ pūrvam na bhāsate na bhāsanam ced  jaḍa tā eva niṣedham ca ittham vidadhyāt  yadi sa na prakāśate tathā ca jaḍaḥ na ca jaḍasya etad  yuktam iti uktam na api ajaḍasya tasmāt  saṃvid prakāśa eva ghaṭa ādi prakāśaḥ na tu asau svatantraḥ kaścid  vāstavaḥ prakāśa eva ca ātmāḥ tad  na tatra kāraka vyāpāravat  pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ api nitya tvavat  sva prakāśa tvasya api tatra bhāvāt  nanu kāraka vyāpāraḥ pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ ca yadi īśvare na saṃbhavati tarhi pratyabhijñāpayāmi iti yaḥ  vyāpāra uktaḥ sa katamaḥ  vyāpāraḥ iti āśaṅkya āha sa īśvara svabhāva ātmā prakāśate tāvat  tatra ca asya svātantryam iti na kenacid vapuṣā na prakāśate tatra aprakāśa ātmanā api prakāśate prakāśa ātmanā api tatra api prakāśa ātmani sarvathā prakāśa ātmanā prakāśaḥ  bhāgaśas  vā bhāgaśas  prakāśane sarvasya vyatirekeṇa avyatirekeṇa vā katipayasya vyatirekeṇa avyatirekeṇa vā ukta prakāra pūrṇa tayā vā tad amī sapta prakārāḥ tatra prathamaḥ prakāraḥ  jaḍa ullāsaḥ antyaḥ parama śiva ātmā madhyamā jīvā bhāsāḥ sā eva bhagavataḥ  māyā vimohinī nāma śaktiḥ tad vaśāt  prakāśa ātma tayā satatam avabhāsamāne api ātmani bhāgena aprakāśana vaśāt  anupalakṣite sarvathā hṛdayaṃgamībhāvam aprāpte ata eva pūrṇa tā avabhāsana sādhyām arthakriyām akurvati tad pūrṇa tā avabhāsana ātmaka abhimāna viśeṣa siddhaye pratyabhijñā vyākhyāta pūrvā pradarśyate katham śakteḥ īśvara niṣṭha tvena prasiddhāyāḥ  dṛkkriyā ātmikāyāḥ āviṣkaraṇena pradarśanena abhimāna sādhya artha kriyāṇām tad abhimāna siddhyā vinā asiddheḥ tathā ca dṛṣṭāntam darśayati taiḥ taiḥ api upayācitaiḥ iti etad uktam bhavati na kārakavyāpāraḥ  bhagavati na api jñāpakavya apāraḥ ayam api tu moha apasāraṇa mātram etad  vyavahāra sādhanānām pramāṇānām tāvatī eva viśrānteḥ ghaṭaḥ ayam agra gaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  iti anena hi ghaṭaḥ  na jñāpyate pratyakṣeṇa eva prakāśamāna tvāt  anyathā pakṣe hetu asiddheḥ kevalam moha mātram apasāryate yaḥ ca ayam mohaḥ tad apasāraṇam ca yad  tad ubhayam api bhagavata eva vijṛmbhā mātram na tu adhikam kiṃcid  iti uktam vakṣyate ca nanu paridṛśyamāne bhāva rāśau kimīyā śaktiḥ āviṣkriyate kam ca prati iti jaḍānām tāvat  na jñāna ātmikā śaktiḥ asti kriyā ātmikā api svātantrya prāṃā svātantrya vyapagamāt  asaṃbhāvanā bhūmiḥ eva tathā ca rathaḥ  gacchati iti ādau upacāram kecana pratipannāḥ na ca jaḍān prati vyavahāra sādhanam ucitam atha ajaḍa jīvat janata adhikāreṇa ubhayam api tarhi sarvasya sva ātmā maheśvara iti dūrataram viprakarṣitā pratyāśā tad etad  āśṅkya nirūpayati tathā hi iti yukti upakramam dyotayati dṛśyatām kila iti arthaḥ tathā iti anena sādhyam sūcyate hinā hetuḥ iti anye prakṛtam sādhyam hetu siddhi āyat tam upakramyate iti arthaḥ tena iti buddhi vartinā tatas  eva smaryamāṇena granthena varṇayiṣyamāṇena prakāreṇa yasmāt  sarvam etad  yuktam iti tathā hi iti śabdasya vā arthaḥ iha tāvat  bhāva rāśiḥ yathā vimṛśyate tathā asti astitvasya prakāśam śaraṇīkurvataḥ prakāśa prāṇita deśīyam āśritya samunmevāt  avimṛṣṭam hi yadi vastu tad na nīlam na pītam na sat  na asat iti kuta iti paryanuyoge kim uttaram syāt  tena yad  yathā yāvat  avādhitam vimṛśyate tad  tathā tāvat  asti tad  eva deśa kāla ākāra vitata ātmānaḥ  api dravya kriyā saṃbandha ādayaḥ eka tvena paramārtha santa iti vakṣyate kriyā saṃbandha sāmānya ityādinā tatas ca vitatam api idam viśvam saṃkṣepa vimarśa daśa adhirohe jaḍam jīvat ca iti etāvatā dvaya rūpeṇa asti tatra jaḍā vimṛśyamānā na svatantrā bhavanti vimṛśyamāna tā hi teṣām na sva śarīra viśrāntaḥ kaḥ  api dharmaḥ jaḍatva abhāva prasaṃgāt  mama nīlam bhāti mayā nīlam jñāyate iti teṣām jaḍa bhūtānām cit maya tve api māyā ākhyayā īśvara śaktyā jāḍyam prāpitānām jīvantam pramātāram āśritya pratiṣṭhā tad pramātra abhimukhyena avasthānam tatas  jaḍā nāma na pṛthak  santi yathā uktam grantha kṛtā evaḥ evam ātmani asat kalpāḥ prakāśasya eva santi amī jaḍāḥ prakāśa eva ekaḥ sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti sa eva hi sva ātmanā san vaktavyaḥ  yasya anyān upahitam rūpam cakāsti na ca bhā rūpān upahitam jaḍam nāma kiñcid  tena jaḍānām hi śaktiḥ āviṣkriyate jaḍān prati iti etad  tāvat  nirutthānam eva ye tu anye jaḍebhyaḥ  jīvanta iti nāma prasiddhāḥ teṣām api śarīra prāṇa puryaṣṭaka śūnya ākārāḥ tāvat  jaḍā eva iti teṣām api kim ucyate ata eva ghaṭa śarīra prāṇa sukha tad bh|ava rūpam yad lagnam bhāti tad eva jīva rūpa bhūtam satyam tasya ca āpāte yadi api bahu tvam bhāti tathā api tad  jaḍa ātmaka vedya śarīra ādi upādheḥ tatas tad apārabha arthikam anyonya āśrayāt jīvā hi jaḍa bhedāt  bheda bhāginaḥ jaḍāḥ ca jīva bhedāt  etad dehaḥ  ayam etad vedyaḥ  ayam iti bhedam upeyuḥ nīla pīta ādi bhāva bhedāḥ tu pramātṛ saṃlagna tayā bheda bhūmim eva parama dhirūḍhā iti kim tena tad ayam jīvānām abheda eva saṃpanna iti jīvan pramātā iti jātam jīvanam ca jīvana kartṛ tvam tad ca jñāna kriyā ātmakam yaḥ  hi jānāti ca karoti ca sa jīvati iti ucyate tad ayam pramātā jñāna kriyā śakti yogāt  īśvara iti vyavaharta vayaḥ purāṇa āgama ādi prasiddha īśvaravat tad prasiddhau  api sarva viṣaya jñāna kriyā śaktimattva svabhāvam eva aiśvaryam tanmātra anubandhi tvāt eva siddham tad api ca kalpita īśvare rāja ādau tathā vyāpti grahaṇāt  yaḥ  yāvati jñātā kartā ca sa tāvati īśvarp rājā iva anīśvarasya jñātṛtva kartṛ tve svabhāva viruddhe yatas  ātmā ca viśvatra jñātā kartā ca iti siddhā pratyabhijñā jñāna kriyā śaktaḥ  eva svābhāvikyau aprarūḍha bheda unmeṣe sadāśiva īśvarau bhedasya sāmānyatas  prarohe vidyā kale viśoṣataḥ prarohe buddhi karma indriya gaṇa iva bhaviṣyati jaḍā iti ajīvantaḥ anye ca jīvanta iti āpāte tāvat  bhāti na tu saṃvid āpāte bhāti iti jīvatām iti jaṅgamā eva amī ittham nirdiṣṭāḥ nanu jñāna kriye eva katham siddhe yata aiśvarya vyavahāraḥ prasādhyate iti śaṅkām śamayitum āha tatra jñānam svatas  siddham kriyā kāya āśritā satī paraiḥ api upalakṣyeta tayā anya jñānam ūhyate aham jānāmi mayā jñātam jñāsyate ca iti evam sva prakāśa ahaṃparāmarśa pariniṣṭhitam eva idam jñānam nāma kim tatra anyat  vicāryate tad aprakāśe hi viśvam andhatamasaṃ syāt  tad api vā na syāt  bālaḥ  api hi prakāśa viśrāntim eva saṃvedayate tad uktam vijñāta āram are kena bojānīyāt  iti tad nihnave hi kaḥ praśnaḥ kim uttaram ca syāt  iti tatra ca jānāmi iti antar saṃrambha yogaḥ  api bhāti yena śukla ādeḥ guṇāt  atyanta jaḍāt  jānāmi iti vapuḥ cit svabhāva tām abhyetiḥ sa ca saṃrambhaḥ  vimarśaḥ kriyāśaktiḥ bhavati yad uktam asmad parameṣṭhi śraḥ sroma ānanda pādaiḥ ghaṭa ādi graha kāle api ghaṭam jānāti sā kriyā iti tena āntarī kriyāśaktiḥ jñānavat eva svatas  siddhā sva prakāśā sā eva tu sva śaktyā prāṇa puryaṣṭaka krameṇa śarīram api saṃcaramāṇā spandana rūpā satī vyāpāra ātmikā mā athā pade api pramāṇasya pratyakṣa ādeḥ viṣayaḥ sā ca para śarīra ādi sāhityena avagatā svam svabhāvam jña ātmakam avagamayati na ca jñānam idantathā bhāti idantā hi ajñāna tvam na ca anyat vastu anyena vapuṣā bhātam bhātam bhavet  tad  jñānam bhāti eva param bhāti ca yad  tad eva aham iti asya vapuḥ iti para jñānam api sva ātmā evaḥ para tvam kevalam upādheḥ deha ādeḥ sa ca api vicāritaḥ  yāvat  na anya iti viśvaḥ pramātṛ vargaḥ paramārtha ta ekaḥ pramātā sa eva ca asti tad uktam prakāśa eva asti sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti tatas ca bhagavān sadāśivaḥ  jānāti iti atas  prabhṛti krimiḥ api jānāti iti antam eka eva pramātā iti phalataḥ sarvajña tvam pramātuḥ evam kartṛ tve api vācyam yad uktam asmad parameṣṭhibhiḥ śiva dṛṣṭau ghaṭaḥ  mad ātmanā vetti vedmi aham ca ghaṭa ātmanā sadāśiva ātmanā vedmi sa vā vetti mad ātmanā nānābhāvaiḥ svam ātmānam jānan  āste svayam śivaḥ ityādi ūhyate iti anena jñānena jñānasya prameya tvam na nirvahati iti darśayati anyathā hi anumīyate iti brūyāt  tad evam yeṣām tārkika pravāda pāṃsu pāta dhūsarībhāvaḥ  na vṛttaḥ  asmin saṃvedana pathe te iyatā eva ātmānam īśvaram vidvāṃsaḥ  ghaṭa śarīra prāṇa sukha tad abhāvān tatra eva nimajjayanta īśvara samāviṣṭā eva bhavanti tatas  ayam upoddhātaḥ upa iti ātmanaḥ samīpe ṭaṅkavat  īśvara pratyabhijñāna lakṣaṇa utkarṣaḥ  hanyate viśrāmyate yena etāvat eva ca asya granthasya tātparyam iti tatas  api ayam upoddhātaḥ upāṃśu avitatam kṛtvā uditi śāstrasya ūrdhva  eva hanyate apasāryate prameya viṣayaḥ  vyāmohaḥ  yena iti gati artha tvāt vā hanteḥ jñānam arthaḥ jñāyate prameyam yena iti kecid tu gatim striyam gacchati iti etad viṣayam eva hanti artham āhuḥ evam śloka catuṣṭaya artha bhāvanā dārḍhy|adeva labhyate parama śivaḥ iti śivam iti śrīmat ācārya utpala deva śiṣya śrīmat ācārya lakṣmaṇa gupta datta upadeśa śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta viracitāyām śrī pratyabhijñā vimarśinyām jñāna adhikāre upoddhātaḥ iti prathama āhnikam atha dvitīyam āhnikam pūrva pakṣa tayā yena viśvam ābhāsya bhedataḥ abheda uttara pakṣa antam nīyate tam stumaḥ śivaḥ iha yad  parama artha rūpam āśaṅkyamāna pratipakṣa pratikṣepeṇa nirūpayiṣyamāṇam suṣṭhutamām spaṣṭokṛtam bhavati yad āha bhaṭṭa nārāyaṇaḥ namaḥ te bhava saṃbhrānta bhrāntim udbhāvya bhindate jñāna ānandam ca nirdvandvam deva vṛtvā vivṛṇvate tatra iha anātmāni īśvara vādinām bhrānti bhedana pūrvakam parama artham vivarīṣyan tad udbhāvanam tāvat  ekādaśabhiḥ ślokaiḥ karoti nanu sva lakṣaṇa ābhāsam ityādibhiḥ tena kartā api kalpitaḥ iti antaiḥ tatra śloka dvayena ātmanaḥ  dhruvasya dṛśya anupalabdhyā abhāva uktaḥ pratyakṣa ātma vādinaḥ prati tatra śloka trayeṇa smṛti anusaṃdhānam saṃskārāt  siddham iti anya bāsiddha tvāt  ātma anumānāya na paryāptam iti proktam anumeya ātma vādinaḥ prati tatra ślokena jñāna ādi guṇaiḥ guṇini pratipattiḥ iti anumānam nirastam evam ātmānam nirākṛtya tatas  jñāna kriyā śakti saṃbandha rūpam aiśvarya nirākartum jñānasya svarūpam eva vyatiriktam vādi antara mate sāṃkhya mate ca ayujyamānam iti nirūpitam śloka dvayena tatas  ekena kriyā nāma na kācid  kvacid api asti iti kathitam tatra sādhakam pratikṣipya bādhakam ca upanyasyati tatas  saṃbandhasya ślokena na astitvam pratipāditam pramāṇa abhāvam vadatā ślokena eva tatra bādhakam pramāṇam uktvā na ātmā sthiraḥ  na api jñātṛtva kartṛtva lakṣaṇam asya aiśvaryam iti sva pakṣa upasaṃhṛtaḥ iti pūrva pakṣasya piṇḍa arthaḥ atha grantha arthaḥ  vyākhyāyate nanu iti ākṣepe iha ātmā saṃvid svabhāvaḥ sthiraḥ iti tāvat ayuktam sthirasya api sva prakāśasya aprakāśanāt  tathā hi ghaṭa prakāśaḥ  ghaṭa vikalpaḥ  ghaṭa pratyabhijñā ghaṭa smṛtiḥ ghaṭa utprekṣā ityādi rūpeṇa jñānāni eva prakāśante bhinna kāntāni bhinna viṣayāṇi bhinna kārāṇi ca tatra nīlasya prakāśaḥ sva lakṣaṇa ābhāsam jñānam svam anyān anuyāyi svarūpa saṃkoca bhāji lakṣaṇam deśa kāla ākāra rūpam yasya ābhāsaḥ prakāśanam antarmukham yasmin bahis mukhīna svarūpa dhāriṇi jñāne tad  avikalpakam viṣaya bhede api eka jātīyam svarūpa vaicitrye api kāraṇa abhāvāt vikalpe hi vaicitrya kāraṇam abhilāpaḥ sa ca ata na asti na hi abhilāpaḥ  nīlasya dharmaḥ na ca cakṣuḥ grāhyaḥ tatas  asau prācyaḥ smartavyaḥ aprabuddhe ca saṃskāre na smṛtiḥ tad prabodhaḥ ca vastu darśana utthitaḥ iti vastu darśana samaye abhilāpa smṛtiḥ na asti tatas  param vikalpakam jñānam sarvasya vikalpasya sākṣāt  pāramparyeṇa vā nirvikalpaka mūla tvāt  param iti ca anya rūpam sāmānya lakṣaṇam tasya viṣayaḥ sva lakṣaṇe ati saṃkocini vitata vikalpa sādhyasya vrḍdhavyāvahārikasya aupadeśikasya vā saṃketasya kartum aśakya tvāt  kṛtasya api vaiyarthyāt  tena hi ananuyāyinā na punar vyavahāraḥ tad ca bahu bhedam yatas tad abhilāpena saṃjalpa ātmanā śabda rūpeṇa saha vartate śabdanam ca idam iti tad  iti tad idam iti bhavet idam iti idam vā idam ityādi bahudhā bhidyate tad ca na viṣaya pakṣaḥ  vartate api tu tasya vikalpasya svarūpam eva vicitraḥ kurvat  pratibhāti iti vikalpaḥ  bahu bhedaḥ evam anubhava vikalpa paramparā tāvat  sva prakāśa tvena bhāti syāt etad  yad lagnā asau paramparā saḥ api ābhāti iti tatra yatas  dvayam api etad  avikalpa itara rūpam na anyasya kasyacid  etad atiriktasya draṣṭuḥ anubhavituḥ saṃbandhi dṛśyasya tu bhavatu bāhya artha vāde atra hetuḥ yatas  tasya draṣṭuḥ ata eva saṃvid svabhāvatā upagamāt sva prakāśa tā yogya tvāt āpanna upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ atraetat bodha dvaya madhye na asti avabhāsaḥ nanu asti eva avabhāsaḥ iti asiddhā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ tathā hi aham vedmi niścinomi smarāmi idam iti vidādi prakṛti artha rūpāt  jñāna smṛti ādeḥ idam iti ca karma rūpāt  viṣayāt  atiriktam eva aham iti anuyāyini prakāśe anuyāyi rūpam bhāti ka evam āha bhāti iti bhānam hi avikalpakam aham iti śabda anuviddhaḥ  vikalpa pratyayaḥ nanu tathā api kim anena vikalpyate śarīra santānaḥ  vā kṛśaḥ aham ityādi pratyayāt jñāna santānaḥ  vā sukhī aham iti pratīteḥ matu arthīyaḥ ca santānam eva spṛśati na atiriktam tad etad uktam ahaṃpratītiḥ api śarīram ādi grahaṇāt  jñānam avasyati saṃtāna rūpa tayā vikalpayati avaśyam sadṛśa aparabhāva bheda grahaṇa sāmarthya vāsanā āviṣṭa tvāt iti eṣā iti na asmābhiḥ nihnutā sa abhilāpam vikalpa ākhyam iti anena saṃgṛhīta tvāt  etad uktam bhavati ahaṃpratītiḥ eva tāvat  na ātmā tasyāḥ  api vikalpa rūpa tvāt  asthaiḥ yāt ca etad pratīti pratyayaḥ api na asti anyaḥ śarīra ādeḥ bhavan  api vā vedya pakṣa patitaḥ syāt  iti tathā api saṃvid saṃvedya vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ  na siddhiḥ iti etad  api śabdena dyotitam evam na asti ātmā saṃvid saṃvedya tri atiriktaḥ  dṛśyasya tasya anupalabdheḥ iti atra ātma vādi anumānam utthāpayati iha smṛti kāle su smūrṣitaḥ  arthaḥ  bhavatu dhvaṃsatām vā iti kintena anubhavaḥ tāvat  dhvastaḥ iti atra sarvasya avivādaḥ tam eva ca anurundhānā smṛtiḥ jāyate tathā hi smṛtau na arthasya prakāśaḥ na adhyavasāyaḥ na api anubhavasya arthasya ca aṅguli dvayavat  na api anubhava viśiṣṭasya arthasya daṇḍivat  sarvatra ayam iti pratyaya prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu anubhava prakāśa eva smṛtau pradhānam anubhavasya tu artha prakāśa ātmaka tvāt  anubhava prakāśana āntarīyakaḥ  artha avabhāsaḥ iti sarvathā yadi anubhavaḥ  dhvastaḥ tadā tad prakāśa rūpā katham smṛtiḥ tad dvāreṇa artha viṣayā syāt  tayā ca sarvaḥ  vyavahāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ iti asau sva rūpeṇa anapahnavanīyā satī anubhavasya nāśe kiṃcid  avinaṣṭam āvedayati tad eva ca anubhava kartṛ  anubhavitṛ rūpam ātmā anubhāvakaḥ  nityaḥ iti iyat eva ca ātma siddheḥ jīvitam tad tu na adhikam iha eva unmīlitam ācāryeṇa vaktavya śeṣa vivakṣayā pūrva pakṣaḥ  mā tāvat  samāpad  iti āśayena katham bhavet  iti arhtaḥ tāvat  tasyām akiṃcitkaraḥ anubhavaḥ ca dhvastaḥ iti na kenacid prakāreṇa smṛtiḥ syāt  tad abhāve ca saṃketa śabda smṛti āyattā api astaṅga tāḥ sarve vikalpāḥ nirvikalpam ca andha badhira mūka prāyam iti hanta nirākrandam avasīdet  viśvam iti iha kārya atirekeṇa tādṛś  kalpanīyam yad  kārya siddhaye paryāpnoti na ca evam ātmā arthaḥ  hi tāvat  smaryate sa ca anubhava prakāśa mukhena anubhavaḥ ca dhvastaḥ iti uktam yadi ātmā kaścid asti kim tena etad api hi vaktavyam ākāśam api asti iti atha ucyate na kevalena ātmanā etad  siddhyati api tu anubhava saṃskāraḥ  api atra upayogī iti tarhi sa eva astu kim anena tad etad darśayati dṛṣṭeṣu anubhūteṣu vastuṣu yā smṛtiḥ tasyām anubhavaḥ  dṛś ātmā dvāram artha āśa sparśe sa ca sati api  ātmani naṣṭaḥ anubhavaḥ tasya hi anāśe idam iti eṣa eva atruṭitaḥ prakāśaḥ iti kā smṛtiḥ tad anubhavitā kim smṛteḥ kuryāt  iti yatra eva viṣaye anubhavaḥ  vṛttaḥ tad eva tasyāḥ smṛteḥ padam smaryamāṇam tad padā iti bahuvrīhiḥ sā iti smṛtiḥ nanu jñāna antarasya viṣayeṇa katham tasyāḥ viṣayitvā abhimānaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha anubhavena hi saṃskāraḥ  janyate sva ucitaḥ saṃskāraḥ ca prātana rūpām sthitim sthāpayati ākṛṣṭa śākhādeḥ cira saṃvartitasya vivartyamānasya bhūrja ādeḥ tena atra api saṃskāraḥ tām smṛtim pūrva anubhava anukāriṇīm karoti iti tad viṣaya eva smṛteḥ viṣayaḥ evam tarhi antargaḍuḥ yathā āyāsāya param tadvat  ātmā sthiraḥ kalpanā āyāsa mātra phalaḥ iti kim tena sarvam hi saṃskāreṇa jagat vyavahāra kuṭumbakam kṛta kara avalambam iti nanu tasma eva saṃskārasya āśrayaḥ  vaktavyaḥ sa hi guṇa tvāt  āśrayam apekṣate ya āśrayaḥ sa ātmā syāt  iti āśaṅkya āha iha saṃskāre jāyamāne yadi ātmanaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sa tarhi avyatiriktaḥ iti na nityaḥ syāt  atha na kaścid  asya viśeṣaḥ tena tarhi kim atha saṃskāra eva asya viśeṣaḥ tarhi na vyatiriktaḥ  asau iti punar api anitye jñāne saṃskāraḥ iti āyātam anubhavāt viśiṣṭam viśiṣṭa smrṭi ākhya kārya kāri jñānam paramparayā jāyate iti iyān eva saṃskāra arthaḥ atha saṃskāra ātmā vyatiriktaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tasya tarhi kim asau saṃbandhaḥ ca vyatiriktaḥ  nirākariṣyate evam jñāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharmā api vikalpanīyāḥ etad āha tatas  iti ātmanaḥ  bhinneṣu dharmeṣu aṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu teṣu satsu api ātmanaḥ svarūpeviśeṣa abhāvāt sa tāvat  ātmā smrṭau na vyāpriyeta asmatṛ rūpa asaṃskṛta rūpa ādi prācya rūp|anapāyāt  iti saṃskārāt eva smṛteḥ siddhiḥ iti aham smarāmi iti yaḥ smartāsaḥ api śarīra saṃtānaḥ  jñāna saṃtānaḥ ca adhyāvasīyate yathā draṣṭā pūrvam hi uktam ahaṃpratītiḥ api eṣā śarīra ādi avasāyinī iti evam ātmani sādhakam pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam ca parākṛtam bādhakam ca sūcitam dharma yoge nityatā ahāni anyathā kim tena tad uktam carma upamaḥ ced saḥ anityaḥ sva tukyaḥ ced asat samaḥ varṣa ātapābhyām kim vyomnaḥ carmaṇi asti hi tad phalam iti ittham ātmānam nirākṛtya tasya aiśvaryam api nirākartum jñānaśaktim eva parīkṣitum āha para abhyupagamena prasaṅga āpādanam etad  pūrva pakṣa vādī karoti prasaṅga viparyaya lābhaḥ  me bhaviṣyati iti tatra ātma vādī nitya tvam ātmana ittham brūte iha kālaḥ  nāma idaṃbhāva viśiṣṭasya viśeṣaṇa tām avalambamānaḥ tam viśiṣṭīkurvan tad saṃkocāt  anityam saṃpādayati ātmanaḥ ca cit svabhāva tvāt  idam iti prathana abhāvena viśeṣya tvam na asti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ  hi yojaka āyattaḥ na ca sva prakāśe yojaka antaram asti sa ittham bruvāṇaḥ paryanuyujyate jñānam api tarhi sva prakāśam iti tatra api eṣā eva vārtā iti tad api kasmāt  na nityam na ca dvayoḥ nityayoḥ kaścid  saṃbandhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  hi asau na anyaḥ tatas  ātmanaḥ  jñānam śaktiḥ iti avasannam adaḥ atha na sva prakāśam jñānam tarhi parasya api adaḥ  na prakāśaḥ sva prakāśa rūpa āveśanam hi asau parasya vidadhat  bodhaḥ prakāśaḥ  bhavati parasya api tatas  sva prakāśa tā śūnyaḥ  na asau arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt  bhāva antaravat jaḍaḥ api asau ittham arthasya prakāśaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti sāṃkhya matam āśaṅkate iha tāvat  artham jānāmi iti asti vyavahāraḥ tatra arthasya prakāśaḥ iti etāvān eva parama arthaḥ tad  na arthasya svam rūpam sarvam prati tathātva prasaṅgāt  na kaṃcid prati vā iti sarvajñam ajñam vā jagat  syāt  na api arthe anyata etad rūpam upanipatitam eṣa eva hi doṣaḥ syāt  tad  nūnam anyatra eva ayam dharmaḥ tattva antare tatra api katham arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt  iti nūnam tatra tattva antare saḥ arthaḥ pratibimba tvena upasaṃkrāmati tad  tattva antaram sattva prādhānyāt  pratibimba graha yogyam tamasā aacchādita tvāt sakala pratibimbanataḥ  vyāvartitam bhāge rajasā tamasaḥ apasāraṇāt kiṃcid eva pratibimba kam gṛhyāti tad eva buddhi tattvam ucyate artha pratibimba grahaḥ ca jñānam asya vṛtti rūpam pūrva vyapadeśa tirodhāyaka dadhi ādi pariṇāma vilakṣaṇa pariṇati viśeṣa ātmakam evam arthasya tāvat  rūpam buddhiḥ dhārayati iyaḥ ca sattva ādīnām sukha duḥkha moha rūpatayām bhogya tvāt  jaḍam iti darpakṣavat  aprakāśam na ca bhogyasya aprakāśasya tad viruddha bhoktṛtā rūpa prakāśa ātmaka svabhāva saṃbhavaḥ  yukti anupātī iti tad vilakṣaṇena bhoktrā bhavitavyam sa ca prakāśaḥ iti etāvat svabhāvaḥ svabhāva antaram hi aprakāśa rūpam bhogyam katham bhoktuḥ svabhāvatayā saṃbhāvyeta sa ca prakāśa mātra svabhāva tvena eva yadi viśvasya prakāśaḥ tarhi yugapad eva prakāśeta ghaṭa prakāśaḥ api paṭa prakāśaḥ syāt  iti viśvam saṃkīryeta sa ca arthāt  artha pratibimbāt  tad ādhārāt ca buddhi tattvāt  anyaḥ katham arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt  asaṃbandhāt  tasmāt  buddhiḥ eva svaccha tvāt  prakāśa pratibimbam api gṛhṇāti tatas  prakāśa pratibimba parigraha mahima upanata prakāśa āveśa buddhi tattva āveśita pratibimbaka nīlā ādi artha paryanta saṃkrānteḥ prakāśa āveśasya arthaḥ prakāśate iti siddhaḥ  vyavahāraḥ tad evam jñānam jaḍa buddhi tattva avyatirekāt  jaḍam api cit pratibimba yogāt  viṣayasya prakāśaḥ iti etad eva tāvat  anucitam yad  prakāśa ātmā pumān buddhau pratibimbam arpayati samāna guṇe bimbaka apekṣayā ca vimale pratibimba saṃkrānti darśanāt  rūpavati ādarśe ghaṭa rūpa pratibimbavat  ātma buddhyoḥ ca ati vailakṣaṇyam ātma apekṣayā ca na buddhiḥ vimalā tad  bahvatu tāvat  etad  iti atha śabdena sūcayati kiṃtu pratibimba vādena api na kiṃcid  pratisamāhitam bhavet  iti darśayati caitanya pratibimba yoge yadi tāvat  tad pratibimbakam api mukhyam prakāśa rūpam eva na bhavati tena api na kiṃcid  kṛtam syāt  na hi pratibimba ta vahni puñja ādarśaḥ  dāhyam dahet  atha mukhya prakāśa rūpam eva tad pratibimbakam tad  tarhi buddheḥ avyatiriktam iti mukhya prakāśa rūpā eva buddhiḥ jātā iti yatas  viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhīrubhiḥ etad  kalpitam sa eva punar  jājvalyamānam nijam ojaḥ  jṛmbhayati tatas ca sā buddhiḥ eva cit mayī syāt  kim puruṣeṇa evam artha pratibimba ka dvāreṇa artha mayī iti api āyātaḥ  vijñāna vādaḥ kuta etasyāḥ tad rūpa tvam iti pūrva kāraṇa paramparātaḥ iti utaram vācyam evam sā eva ced  cit rūpā prāgvat  nitya tā prasaṅgaḥ na ceta cit rūpasya api nitya tā tarhi ātmā na nityaḥ kaścid asti yasya jñānam nāma śaktiḥ syāt  iti jñāna mātram eva asti yaḥ  artha prakāśa rūpaḥ  bodhaḥ  yaḥ ca vikalpa smṛti ādi rūpaḥ tāvatā artha vyavahāra siddheḥ iti prasaṅga viparyaya lābhaḥ jñānam ca cit svarūpam ced  iti ādeḥ śloka dvayasya tātparyam evam jñānam parīkṣya kriyām parīkṣate iha parispanda rūpam tāvat  gavcchati calati patati ityādi yad  pratibhāsa gocaram tatra gṛhaseśa gata deva datta svarūpāt anantaram bāhya deśa varti deva datta svarūpam iti etāvat  upalabhyate na tu tad svarūpa atiriktām kāṃcid  anyām kriyām pratīmaḥ devadattaḥ  dinam tiṣṭhati iti atra tu prabhāta kāla āviṣṭa devadatta svarūpam tatas  prahara kāla āliṅgita tad svarūpam ityādi bhāti dugdham pariṇamate iti atra madhura vastu rūpam amla vastu rūpam drava rūpam kaṭhina rūpam ityādi evam sādṛśyāt ca tatra pratyabhijñā bhinne api kāya keśanasva ādau  iva deśa ākāra anya tve tu kāla anya tvam avaśyaṃbhāvi deśa kāla anya tve api svarūpasya eva deśa tvāt  kāla bhede ca svarūpa bhedāt  deśa kāla ākārā ākāra eva yadi api paryavasmanti tathā api sthūla dṛṣṭyā asti bhedaḥ iti te hi bhedena bauddhaiḥ ucyante iti tātparyam evam pratyakṣeṇa na dṛśyate kacid  kriyā tad bhāvāt na tad pūrvakeṇa anumānena kāryam ca prāma prāpti ādi uttara kṣaṇa rūpam tad deśa vastu rūpa ādi iti kārya anyathā anupapattyā api na sā kalpyā evam pratyakṣa anumānābhyām tasyāḥ  adṛṣṭiḥ iti sādhaka pramāṇa abhāva uktaḥ bādhakam api āha tatra pūrva apara rūpa tā kṣaṇānām vikalpa budvya anusaṃdhānāt na tu sva ātmani kiṃcid  pūrvam aparam vā vastu mātram hi tad  atas  vikalpa prāṇitam pūrva aparībhūta tvam krama rūpa tā kriyāyāḥ kiṃcid  kṣaṇam na vastu spṛśati te hi kṣaṇā na anyonya svarūpa āviṣṭāḥ iti katham ekā kriyā kramaḥ  hi bhedena vyāptaḥ abhiśne tad abhāvāt bhedasya viruddham ekyam iti katham kramikā ekā ca iti syāt  atha ekatra āśraye avasthānāt  ekā tatra api tad kṣaṇa atiriktaḥ  na kaścid  āśrayaḥ anubhūyate kṣaṇā eva hi prabandha vṛttayaḥ bhānti kim ca tathābhūtaiḥ bhinna deśa kāla ākāraiḥ kriyā kṣaṇaiḥ āviṣṭa āśrayaḥ katham ekaḥ syāt  ata eva devadattaḥ ayam sa eva grāmam prāptaḥ iti sādṛśyāt  bhavantī pratyabhijñā na aikyam vāstavam gamayitum alam evam jñānam kriyām ca parīkṣya yasmin sati te saṃbaddhe sarvajñatva sarva kartṛ tā ru upa aiśvarya prasādhanāya prabhavataḥ tam saṃbandham dhvaṃsayitum tad viṣayam pramāṇa abhāvam tāvat āha mṛtppiṇḍe sati stūpakaḥ tatra sati śivikaḥ  yāvat  ghaṭaḥ iti evam bhāva kṣaṇā eva upalabhyante na adhikam kiṃcid  pratyakṣeṇa avabhāsate na api anumānena iti kriyāyām iva vācyam sarvatra ādhāra ādheya bhāva ādau ayam eva panthāḥ pṛthagrūpa kuṇḍavat rakṣaṇa anantaram nirantara ātmaka viśiṣṭa kuṇḍavat ara udayaḥ iti ayam eva ca bhāvaḥ bhāva antareṇa saha niyata pūrva apara tayā vikalpena vyavahiyamāṇaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti abhidhīyate na ca jñāna kriyābhyām saha ātmanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ātmanaḥ tad kāryatva abhāvāt  jñānasya ca svasām agrokārya tvāt kriyāyāḥ ca abhāvāt  iti na jñāna kriyā saṃbandhaḥ  yatas  jñātṛtva kartṛ tve syātām evam pramāṇam parākṛtya saṃbandhe bādhakam sāmānya viśeṣa mukhena nirūpayati saṃbandhaḥ tāvat  paraspara prāpti rūpaḥ  dvayoḥ prāpti bhājoḥ ekaḥ tiṣṭhati iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam tad ca katham na hi ekatra viśramita aśeṣa śarīra sāraḥ anyatra viśramitum alam svarūpa bheda prasaṅgāt  etena saṃyoga samavāyau tad mūlāḥ ca anye api saṃbandhā bādha vidhurām dhuram adhyāropitā mantavyāḥ yaḥ api cetaneṣu tad kalpanayā ca acetaneṣu pāratantrī ātmā saṃbandhaḥ  vyavahiyate tatra siddhasya na pāratantryam asti siddha tvāt eva asiddhasya natarām niḥsvarūpasya tāddharmyā yogāt evam apekṣāyām api vācyam dve ca rūpe katham śliṣyataḥ dvayoḥ ekatva anupapatteḥ ekatve vā kaḥ śleṣaḥ tasmāt  jñāna saṃbandhāt jñātā iti yathā vikalpa kalpitaḥ  arthaḥ  na vastu tathā kriyā saṃbandhāt kartā iti api kalpanā mātram iti pūrva pakṣasya saṃkṣepaḥ iti śivam āditas  iti śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta viracitāyām pratyabhijñā sūtra vimarśinyām jñāna adhikāre pūrvapakṣa vivṛtiḥ nāma dvitīyam āhnikam atha tṛtīyam āhnikam vinā yena na kiṃcid syāt samastā api dṛṣṭayaḥ anastamita saṃbodha svarūpam tam stumaḥ śivam etasmin pūrva pakṣe yad uktam smṛteḥ saṃskāra mātrāt eva siddhiḥ iti tad eva dūṣayitum satyam ityādi jñāna smṛti apohana śaktimān iti antam śloka saptakam kriyāyām saṃbandhe ca dūṣaṇa uddharaṇam dvitīye kriyā adhikāre bhaviṣyati yad tu pareṇa vyatiriktam jñānam kāśāt asāṃkhya ādi dṛṣṭau nirākṛtam tad abhimatam eva grantha kṛta iti tad  dūṣaṇa antaram eva tatra śloka dvayena jñānasya sva saṃvedana rūpa tayā anubhavasya smṛtau aprakāśa tvam darśitam saṃskāra ja tve api tatas  śloka dvayena smṛteḥ bhrānti tvam āśaṅkā pūrvakam parākṛtya tṛtīyena prasaṅgāt  sarva adhyavasāyānām api bhrāntitva āśaṅkā śamitā tatas  sati api saṃskāre smṛti anupapattau vyavahāra ucchedaḥ iti ślokena uktvā sva pakṣe tad upapattiḥ iti ślokena uktam iti tātparyam grantha arthaḥ tu nirūpyate pūrva pakṣa madhyāt  mayā tāvat  bahu aṅgīkartavyam iti satyam iti anena darśitam yad tu na aṅgīkartavyam tad  dūṣyate iti etad uktam kiṃtu iti anena viśeṣa abhidhāyinā iha smṛtau viṣaya mātrasya prakāśaḥ  na samarthanīyaḥ  vartate yaḥ saṃskārāt eva siddhyet  kiṃtu anubhava prakāśena vinā tad  iti evaṃrūpā katham smṛtiḥ syāt  katham ca tayā vinā abhilāṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ syāt  anubhavena hi asya sukha sādhana tā niścitā tatas  upādānam tatra pūrva anubhava janitāt saṃskārāt  etāvat  jātam yadi api tad jñānam viṣayeṇa na janitam tathā api tad viṣayam iti na ca etāvatā kiṃcid  ātma niṣṭhe sva prakāśa jñāne viṣayasya iva anubhavasya prācyasya aprakāśāt  nanu saṃsk|a raja tvāt eva prācyam anubhavam api viṣayīkurutām smṛtiḥ iti āśaṅkya āha dṛś  jñānam tad ca jaḍāt  vibhidyate sva prakāśa eka rūpa tayā jaḍaḥ  hi prakāśāt  pṛthak bhūtaḥ  vaktavyaḥ tena dṛś  su ābhāsā ābhāsaḥ prakāśamānatā sā svam rūpam avyavhicāri yasyāḥ svasya ca ābhāsanam rūpam yasyāḥ sati api bāhye tad śarīra saṃkrāntam na prakāśanam jñānasya rūpam bhavitum arhati para prakāśana ātmaka nija rūpa prakāśanam eva hi sva prakāśa tvam jñānasya bhaṇyate nanu svābhāsam eva sat  tad  anubhava jñānam smaraṇe bhāsiṣyate na iti āha na anyena vedyā paratra yadi dṛś  bhāseta tarhi na sā su ābhāsā idam eva hi sva prakāśasya lakṣaṇam svayam hi yadi prakāśeta tadā pareṇa saha asaṃbandhāt  saṃbandha prāṇā katham paratra iti saptamī saṃgacchatām tathā ca rūpa jñānena rase dṛś rasa viṣayam jñānam na vedyate evam hi cakṣuṣā eva rasaḥ phalataḥ gṛhīta eva syāt  nanu yadi na ābhāti smaraṇe anubhavaḥ kim tarhi saṃskāreṇa kṛtam syāt  rūpa jñānam na rasa jñāna jāt  saṃskārāt  jātam tad  katham ayam prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  saṃskāra eva bhavat saṃbhāvita doṣa bhaṅgāya prabhavet  na etad  yatas  hi asau tad saṃskāra saṃskṛtāt  samanantara pratyayāt  utthitaḥ smṛti bodhaḥ tena tad sadṛśaḥ  bhavatu śāsvāsaṃniveśa iva pūrva saṃniveśa tulyaḥ na tu yaḥ  yad saṃskārāt  jātaḥ sa tasya vedana svabhāvaḥ  bhavati iti yuktam sadṛśa tvasya api gatiḥ avagamaḥ katham na hi anubhava jñānam sādṛśyam gamayati na api smṛti jñānam parasparam asaṃvedane dvaya niṣṭha sādṛśya adhyavasāya ayogāt abhyasya ca tad ubhaya vedana rūpasya abhāvāt  iti saṃskārāt  param sa viṣaya tā mātram smṛteḥ siddham na tu anubhava viṣaya tvam na api asya viṣayasya pūrva anubhava viṣayīkṛta tvam iti niścayaḥ eṣaḥ nanu yadi smṛti jñāne anubhavasya satyataḥ prakāśaḥ syāt  tad mukhena ca tad viṣayasya tadā bhavet  bhavat ukteḥ avakāśaḥ yāvatā smṛtiḥ vikalpa rūpa tvāt  kevalam aparakāśa mānam eva anubhavam tad viṣayam ca adhyavasyati tad  iyam bhrānti svabhāvā tatra kaḥ ayam nirbandhaḥ tad etad darśayati śaṅkyamāna tvena na tad darśanam na api tad viṣayaḥ smṛteḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api tu ubhayam adhyavasīyate bhrama rūpa tayā smṛteḥ etad  nirākaroti atra kārikayā upapattim āha anubhūtasya anubhava prakāśitasya viṣayasya apramoṣaḥ anapahāraḥ tathā eva prakāśanam yad  etad  smṛteḥ ātmīyam rūpam tad  tathā aprakāśana abhāve vighaṭa itamām kim ca bhrāntau asat vā ātma ākāraḥ  vā prakhyāti na tu tayā arthaḥ svīkriyate tasya aprakāśanāt  iti tayā arthaḥ  na vyavasthāpita eva prakāśana ātmā hi vyavasthāpanā tatas ca smaraṇāt abhilāṣeṇa katham artha viṣayaḥ  vyavahāraḥ na ca tad aprakāśane saṃskāra ja tvena kiṃcid  kṛtyam tad hi sādṛśyam labdhum avalambyate na ca anubhavena viṣaya prakāśana ātmanā smṛti abhidhānāyā bhrānteḥ kicid api sādṛśyam asti sarvathā viṣayam aspṛśantyā nanu yaḥ anubhavaḥ  yaḥ ca tad viṣayaḥ sa yatas  tayā adhyavasīyate tatas  aṃśāt  sādṛśyam anubhavena smṛteḥ tad siddhaye ca saṃskāra parigrahaḥ adhyavasīyate iti kim ucyate prakāśyate iti ced  na bhrānti tvam na prakāśyate iti ced  punar api viṣayaḥ  na spṛṣṭa eva anayā iti sādṛśyam iti śabda gaḍu mātram tad etad darśayitum āha iha smṛteḥ anyasya vā bhrānti bodhasya sva saṃvedana aṃśe prakāśamāne na bhrānti tā tatra vaiparītya abhāvāt yaḥ tu tatra adhyavasīyate su ākāraḥ sa viparīta tayā asvākāra tvena artha tayā iti tatra aṃśe bhrānti tā sa ca aṃśaḥ artha lakṣaṇaḥ  na smṛtyā anyayā vā bhrāntyā spṛśyate iti tatra asau tūṣṇīkā iti balāt eva tatra aṃśe jaḍa tvam asyāḥ  āyātam ghaṭa jñānasya iva paṭe na ca jaḍena viṣayasya kiṃcid  kṛtyam tatas ca artha viṣayaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  vilupyeta atha tu tam avasāya rūpam sva saṃvedana aṃśam su ākāram vā avalambya ajaḍa tvam asyāḥ evam api ajāḍye nijam sva saṃvedanam ullekhaḥ ca su ākāraḥ itīyati eṣā pariniṣṭhitā smṛtiḥ iti viṣayasya nāma api prahītum aśaknuvataḥ tatas  smṛti adhyavasāyāt  katham viṣayasya vyavasthāpanam vyavahāryatva saṃpādana sāmarthyam saṃskāre sati api smṛtiḥ na kathaṃcana ghaṭate tatas ca paraspara saṅgati hīnāni sakalāni jñānāni iti yad uktam śloka pañcakena tad  idānīm prakṛte yojayati janasya lokasya yā kācana sthitiḥ vyavahāraḥ sā sarva jñānānām yad  anusaṃdhānam eka viṣaya bhāva upapanna smṛti tā prāpti rūpam tatra āyattā tathā hi smaraṇa nibandhanāḥ sarve vyavahārāḥ prathamam api hi pratyakṣa jñānam aham iti pūrva apara rūpa anusaṃdhānena smaraṇa anuprāṇitena vinā na ghaṭate pramātari viśrānti abhāvāt  apratyakṣatva prasaṅgāt  evam sukha ādau mantavyam hāna ādāna preraṇa abhyupagamāda vastu vyavahārāḥ smaraṇa mayā eva evam jñānānām yad  anusaṃdhānam tatas  jāyamānā jana sthitiḥ evam iti para abhyupagame sati naśyet  naśyati iti saṃbhāvyate kuta iti ced  viśeṣaṇa dvāreṇa hetum āha anyonyam tāvat  bhinnāni jñānāni anyat  anubhava jñānam anyat  idānīntanam jñānam vikalpa abhimatam anyat  smaraṇa saṃmatam jñānam tad etāni sva viṣaya prakāśa mātra rūpāṇi para viṣaye jaḍa andhāneḍamūka kalpāni na ca anyonyasya prakāśa rūpāṇi evam na svarūpataḥ  na vedyayaḥ  vā ekībhāva rūpam anusaṃdhānam asti anyonyam ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ  na asti na ca turyam jñāteya nibandhanam anusandhān ādhāyi saṃbhāvyate iti dhvaṃseran vyavahārāḥ na ca dhvaṃsantām iti bhavat abhīṣṭa śāpa mātrāt te dhvaṃsante prakāśante yatas  tatas  etad  āpadyate etad eva samarthayitum udyantavyam iti tad ca asmad abhimata prakāreṇa vinā vidheḥ api aśakya samarthanam iti darśayati saṃvid  tāvat  prakāśate iti tāvat  na kecid  apahnuvate sā tu saṃvid  yadi sva ātma mātra viśrāntā arthasya sā katham prakāśaḥ sa hi artha dharma eva tathā syāt  tatas ca artha prakāśaḥ tāvatī eva paryavasita iti galitaḥ  grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ atas  artha prakāśa rūpam saṃvidam icchatā balāt eva arthaḥ api tad rūpa antargata eva aṅgīkratavyaḥ sa ca artha prakāśaḥ  yadi anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca tad  na smaraṇam upapannam ityata eka eva asau iti eka tvāt  sarvaḥ  vedya rāśiḥ tena kroḍīkṛtaḥ iti etad api anicchatā aṅgīkāryam evam api satatam eva unmagnena nimagnena vā viśva ātmanā prakāśeta tathā svabhāva tvāt  na ca evam atas  svarūpa antar bruḍitam artha rāśim aparam api bhinna ākāram ātmani parigṛhya kaṃcid eva artham svarūpāt  unmagnam ābhāsayati iti āpatitam sā eṣā jñānaśaktiḥ unmagna ābhāsa bhinnam ca cit svarūpam vahirmukha tvāt  tad chāyā anurāgāt navam navam jñānam uktam evam api nava nava ābhāsāḥ pratikṣaṇam udaya vyaya bhāja iti sā eva vyavahāra nivaha hāniḥ tena kvacid  ābhāse gṛhīta pūrve yad  saṃvedanam bahirmukham abhūt  tasya yad  antarmukham cit svarūpa tvam tad  kāla antare api avasthā snu sva ātma gatam tad viṣaya viśeṣe bahirmukha tvam parāmṛśati iti eśā smṛti śaktiḥ yad ca tad  navam bhāsayati smarati vā tad  vastutas  saṃvidā viśva mayyā tādātmya vṛtti iti viśva mayam pūrṇam eva iti navam na kiṃcid  ābhāsitam smṛtam vā syāt  idam api pravāha patitam urīkāryam yad  kila tad  ābhāsyate tad  saṃvidaḥ  vicchiidyate saṃvid ca tatas  saṃvid ca saṃvid antarāt  saṃvedyam ca saṃvedya antaraāt  na ca vicchedanam vastutas  saṃbhavati iti vicchedanasya avabhāsa mātram ucyate na ca tad  iyatā pāramārthikam nirmīyamāṇasya sarvasya ayam eva parama arthaḥ yatas  eṣa eva paritas chedanāt  pariccheda ucyate tad avabhāsana sāmarthyam apohana śaktiḥ anena śakti trayeṇa viśve vyavahārāḥ tad ca bhagavata eva śakti trayam yad  tathābhūta anubhavitṛ smartṛ vikalpayitṛ svabhāva caitra maitra ādi avabhāsanam sa eva hi tena tena vapuṣā jānāti smarati vikalpayati ca yathā uktam ācāryeṇa eva yadi api artha sthitiḥ prāṇa puryaṣṭaka niyantrite jīve niruddhā tatra api parama ātmani sā sthitā ityādi etāsām ca jñāna ādi śaktīnām asaṃkhya prakāraḥ  vaicitrya vikalpa iti tad sāmarthyam svātantryam apara adhīnam pūrṇam mahat aiśvaryam tad nirmita brahma viṣṇu rudra ādi aiśvarya apekṣayā ucyate tad evam cit vapuḥ iti ekam kṛtvā iyat āyātam viśva rūpaḥ iti tatas  eva ca pariniṣṭhita eka rūpa jaḍa bhāva vailakṣaṇyāt  jñāna ādi śakti yukta tā māha īśvaryam upasaṃprāptaḥ etad anupagame na kiṃcid  idam bhāseta iti prasaṅgaḥ bhāsate tu tasmāt  etad  avaśya aṅgīkartavyam iti prasaṅga viparyayaḥ naśyet jana sthitiḥ yadi evam na syāt  iti prāktanena ślokena saha saṃbandhaḥ ced  iti anena tad viparyayaḥ sūcitaḥ iti śivam āditas  iti śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta viracitāyām īśvara pratyabhijñā sūtra vimarśinyām jñāna adhikāre para darśana anupapattiḥ nāma tṛtīyam āhnikam atha caturtham āhnikam padārtha ratna nikaram nija hṛd gañja puñjitam grathnantam smṛti sūtra antaḥ saṃtatyā eva stumaḥ śivam evam jñāna pūrvikā smṛtiḥ tad ubhaya anugrāhiṇī apohana śaktiḥ iti tāvat  vastu saṃbhava krameṇa pradarśitam upakrama anusāreṇa smṛtiḥ eva sūcita prasaṅga viparyaya samarthana dṛśā vivecyā satyam kiṃtu smṛti jñānam iti hi upakrāntam tatra saṃskāra mātrāt tāvat  mā nāma udapādi smṛtiḥ idam tu vaktavyam tathābhūta bhavat abhyupagata bhagavat prabhāvaḥ api katham enām kuryāt  iti śaṅkām śamayitum smṛti tattva nirūpaṇāya sa hi pūrva anubhūta artha upalabdhā ityādi arthau bhātaḥ pramātari iti antam śloka aṣṭakam tatra ślokena sva pakṣe smṛtiḥ upapannā iti kathitam dvitīyena smṛteḥ pūrva anubhava viṣayīkṛta sva lakṣaṇa prakāśana sāmarthyam uktam tṛtīyena anubhavena tad viṣayeṇa ca ekībhāva paryanta āveśaḥ smaraṇasya uktaḥ turyeṇa anubhavasya na viṣaya tayā smṛtyā prakāśanam iti nirūpitam pañcamena yogi jñānam api anubhavam pṛthak bhāvena na viṣayīkaroti iti baḍatā turya śloka artha eva upodvalitaḥ ṣaṣṭhena āśaṅkyamānam anubhavasya smṛtyā pṛthak viṣayīkaraṇam kākpanikam iti avāstavīkṛtam saptamena smṛti prasaṅgāt  vikalpe api pūrva anubhavena aikya ātmā āveśaḥ  darśitaḥ aṣṭamena smartavyasya smṛteḥ smartuḥ ca ekacit tattva viśrāntiḥ uktā prasaṅgāt ca dṛśyasya darśanasya draṣṭuḥ ca iti tātparya arthaḥ atha krameṇa śloka artha ucyate pūrvam anubhūtasya arthasya ya upalandhā antarmukhaḥ  bodhaḥ sa tāvat  adya api paratas  smṛti kāle api asti eva saṃvid mātra svarūpasya kāla kṛta saṃkoca rūpa viśeṣa ātmaka avaccheda ayogāt  anubhavasya ca antar  arthaḥ api apṛthagbhāvena avasthitaḥ iti etad api ayatna siddham iyat  tu cintyam akāla kalite saṃvedane tad antar vartini ca viśvatra bhāva jāte yadi tāvat  cit mayatā parāmarśaḥ tad  aham iti etāvatā eva pūrṇena vimarśena bhāvyam atha idamtayā pṛthak bhāva avabhāsanena tathā api tatra dvayī gatiḥ aham iti aṃśe yadi viśrānyati idantā tadā aham idamiti sadāśiva ādi daśayā bhāvyam atha na rohati tad  idam iti eva ābhāsanena bhavitavyam apūrva tā ābhāsanāt ca tad  anubhavanam eva syāt  na smaraṇam iti āśaṅgya āha svairī iti svam ātmīyam upakaraṇam īrayati sva kartavyeṣu avaśyam tad śīlaḥ ca svam ca ātmānam īrayati na punar  sva kartavye prerakam apekṣate iti svairī svatantraḥ tena svatantra tvāt sa iti vimṛśati sa iti vimarśanasya ca iyat rūpam yad  sarvathā akāla kalita svarūpa parāmarśanam eva na na api atyantam bhedena vimarśanam eva api tu yaḥ  bhāvaḥ pūrvam anubhava kāle tad deśa kāla pramātṛ antara sācivyena pṛthak kṛtaḥ  na ca ahantāyām eva līnīkṛtaḥ sa tādṛś eva tamasā iva ācchādya avasthāpitaḥ saṃskāra śabda vācyaḥ tasya tam ācchādakam apahastayati tatra apahastite sa pūrvavat  pṛthakkṛte eva avabhāti nanu ca idantayā avabhāset  pūrvavat eva na evam tadānīntana avabhāsana pṛthak kṛta śarīra ādi saṃbandham anavadhūya eva hi tad prakāśaḥ tatas ca idānīntana avabhāsana smaraṇa kāla parāmarśaḥ api na nimīlati iti tad parāmarśa bhitti prādhānyena pūrva kāla parāmarśaḥ iti viruddha pūrva apara parāmarśa svabhāva eva sa iti parāmarśa ucyate evam ca sa eva parameśvaraḥ smarati etad eva hi tasya smartṛ tvam yad  evaṃprakāra parāmarśa ucita kāla kalā ādi sparśa sahiṣṇu māyā pramātṛ bhāva parigrahaḥ iti māyā avidyā dvaya advaya mayam tatas  eva sakala siddhi vitaraṇa catura cintāmaṇi prakhyam āgamikāḥ smaraṇam eva mantra ādi prāṇitam manyante tathā ca dhyāna ādi bhāvam smṛtiḥ eva labdhvā cintāmaṇiḥ tvad vibhavam vyanakti iti alam tāvat  anena tṛd nanta samāsena yatnataḥ  anubhavasya artha mukhena kāla sparśam artha viśrānta tām dvayoḥ api pramātari nirūḍhim bheda abhedābhyām darśayati vṛttaḥ  eka arthībhāvāt tasya ca bheda abheda maya tvam iti vakṣyāmaḥ etad eva smṛti tattvam upapādayitum śloka antarāṇi tatra yadi kaścid  brūyāt  iha smṛtiḥ vikalpaḥ na ca anena arthaḥ prakāśyate artha asaṃsparśinaḥ  hi vikalpāḥ anubhavena ca yena saḥ arthaḥ prakāśatām nītaḥ sa idānīm kīrti mātra mūrtiḥ jātaḥ na ca saḥ api smṛtyā prakāśyate jñānasya jñāna antareṇa asaṃvedya tvāt asattvāt ca iti arthasya prakāśana abhāvāt idam smarāmi iti jñānam bhrānti mātram eva iti punar api āpatitam iti tadā tam prati ucyate iha smṛti vikalpe tāvat  arthaḥ  avasīyate anyathā supta mūrcchita kalpa tā āpatteḥ evam ca yāvat  adhyavasāyaḥ arthasya tāvat  arthāt  iti sāmarthyāt  iyat  abhyupagantavyam yad  saḥ arthaḥ prakāśate aprakāśamāne adhyavasātavye adhyavasāyaḥ andha prāyaḥ syāt  prakāśanam ca na tad ānīntana kālasya tyāgena na api dvīkāreṇa idam iti eva avabhāsana prasaṅgāt  tasmāt  atīta anubhava kālaḥ pūrva anubhūta bhāva sva alakṣaṇyākṣepaka tvena apekṣaṇīyaḥ  vedya bhāge prakāśa ātmaka avabhāsā abhiniveśitayā smartṛ deha prāṇa ādi avabhāsa kālaḥ ca avalambanīyaḥ  vedaka bhāge vimarśa aṃśa abhiniveśi tvena ābhāsa mātram hi bhāvasya svarūpam pratyābhāsam pramāṇasya vyāpārāt  tad eva ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇayā dipa sahasra prabhā saṃmūrcchanavat sphuṭībhavati ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇa abhāve api tu kāla ābhāsa saṃbhedena eva svālakṣaṇyam tasya ābhāsasya karoti kāla śakteḥ eva bhedaka tvāt  iti vakṣyate evam tāvat  sva lakṣaṇībhāvaḥ prāktana deha ābhāsa sācivyā abhyudita kāla ābhāsayā ghaṭa ābhāsasya iti tāvatī eva vā smṛtiḥ ābhāsa antaraiḥ api vyāmiśrāḥ  ati sphuṭa iti atyanta sphuṭībhāve api tadā anīntana kāla tā na truṭyati anya sādhāraṇya anavabhāvāt tathā avabhāse tu yoginaḥ tad nirmāṇam eva brahma bhāṣita ādau tu navam eva avabhāsanam iti atra tu āgama ādi māna antara anubhūta brahma ādi svarūpa smaraṇa paramparā abhyupāyaḥ bhāsayet  iti vidhi rūpeṇa niyogena niyamaḥ  lakṣyate na bhāsayati iti etad  na api tu bhāsayati eva iti sva kāle iti smaraṇa kāle āmṛśan iti vedaka bhāga niveśī vartamāna kāla uktaḥ pūrva ābhāsitam sva lakṣaṇam iti vedya aṃśa sparśī bhūtakālaḥ  ghaṭa ābhāsasya api kevalasya svālakṣaṇya āpatti hetuḥ darśitaḥ iyat eva smṛteḥ avyavhicāri vapuḥ arthita atiśayāt  tu sphuṭa tvam iti atha śabdaḥ  dyotayati tad eva āha asvila ātmanā iti sarva ābhāsa miśreṇa vapuṣā iti arthaḥ nanu evam sva lakṣaṇasya prakāśane bhedena bahis tad avabhāseta etad eva hi bahis avabhāsanam yad  sva lakṣaṇa prakāśanam iti śaṅkā śamanāya nirūpayati smaraṇa jñānāt  bhinna tvena bahīrūpatayā yadi saḥ  arthaḥ  bhāseta smaryamāṇasya ca yad  bhāsanam tad eva na syāt  smaryamāṇam eva tad  na syāt  anubhūyamānam eva tad  bhavet  iti yāvat  nanu ca evam katham sva lakṣaṇasya prakāśanam uktam etad  na idāṇīm prakāśanam api tu pūrva kāle eva tadā ca asau bahis avabhāsata eva nanu ca idānīm tarhi kim vimarśanam iti brūmaḥ nanu prakāśana vimarśanayoḥ bhinna kāla tvam āpatitam tatas  kim ubhayam api na kiṃcid  syāt  anyonya jīvita tvāt  asya mā evam yasya hi saṃvedanāni eva bhinnāni tattvam tasya idam apratisamādheyam eva asmad darśane tu bhinna kālā api saṃvidaḥ tad kāla atyāgena eva ekatā avabhāsanena svatantraḥ pramātā yāvat antar mukha tayā tāvatī aṃśe vimṛśati tāvat  prakāśasya tātkālika bahirbhāva ābhāsaḥ  vimarśasya idānīntana antarmukhā sthitiḥ iti etad eva vedanā adhikam veditṛ tvam vedaneṣu saṃyojana viyojanayoḥ yathāruci karaṇam svātantryam kartṛ tvam ca etad eva ucyate ghaṭam aham anvabhūvam iti vā sa ghaṭaḥ iti vā aikyam anusaṃdhānam anusaṃdha ātura bhinnam iti darśayitum yad eva aikyam sa eva veditā iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena darśitam eṣa sa iti ācchāditasya iva pramātṛ tattvasya sphuṭa avabhāsanam kṛtam idam iti vismaya garbhayā anayā uktyā pratyabhijñā eva sūcitā yad āha granthakāra eva ittham sva saṃvittim apahnuvānaiḥ yad tad vadadbhiḥ kaluṣīkṛtam yad  pramātṛ tattvam sphuṭa yuktibhiḥ tān mūkān vidhāya prakaṭīkṛtam tad  iti nanu ca prācya eva anubhavaḥ  yadi smaryamāṇasya bahi s avabhāsana rūpaḥ prakāśaḥ tarhi iyat  ucyatām saḥ anubhava idānīm smaraṇena viṣayīkriyate iti aikyena tu alaukikena kaḥ arthaḥ iti vyāmoham vihantum āha pūrvaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ arthaḥ pṛthak  iti idantayā bhāti sma na evam smaraṇa kāle smṛti jñānāt  pṛthaktvena idam pūrvam anubhavanam iti bhāti yathā ca smṛti kāle tasmāt  smṛti jñānāt  saḥ arthaḥ prāk  iti pūrva svabhāvaḥ  na bhedena ābhāti smṛti kāle bahis avabhāsa abhāvāt evam tatas  eva hetoḥ pūrvaḥ api anubhavaḥ  na bhedena ābhāti katham tarhi ubhayam bhāti anvabhūvam iti evam etad  kim ucyate iti ced  aham iti evaṃsvabhāvaḥ  ya ātmā pūrva apara saṃvid antarmukha svabhāvaḥ tatra yad  ārohaṇam viśramaḥ tena hetunā pūrva saṃvid rūpa tāyāḥ sva prakāśāyāḥ  bhāsanāt  tad lonasya api ghaṭasya sva prakāśa deśīya tvena bhāsanam ātmani ca ārohaṇam viśramaṇā anubhavasya arthasya ca prakṛti pratyayau pratyaya artham saha brūtaḥ iti nyāyāt  saṃkhyā ākṣipte tadvati vā kartṛ bhūte asmad arthe anubhavaḥ  bruḍitaḥ tad dvāreṇa arthaḥ api ca na tu svātantryeṇa eva asau tad artham eva karma na nirdiṣṭam ghaṭa ādiḥ punar  anubhava kāle na asmad artham ārohati hi yasmāt  na eva bhāti pūrvaḥ anubhavaḥ pṛthak  apara ardha uktāt  hetoḥ tasmāt  saṃvidām aikyam iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ luṅā bhūtakālasya dyotita tvāt  prāk  iti bhinnakramaḥ uttama puruṣeṇa asmad arthasya aham iti api ārohaṇam iti ruhiḥ iti aṇijantaḥ ṇijanta upi nanu ka evam āha anubhavaḥ pṛthak  na bhāti iti ghaṭavat  na bhāti iti ced  kim tatas  ghaṭaḥ api hi na anubhava sakhyaḥ bhāti iti kim na bhāti svabhāvena bhāti iti tu ubhayatra api samānam tathā hi atīta anāgata sūkṣma ādi yathā yogi jñāne viṣayībhavati iti abhyupagatam tathā para cittam api pratyayasya para citta jñānam iti ādau tatra jñāna vṛtti pariṇatam eva sattvam citta śabdena uktam anyathā pratyayasya saṃyama viṣayī kārya tvam katham ucyeta ālambana yogaḥ ca katham śaṅkayeta na ca sa ālambanam iti tasmāt  parakīyam anubhavanam iva nijam api viṣayīkriyatām iti āśaṅkya dṛṣṭānta eva asiddhaḥ iti bhānti iti antena abhyupagamena vā siddha tve api prakṛte arthe viṣamaḥ iti śeṣeṇa darśayati yoginām yad  etad  darśana antaram bhāvanā ādi udbhavaḥ para citta viṣayaḥ  jñāna viśeṣaḥ tatra dṛśaḥ iti upalabdhayaḥ  na bhānti tathā hi saugatānām tāvat  sva prakāśa eka rūpam jñānam tad  ced  jñāna antareṇa vedyam tarhi yad  asya nijam vapuḥ ananya vedya tayā prakāśanam nāma na tad prakāśitam syāt  sāṃkhyānām api puruṣa  chāyā eva upalabdhiḥ puruṣaḥ ca asaṃvedya parvā iti katham vedyā syāt  vaiśeṣikāṇām api ātmani abhedena samavāyi saṃvedanam para gatam manasā katham gṛhyeta antar śarīra vṛttinā tad śarīra antaranupraveśe tu tasya eva aham iti śarīrīkaraṇāt  ahanta avabhāsita tvāt ātmanaḥ  bhedaḥ  vigalet  nitya anumeya tvam tu na ātmana upapadyate jñānasya ca jñāna antara vedya tve anavasthāna ādi uktam tasmāt  yoginaḥ para citta vedanā avasare iyān prakāśaḥ etad deha prakāśa sahacārī ghaṭa sukha ādi prakāśaḥ iti tatra ghaṭa sukha ādi idantayā bhāti tad gataḥ tu prakāśaḥ  aham iti eva sva prakāśa tayā prakāśate pramātrīkṛta para deha prāṇa ādi samavabhāsa saṃskārāt  tu tad niṣṭhām idantām eva prakāśa bhāge api manyamāna idam para jñānam iti abhimanyate avigalita sva para vibhāgaḥ  yogī prāpta prakarṣaḥ tu sarvam ātma tvena paśyan sva sṛṣṭam eva sva para vibhāgam manyate iti jñānasya na yogi jñānena prakāśyatā bhavatu vā tathā api prakṛtam na etad samam tathā hi ayam anubhavati iti para niṣṭha eva asau anubhave yoginaḥ prakāśaḥ na tu aham anubhavāmi iti ātma āroheṇa vartamānaḥ iha tu anvabhūvam iti aham aṃśa viśrāntiḥ anālīḍhet aṃbhāva eva anubhavasya iti yuktam uktam yasmāt  anubhavaḥ pṛthak  na bhāti tasmāt  aikyam bhinna kālānām saṃvidām veditā iti yadi ahaṃa bhāva viśrānti vaśāt anubhavaḥ smṛtau pṛthak  na bhāti iti ucyate tadā parāmarśa antaram sākṣāt eva idantayā anubhavam parāmṛśat  yadi vā idaṃbhāva ucita ghaṭa ādi viśrānta tām anubhavasya prathayat  upalabdham iti tad anusāreṇa api kim na vyavahriyate iti para abhiprāyam pratikṣipati lokasya tāvat  evam na saṃvedanam sa hi na pṛthak bhūtām dṛśam kāṃcid  manyate sā dṛś  me āsīt  iti evam evam api tu yad  smaryate evaṃbhūtam api yad  smaraṇam kasyacid  vivecakaṃmanyasya tad  smṛteḥ vyākaraṇam padasya iva prakṛti pratyaya artha nirūpaṃam kālpanikam vibhajya ākaraṇam paratra pratipādana mātram saḥ  api yadi mūlaprati iti vedayate pūrva ukta krameṇa tadā anubhavam pṛthak bhūtam na veda yata eva tad  rāhoḥ śiraḥ itivat  kalpitam bhedam manyate anyathā sa ghaṭaḥ itivat  sā dṛkiti atra api prāktanam dṛś antaram apekṣaṇīyam syāt  tad  iti anena hi ghaṭasya vā dṛśaḥ  vā pūrva anubhava viṣaya āpattiḥ ucyate anyathā dṛś  iti eva syāt  tatas ca dṛś  mayā dṛś antareṇa anubhūtā iti āpatet  tatra api tathā tve anavasthā nanu smṛteḥ maulikam kim rūpam ucyate mayā dṛṣṭam iti nanu atra dayitā vadana nalina ādi viśrāntam darśanam uktam na tu ātma ārūḍham karmaṇi niṣṭhā utpatteḥ sa eṣa sva vācam eva na cetayati kartuḥ kriyayā hi āpyam karma iti dṛśi kriyāyāḥ kartṛ niṣṭhatā eva tathā ca kartṛ sthām eva dṛśikriyām āhuḥ darśayate bhṛtyān rājā iti ādau jaiminīyaiḥ api jñāna rūpā dṛśiḥ bhāvanā ātmikā pramātṛ viśrāntā eva uktā kevalam prakaṭa tā viṣaya dharmaḥ  dṛṣṭa tā ākhyā anyā saṃvid  vā asvatantrā iti anyat  etad  pramātṛ viśrānta tvam eva kathayitum mayā iti uktam tena anvabhūvam aham mayā anubhūtam iti śabda vaicitrya mātram idam na tu artha bhedaḥ anye tu bhinnakrama tvena yojayanti dṛś  āsīt  sā me iti evam mayā dṛṣṭam iti ca yad  smaraṇam tad  vyākaraṇam asyāḥ iti anantara ukta anvabhūvam iti ucita parāmarśāyāḥ smṛteḥ iti apiḥ ca arthe nanu dṛṣṭam api nirvikalpakena yāvat  na parāmṛṣṭam vimarśa viśeṣa viśrāntyā tāvat  na smaryate mārga dṛṣṭam iva tṛṇa parṇa ādi viśeṣeṇa rūpeṇa tad idam eva vicāraṇīyam samanantara bhāvi vikalpa kāle tad darśanam idantayā avabhāta pūrvam vā na vā iti tad etad āśaṅkya āha iha darśanam yādṛśam nijena vapuṣā tādṛśena eva tena bhātavyam sarvadā tad ca sva kāle ananya prakāśam aham iti etāvatā sva rūpeṇa ucita prakāśam tad vikalpa aṃśa vicāraḥ tāvat  na kutracid  aṅgam bhavatu vā aṅgam kim tu avasāyaḥ  api evaṃbhūtaḥ iti api śabdena sūcayati tatra samanantara bhāvinā vikalpena vastu parāmṛśyamānam anubhava parāmarśa mukhena vā parāmṛśyate aham imam paśyāmi iti vartamāna tayā imam iti anena ca pratyakṣa vyāpāra tvam pratyakṣāyamāṇa tvena darśitam evam eva vā parāmṛśyate ghaṭaḥ ayam iti atra ayaṃśabdena pratyakṣāyamāṇa tvam uktam tatra antye vikalpe darśanasya pṛthak  parāmarśa eva na asti iti kā tatra idanta āśaṅkā tatas ca pāriśeṣyāt  ahantayā tasya atra asti parāmarśaḥ tad abhāve vikalpasya nimīlita akṣe api bhāvāt  svayam artha sparśe sati sphuṭam aviṣaya paryavasitaḥ kathamadhyavasāyaḥ  bhavet  ādye tu darśanam parāmṛṣṭam api asmad arthe antarbhūtam ahaṃbhāva āspadam avasātari viśrāntam sva prakāśam eva parāmṛṣṭam iti vikalpaḥ api na bodha antara bodhyatām bodhayati bodhasya avasāyaḥ avasā samavetam iti apṛthagbhāvam āha avasātari iti svatantre antar mukhe bodha ātmani ahanta āspade iti arthaḥ darśanam iti nirvikalpakam anubhavanam upalakṣaṇam ca etad  vikalpa smṛti ādeḥ api jñānasya jñāna antareṇa parāmarśe hi ayam eva nyāyaḥ vikalpayāmi aham smarāmi aham vikalpitam mayā smṛtam mayā iti ahanta ārūḍhyā eva vikalpa ādeḥ avabhāsāt  ata eva ātmanaḥ amī vikalpa ādyāḥ śakti viśeṣāḥ tad viśrānta śarīra tvāt iti darśitam jñāna smṛti apohana śaktimān iti atra evam iyataḥ prameyasya yad phalam tad upasaṃhartum āha tad  iti tasmāt arthe pūrva uktasya prameyasya hetu bhāvena upajīvanam iha sūcayati yata evam uktam anubhavasya arthasya iva smaraṇāt  na bhedena avabhāsaḥ smrṭi śaktiḥ ca parameśvarasya eva tatas  idam atra pariniṣṭhitam tattvam iti iha smṛtiḥ anubhavam kroḍīkaroti iti uktam anubhavaḥ ca dvidhā parāmarśa bhedāt  kadācid  sva ātma parāmarśa pūrvakam anubhāvyam parāmṛśati yatra asya abhisaṃdhi pradhāna tā mayā dṛśyate iti kadācid  anubhavanīyam eva pradhāna tayā parāmṛśati yatra anabhisaṃdheḥ eva sahasā vastu upanipātaḥ artha kriyām prati āgraha viśeṣaḥ  vā ayam iti tatra api ca prakāśa parām arśaḥ  asti eva anyathā prakāśa ayogāt  evam ubhayathā anubhave pratyekam smṛtiḥ api dvaya parāmarśa mayī udeti iti catvāraḥ smaraṇa bhedāḥ dvau anubhava bhedau anusaṃdhānam pratyabhijñānam api etad ubhaya melana ātmakam atra eva antarbhūtam tad ca etad bhedāt  aṣṭadhā pūrva apara viśrānti kṛtāt  pratyekam dvidhā bhedāt ca ṣoḍaśadhā tad ete dvāviṃśatiḥ saṃvedana bhedāḥ teṣu ca grāhyam tāvat  prakāśāt  abahiḥ bhūtam anyathā prakāśanā yogāt bahis bhūtam ca tad  anyathārthatva asaṃbhavāt  na ca tatas  eva tadā eva tad eva apṛthak bhūtam atra pṛthak bhūtam ca bhavati iti nūnam anyaḥ kalpita prakāśa ātmā kaścid  atra arthaḥ  asti yatas  ayam artha rāśiḥ pṛthak bhavan anyonyam api pṛthaktām adhigacchet  anyathā prakāśa abhinnānām parasparam api kathaṅkāram pṛthak bhāvaḥ  bhavet  saḥ  ayam vedya eka deśa eva vicchinna eva anujjhita vedya bhāva eva aham iti viccheda śūmya prakāśa ucitena parāmarśena parāmṛśyamānaḥ  māyā pramātā iti vakṣyate dehe buddhau iti atra sa ca grāhaka iti ucyate evam samam eva sva ātmani nirmalam akura sthānīye yad  yugalakam svasmāt  prakāśa rūpāt  avyatiriktam avabhāsayati parameśvaraḥ tad eva etad  bhagavataḥ  jñāna kartṛ tvam smaraṇa kartṛ tvam jñāna śakti smṛti śakti rūpam ucyate iti tātparya arthaḥ akṣara arthaḥ tu mayā dṛśyate iti ayam iti ca yad  āmṛśati pramātā prakāśa rūpaḥ  yena anubhavati iti ucyate tatas  āmarśanāt  etad  lakṣyate grāhya rūpeṇa grāhaka rūpeṇa yojitau ghaṭa ādi deha ādi svabhāvau arthau vedyau pramātari viśuddha prakāśa rūpe bhātaḥ prakāśete evam dṛṣṭaḥ iti sa iti ca yad  parāmṛśati prakāśa rūpaḥ pramātā yatas  asau smarati iti vyapadeśyaḥ tatas  api etad eva lakṣyate anubhava rūpa upajīvi tvam pūrva uktam draḍhayitum prasaṅgāt  atra jñāna śakteḥ api unmīlanam kṛtam lakṣaṇe śatra ādeśaḥ api śabdaḥ ca arthe artha śabdaḥ  vicchinna vedya vācī grāhakaḥ  māyīyaḥ kalpitaḥ pramātā aśuddha prakāśa svabhāvaḥ iti śivam āditas  ślaḥ  iti śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta viracitāyāṃīśvara pratyabhijñā sūtra vimarśinyām prathame jñāna adhikāre smṛti śakti nirūpaṇam nāma caturtham āhnikam atha pañcamam āhnikam mahā guhā antar nirmagna bhāva jāta prakāśakaḥ jñāna śakti pradīpena yaḥ sadā tam stumaḥ śivam evam tāvat  smṛti śakteḥ svarūpam pratipāditam adhunā tad upajīvanīya jñāna śakti parama artha nirṇayam vitatya vartamāna avabhāsñām iti ādikayā sa kramam pratibhāsate iti antayā śloka ekaviṃśatyā nirūpayati tatra ādi eva ślokena vastuni pratijñām karoti evaṃbhūtā jñānaśaktiḥ iti tatas  śloka dvayena prakāśa eva arthānām svarūpa iti āha tatas  dvayena prakāśa bāhyānām arthānām sadbhāvam vijñāna vādi upagata vāsanā dūṣaṇena dṛḍhīkṛtam āśaṅkya tṛtīyena tad anabhyupagame api tāvat  na kiñcid  uparudhyata iti darśayati atha ślokena sva darśane artha tattvam upadarśayan bāhya artha sadbhāve pratyakṣam parākaroti pramāṇa tvena tatas  dvayena anumeya tām api bāhyasya nirasyati anantaram ślokena cit ātmani arthānām avaśyam sadbhāvaḥ parāmarśa ātmanā iti prakaṭayati tatas  api prakāśasya pramātṛ rūpasya pratyavamarśa eva jīvatam iti śloka catuṣṭayena anubhava āgama nyāya svarūpa nirūpaṇābhiḥ abhidhatte anantaram jñāna parāmarśa eva jñeyam śuddham pramātṛ rūpa tā an ujjhitam ca prakṣayati iti tasya eva pradhāna tve nyāyam śloka trayeṇa āha prakāśa eka rūpa tve ca jñāna jñātra ādi bhinnam iti ślokena āha tatas  jñātari iva viśuddhe jñāne api avikalpaka savikalpaka rūpe vimarśa eva prāṇitam iti śloka dvayena āha tatas  jñātuḥ jñānasya ca pūrva pakṣe dūṣi yad  bhinna tvam tad  upasaṃhāra diśā ślokena samarthayate iti tātparyam āhnikasya śloka arthaḥ tu nirūpyate nanu smaraṇa vikalpa ādīnām anubhava eva jīvitam tatra yadi bhedena ābhāsa ante arthāḥ tad  teṣu api tathā eva avabhāsa ucitaḥ naḥ ced  anyathā tad anubhava eva tāvat  jñāna śakti rūpaḥ  vicāraṇīya iti āśayena āha vartamāna tvena sphuṭa tayā avabhāsanam idam iti evam ākāram yeṣām teṣām yad etad  bahis ātmanā kalpita māyīya śūnyādi śarīra anta pramātṛ pṛthak bhāvena hetunā bhinnānām tatas  māyā pramātuḥ vicchinnānām avabhāsanam tad  parama artha pramātari śuddha cit maye antar sthitavatām tena saha aikātmyam anujjhitavatām eva ghaṭatepramāṇena upapadyate tena anujjhita saṃvid abhedasya bhāvasya kalpita pramātṛ apekṣayā bhedena prakāśanam bhagavataḥ  jñānaśaktiḥ iti uktam bhavati pramāṇena upapadyate iti uktam tad  pramāṇam darśayati arthaḥ  nīla ādiḥ tasya nīla ādi rūpa tā eva yadi prakāśamānatā na punar  sā aparā kācid  artha śarīra uttīrṇā prakāśa ātma tā tarhi yathā sarvān prati nīlam eva tad saṃbhāvanayā bhaṇyate na kaṃcid  vā prati vastu tas  vā sva ātmani eva tad  nīlam parasya para niṣṭhatvā anupapatteḥ sva ātmani vā na nīlam na anīlam prakāśa anugraheṇa vinā vyavasthāna ayogāt tathā prakāśamāna tā api asya sarvān prati na kaṃcid  vā prati api tu sva ātmani eva sva ātmani api vā na syāt  iti andhatā jagataḥ atha indriya āloka ādi kṣaṇa vargāt prakāśa rūpaḥ  asau nīla kṣaṇaḥ  viśiṣṭa eva jātaḥ evam api sa eva prasaṅgaḥ prakaṭa tā vāde api ayam eva doṣaḥ sarvathā artha śarīra viśrāntaḥ ced  prakāśaḥ  mama avabhāsate iti pramātṛ lagna tayā prakāśa sthitiḥ durupapādā pramātā hi tadānīm indriya ādi mayaḥ  artha rūpa prakāśasya kāraṇam bhavet  bījam iva aṅkurasya na ca aṅkuraḥ bīja apekṣaḥ  aṅkura ātmā tatas  yadi na prakāśa ātmā sa syāt  prāk iva jñāna udayāt pūrvam yathā asau  aprakāśaḥ tathā jñāna udaye api syāt  nanu jñānam artha prakāśa rūpam eva tad  katham jñānasya udaya anudayayoḥ arthasya tulya tā syāt  syāt  etad  yadi upapadyet  yāvatā arthāt  bhinnam yad  jñānam prakāśa rūpam tad  arthasya saṃbandhi tayā katham syāt  yadi tāvat  arthaḥ prakāśate iti evaṃbhūtam jñānasya svarūpam tad  artha jñānayoḥ abheda eva āyātaḥ artha svabhāvasya jñāna tvena ukta tvāt  artha svabhāva tve ca sati prakāśasya artha ātma tāyām uktam dūṣaṇam atha artham prakāśayati iti jñānasya svarūpam tarhi prakāśamānam artham karoti jñānam iti āpatite punar api sa eva doṣaḥ kṛta pratānaḥ ca ayam prakṛti arthaṇī artha vivekaḥ  mayā eva bheda vidāraṇe iti tatas  eva anveṣyaḥ tasmāt  bhinnaḥ prakāśaḥ  arthasya saṃbandhī bhavati iti saṃbhāvanā eva na asti tad ca idam upapattyā āyātam arthasya svarūpam prakāśamānatā prakāśa abhinna tvam iti prakāśaḥ ca yadi ghaṭe anyaḥ paṭe anyaḥ tadā anusaṃdhānasya ayogaḥ dvayoḥ prakāśayoḥ sva ātma mātra paryavasānāt  iti vitatya upapāditam naśyet  jana sthitiḥ iti atra tasmāt  eka eva prakāśaḥ etad eva āvṛttyā darśitam na ca prakāśaḥ  bhinnaḥ syāt  iti vyatiriktasya jñānasya artha prakāśa rūpa tām abhyupagamya api bādhaka antaram āha yadi arthāt  anya eva jñāna ātmā prakāśaḥ ata eva bhinnaḥ arthataḥ tarhi sva ātmani tasya prakāśa mātra rūpa tvāt  abheda eva tathā hi nīlasya prakāśaḥ pītasya prakāśaḥ iti yaḥ  nīla aṃśaḥ pīta aṃśaḥ ca sa na tāvat  jñānasya svarūpam bheda vāda tyāga āpatteḥ atha viṣayaḥ tad eva idam vicāryate iha prakāśa balāt  nīla pītayoḥ bhedaḥ  abhyupagantavyaḥ yena eva ca prakāśena nīlaḥ  nīla eva iti upagamyate tena eva ca prakāśena pītaḥ pīta iti katham saṃgacchatām nīlena janitaḥ pītena janitaḥ tena vā saha samāna sāmagrīka ityādi yad  ucyate tad  siddhe nīla pītayoḥ bhede syāt  sa eva vicāryaḥ atha nīla ākāraḥ  asau tad  yadi pratibimba balāt  tad dvitīya bimba anavabhāsāt ayuktam atha abhedaḥ tarhi tyaktaḥ  bheda vādaḥ tathā karaṇa tā ādi vāde śikhara stha jñānam bahutara nīlā ādi janyam ekatra paṭu anyatra mandam iti katham bhedaḥ prakāśa śarīrasya abhedāt  tathābhūte ca anyatara darśana udbhūte api saṃskāre balāt eva aśeṣa smaraṇa prasaṅga iti bhūyān saṅkaraḥ syāt etad  artha eva astu kim anena doṣa āpādakena prakāśena iti atra āha aprakāśasya prasiddhiḥ eva na kācid  sva ātmani hi nīlam yadi pūtam na kiṃcid  vā tad  kim duṣyet  ata eva grantha kṛtā eva anyatra uktam evam ātmani asat kalpāḥ prakāśasya eva santi amī jaḍāḥ prakāśa eva asti sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti tad  yadi prakāśaḥ tadā bhavati arthaḥ prakāśaḥ ca asau katham yadi prakāśa tā eva ghaṭasya vapuḥ sā eva paṭasya ityādi viśva vapuḥ prakāśaḥ siddhaḥ ekasya eva prakāśasya evaṃbhūta krama ākrama kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi vicitra vaiśvarūpya pradarśana sāmarthya rūpam aiśvaryam iti etāvat  paryavasāyayitavyam tad ca evam paryavasyati yadi prakāśasya vicitra bhāve hetu antaram apākṛtam tatra prakāśasya avicitrasya krameṇa vicitra tā kāraṇam pratibimba ātmakam tad pratibimba sajātīyam yad  tad eva nīla ādi rūpam bāhyam tad ca yadi api anumeyam tathā api idam nīlam iti pratyakṣeṇa adhyavasāyāt  adhyavasāya prāṇita tvāt ca pramāṇa sthiteḥ pratyakṣa vyapadeśyam bhaviṣyati bāhya artha vāda ukathitam iti hetu antaram anumīyamāna bāhya rūpam āśaṅkyamāna tvena darśayati iha bodhaḥ tāvat  abhinnaḥ prakāśa mātram eva hi asya parama arthaḥ prakāśa adhikam yadi nīlasya rūpam tarhi tad  aprakāśa rūpam iti na prakāśeta atha tathā prakāśa tvam eva asya rūpam pīta prakāśaḥ katham syāt  atha api kramika nīla pīta ādi prakāśa rūpam eva tasya svarūpam nīla ādi ābhāsa śūnyaḥ  aham iti prakāśaḥ svāpa ādi avasthāsu na syāt  tasmāt  prakāśaḥ prakāśa eva aṇu mātram api na rūpa antaram asya asti iti abhinnaḥ bodhaḥ tasya ca abhinnasya kadācid  nīla ābhāsa tā kadācid  pīta ābhāsa tā iti ye vicitra ābhāsāḥ tatra kāraṇa tvam hi yasymāt  na upapannam hetau abhinne kārya bhedasya asaṃbhavāt  tasmāt  sa sa vicitra nīla pīta ādi rūpa ākāsmikaḥ  ajñāta pratyakṣa siddha hetukaḥ san bāhyam vijñāna gata pratibimba ātmaka sva svabhāva saṃpādakam aucityāt  nija rūpa sadṛśam krama upanipatat rūpa bahutara bheda ātmakam jñānāt  sarvathā pṛthak bhūtam anumāpayati iti saṃbhāvayate bāhya artha vādī na ca asya idam saṃbhāvanā mātram api tu niścaya paryavasāyi eva bhavati tathā hi vijñāna vādinā yaḥ  hetuḥ vaicitrye vāsanā prabodha lakṣaṇa uktaḥ sa na upapadyate smṛti janakaḥ saṃskāraḥ  vāsanā iti tāvat  prasiddham iha tu anubhava vaicitrya hetuḥ paryeṣaṇīyaḥ  vartate astu vā nīla ādi ābhāsa saṃpādana sāmarthya rūpā jñānasya yogyatā ātmikā śaktiḥ vāsanā tasyāḥ ca sva kārya saṃpādana unmukhyam prabodhaḥ tatas  bodheṣu ābhāsa vaicitryam iti tatra api tu brūmaḥ iha yadya api ābhāsānām jñāna antarvartinām apāramārthika tvam saṃvṛti sattvam ucyeta api tathā api yad eṣām tad  vastu sadeva aṅgīkāryam avastunaḥ sarva sāmarthya virahita alakṣaṇasya kārya saṃpādana prāṇita sāmārtthya ātmaka svabhāva anupapatteḥ evaṃsthite yā etā vāsanā ābhāsa kāraṇa tvena iṣyante tāsām bodhāt  yadi bhinnam rūpam tad ca paramārtha sat  tad ayam śabda antara pracchannaḥ  bāhya arthavāda prakāra eva atha saṃvṛti sat  tarhi tena rūpeṇa kāraṇa tā anupapattiḥ tathā yena rūpeṇa āsām pāramārthika tā tena kāraṇa tā tad  tarhi jñāna mātram tad ca abhinnam iti nīla ādi ābhāsa rūpasya kārya bhedasya asiddhiḥ evam vāsanānām abicitra tve tad prabodhaḥ  vicitra iti kā pratyāśā bhavantu vā vāsanā bhinnāḥ tathā api bodha mātra atiriktasya deśa kāla bhāva ādeḥ prabodhaka abhimatasya vicitrasya kāraṇasya abhāvāt  prabodhaḥ avicitra iti eka eva prabodhaḥ iti samam eva nīla ādi vaicitryam bhāseta atha sva saṃtāna vartīni jñāna antarāṇi vicitrāṇi prabodha kāraṇāni iti tad asat  sukha duḥkha nīka pīla ādi pūrva apara ādi deśa kāla bhedasya vijñāna mātra rūpa tve vijñānasya ca prakāśa mātra pramā artha tāyām svarūpa bheda asaṃbhave tathā bodha vailakṣaṇya anupapatteḥ para pramātṛ rūpeṣu bodha antariṣu saṃtāna antara śabda vācyeṣu api tulyaḥ ayam availakṣaṇya prakāraḥ tatra api parakīya abhimatasya kṛśa sthūla ādeḥ kāyasya śvāsa praśvāsa ādeḥ prāṇasya sukha duḥkha ādeḥ dhī guṇasya anumātṛ abhimata saṃbinmātra rūpa abhede para tvam kasya bhavet  iti na vidmaḥ bodhasya tad niṣṭhasya iti ced  saḥ  api pramāṇena yadi na siddhaḥ tad  asat  eva siddhaḥ  api prameya tayā ced  tad  jaḍa eva tathā api ca kāya ādivat  eva jñāna mātra svabhāvaḥ sva saṃvid mātra rūpa tve param prati asya asiddheḥ nanu vyāhāra ādi kriyā sva ātmani icchayā vyāhareyam iti evaṃrūpayā hetu bhāvena vyāptā dṛṣṭā tad  caitra kāye api tayā tad hetukayā bhāvyam na ca mad saṃtati patitā samīhā asti iti sva saṃvedanena niścitam tatas ca para samīhā siddhyati tad eva saṃtāna antaram iti atra ucyate iha anumātuḥ vyāhāra ābhāsaḥ  dvidhā bhavati vyāpti grahaṇa kāle aviccheda prāṇaḥ  aham vyāharāmi iti evaṃrūpaḥ anumāna avasare ca vyāharati ayam iti viccheda jīvita iti anyasya vyāptiḥ gṛhītā anyaḥ ca ābhāsaḥ katham idānīm hetuḥ syāt  vyāharati iti ābhāsasya hetuḥ avidita eva iti katham tatas  hetoḥ samīhā anumīyeta kim ca vyāharati ayam iti yaḥ pramātṛ antare anumātṛ saṃmate vicchinna tayā avabhāsaḥ saḥ anumeya saṃmatāyāḥ paramīhāyāḥ katham kāryaḥ syāt  tasyāḥ  hi vyāharāmi iti ābhāsaḥ kāryaḥ  yaḥ asau aviccheda jīvitaḥ na ca aviccheda mayasya viccheda mayaḥ kāryam iti yuktam tathābhūta kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇa upāya abhāvāt na hi sva ātmani yaḥ ayam avicchinna ābhāsaḥ sa paratra vicchinnam vyāharati iti evaṃrūpam ābhāsam janayati iti kenacid  pramāṇena siddham para siddhi pūrvaka tvāt  asya arthasya para pramātṛ siddhaḥ ca evaṃbhūta artha adhīna tvena itaretara āśrayāt na ca avaśyan avicchinnāt  vicchinnena bhāvyam iti niyamaḥ  asti vyavhicārāt  na ca vicchinnaḥ api ābhāsa
