upadyatām iti tad anusaṃdhānāt tad utpattiḥ niyatā tad sadbhāve api asya anutpatteḥ tad abhāve ca utpatteḥ vicchinna ābhāsaḥ paratra utpadyatām iti yā samīhā tayā saha pratra utpannasya vicchinna ābhāsasya kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam eva para asiddhau na yukta iti vyāpteḥ eva asiddhiḥ pramātṛ antarāṇi ca yadi bhinnāni tadā tad niṣṭhānām avabhāsānām bheda eva jñānāt avyatiriktam ca iti nyāyāt  tatas ca eka ābhāsa niṣṭhatva abhāvāt eka ābhāsa viśrāntaḥ saṃbhūya pramātḥṇām vyavahāraḥ  na syāt  iti anyosaṃbhavaḥ yad  prameyam bodhāt  bhinnam bhavati iti saha upalambha niyama ādeḥ anaikāntika tvāt  nīla pīta ādinā api prameya rāśinā kim apakṛtam yena asya sva rūpa viśrāntiḥ na sahyate tasmāt  pramātṛ antarāṇām api asiddhiḥ eva siddhau vā sarva pramātṛ antargatā ābhāsā eka ekatra paratra ābhāsa vaicitrya hetum vāsanā udvodha vaicitryam janayeyuḥ niyame hetu antara abhāvāt  iti tathā api na nīla ādi vaicitrya siddhiḥ evam vāsanānām tad udbodha hetūnām ca vicitrāṇām anupapattiḥ eva tatas ca sthitam etad  abhinnaḥ bodhaḥ tasya ākasmikā ābhāsa bheda hetutva anupapatteḥ bāhyaḥ arthaḥ anumeyaḥ saṃbhāvyate iti yadi bāhya artha vādinā ucyate iti śloka dvaya arthaḥ ced śabdaḥ śloka dvaya vākya artha śaṅkā ādyotakaḥ evam āśaṅkyamāna tvena para saṃbhāvanā dṛḍhā darśitā adhunā tu enām saṃbhāvanām śithilayitum tāvat āha syāt etad  iti pūrva ukta saṃbhāvanā abhyupagame yadā vyākhyāyate tadā kim tu iti vākya śeṣeṇa tad śaithilya viṣayam saṃbhāvanā antaram śeṣa ślokena darśayate iti vyākhyeyam yadi tu adhyāhāraḥ  na sahyate tadā syāt etad iti idam api saṃbhāvanā antaram syāt  yad anena ślokena ucyate iti eka vākyatayā yojyam anayā api kaṣṭa kalpanayā bāhyān arthān prasādhayatā bhavatā taiḥ na kiṃcid  kartavyam ābhāsaiḥ eva taiḥ bhavatā abhyupagataiḥ vyavahāra siddheḥ na hi nitya anumeyena kaścid  vyavahāra iti kim bāhyena yatra sādhakam ca na asti pramāṇam bādhakam ca prakāśāt  bhede anumeya tayā api prakāśana abhāva iti tāvat  mukhyam abhyuścaya bādhakaḥ tu avayavinaḥ  vṛtti anupapattiḥ samavāya asiddhiḥ kampā kampa āvaraṇān āvaraṇa raktā rakta diś bhāga bheda ādi viruddha dharma yogaḥ aṇu saṃcaya bāhya vāde api saṃcayasya anyasya abhāve paramāṇava eva te ca yadi saṃyujyante nirantara tayā tad  avaśyam diś bhāga bhedaḥ eva na akṣe ṣaṭsu dikṣu saṃcīyamāneṣu ṣaṭsu aṇuṣu madhyamasya paramāṇoḥ yatra eva dhāmni ekaḥ  lagnaḥ tatra eva yadi aparaḥ tad  eka paramāṇu mātra tā atha anyatra ekaḥ anyatar aparaḥ tad  avaśyam bhāga bheda āpattiḥ iti bhāga eva san tasya api eṣā eva saraṇiḥ iti na kiṃcid  avaśiṣyate bāhyam tattvataḥ na ca etad  vācyam mūrtānām eka deśatva ayogāt saṃyoge bhinna deśatva avyāvṛtteḥ tad niṣṭam dvi aṇukam nāma kārya dravyam aṇu parimāṇam tebhyaḥ tribhyaḥ  mahat kāryam iti avayavī ivādaḥ  hi ayam sa ca pūrvam eva apabādhitaḥ yad ca avyāpya vṛtti tvam saṃyogasya ucyate tad niraṃśe katham saṃgacchatām sva āśraye hi yadi asau samavaiti kim anyāt  asya avaśiṣyate yad  na vyāpnuyāt  iti abhyuścaya bādhakam ca idam iti na atra asmābhiḥ bharaḥ kṛtaḥ vistareṇa ca prajñā alaṅkāre darśitam ācārya śaṅkara nandanena nanu bādhakam nāma pramāṇa siddhe vastuni na kiṃcid  kartum samartham tena eva dṛḍhena pramāṇena bādhaka abhimatasya bādhitasya apramāṇatva saṃpādanāt  darśitam ca iha sādhakam pramāṇam kārya hetuḥ tad tad ākasmika ābhāsa iti kārikayā iti āśaṅkya āha iha tāvat  svapna smaraṇa manaḥ rājya saṃkalpa ādiṣu nīla ādi ābhāsa vaicitryam bāhya samarpa kahtu vyatirekeṇa eva nirbhāsate iti yadi api asti saṃbhavaḥ tathā api tad ābhāsa vaicitryam asthaiḥ yāt  sarva pramātra sādhāraṇyāt  pūrva anubhava saṃskāra jatu asaṃbhāvanāt avastu iti śaṅkyeta yad  punar idam yoginām icchā mātreṇa purasena ādi vaicitrya nirmāṇam dṛṣṭam tatra upādānam prasiddha mṛd kāṣṭha śukra śoṇi tādi vaicitrya mayam na saṃbhavati eva na hi evam vaktum śakyam sarva gatāḥ paramāṇavaḥ  yogi icchayā jhaṭiti saṃghaṭitāḥ kāryam ārapsyante iti yad  etad  loka prasiddha kāraṇa bhāva anatikrama siddhaye nirūpyate na ca etad  prasiddham pramāṇubhya eva sthūlam ghaṭa ādi jāyate iti kim tu kapāla ādi vyavadhānena tathā api niyata sahakāri samavalambanam kara caraṇa ādi vyāpāre viśiṣṭa deśa kāla dharma ādhipati ayogaḥ śikṣā abhyāsa prakarṣa iti iyati ca āṃśrīyamāṇe yogī kumbham nirmimāṇaḥ kumbhakāra prasiddha sanasta sāmagrī sanarjana puraḥsaraṃghaṭam ghaṭayan kumbhakāra eva syāt  tasmāt  prasiddha kāraṇa ullaṅghane kim asaṃcetyamāna paramāṇu ādi upādāna kāraṇa antara cintayā iti tatra yogi saṃvida eva sā tādṛśī śaktiḥ yad  ābhāsa vaicitrya rūpam artha jātam prakāśayati iti tad asti saṃbhavaḥ yad  saṃvid  eva abhyupagata svātantryā apratīdhāta lakṣaṇāt  icchā viśeṣa vaśāt saṃvidaḥ  anidhika ātma tāyā anapāyāt  antar sthitam eva sat  bhāva jātam idam iti evam prāṇa buddhi deha ādeḥ vitīrṇa kiyat mātra saṃvidūpāt svātantryam kim na abhyupagamyate sva saṃvedana siddham kim iti hetu antara paryeṣaṇa aprayāsena khidyate eva kāreṇa idam āha sarveṇa tāvat  vādinā viṣaya vyavasthāpanam saṃvid rūpam anapahnavanīyam ādi siddham hi tad  iti uktam tasya ca svātantryam eva deva śabda nirdiṣṭam cit rūpa tvam iti kim apara kāraṇa anveṣaṇa vyasani tayā hi yasmāt  evam prakāśayati deva iti saṃbhāvyate tasmāt  kim bāhyena anupapattinā iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ nanu evam ubhayathā api saṃbhāvanā anumānam unmiṣati tatra kim makura pratibimbita ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭāntena jñāna pratibimba tā ābhāsa vaicitrye vijñāna darpaṇa atiriktam tatas  eva bāhya abhimatam hetum kalpayema kim vā yogi dṛṣṭāntena saṃvid svātantryam eva hetu bhāvena brūyāma tad idam sāṃśayikam vartate iti āśaṅkya bāhya artha anumāna saṃbhāvanām sūtra dvayena apākartum āha na kevalam anantara śloka nirdiṣṭābhiḥ yuktabhiḥ pratyakṣeṇa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ  na bhāsate iyat eva hi pratyakṣam tad ca nīlam bhāti iti sva prakāśa saṃvid rūpam na adhikam kiṃcid  iti yāvat  anumānena api na asya bāhya asya siddhiḥ iti api śabdasya abhiprāyaḥ tatra anumānam atra na eva pravartitum utsahate pravṛttam api na prakṛta siddhim ādavyāt  iti anena sūtra dvayena upadarśyate tatra anumānam vikalpaḥ sarvaḥ ca ayam vikalpaḥ anubhava mūla iti prasiddham tena yad  sarvathā anābhāta pūrvam ananubhūta caram tatra anumānam anumiti vyāpāraḥ  vikalpa ātmā na eva kenacid  vādinā iṣyate nanu bhavatu pratyakṣataḥ dṛṣṭe anumāne saṃkathā iyam sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭe tu kim vakṣyasi yathā artha upalabdhyā indriya anumāne ucyate tatra api vikalpena yathā saḥ arthaḥ spṛśyate tathā anumeya iti sthitiḥ vikalpaḥ ca na indriya ādikam artham kenacid  saṃniveśa viśeṣa ādinā viśeṣa ātmanā spṛśati api tu kiṃcid upalabdheḥ kāraṇam iti amunā svabhāvena sa ca svabhāvaḥ kāraṇa tā lakṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣa gṛhīta eva tathā ca bījāt  aṅkuraḥ tantubhyaḥ paṭa iti ādau kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha balena tāvat  niśceyaḥ tatra ca pratyakṣam pratyābhāsam prāmāṇyam bhajate vimarśa lakṣaṇasya pramiti vyāpārasya ekaika śabda vācye arthe pravṛtteḥ tad anusāri tvāt ca pramāṇasya iti vakṣyate eka abhidhāna viṣaye mitiḥ vastuni abādhitā iti ābhāsa mātram ca sāmānyam iti nir eṣuate anupalambhaḥ api anya upalambha rūpa ābhāsa mātra viśrānta eva iti kāraṇa ābhāsaḥ  viśeṣa śūnyaḥ parigṛhīta eva bījāt  aṅkura iti pratītau yad  yasya niyamam anuvidhatte avyatiriktam tad  tasya kāryam iti pratighaṭam mṛttikā ādi rūpa hetu tadvat mātrasya āmāsāt  ābhāsāt  bāhyaḥ punarnābhāsa rūpaḥ sa ca ābhāsate iti vipratiṣiddham anābhāse ca na asti vikalpa rūpasya anumānasya vyāpāraḥ grāma gṛha ādeḥ tu yad  bāhyam tad  agrāma ādi rūpam na ucyate pratyekam vāṭānūpa kuṇya tula ādeḥ bāhyatva prasaṅgāt  api tu tad saṃnikaṭam tasmāt  grāma bāhyam ābhāsa bāhyam iti ca śabda sāmya mātram etad  na vastu sāmyam evam ye vikalpe vastu na ābhāti iti manyante teṣām api tāvat  anumāna vikalpaḥ  na bāhye upapannaḥ asmābhiḥ tu upapāditam adhyavasāyasya api ābhāsamāna viṣaya tvam bhrānti tve ca avasāyasya iti sūtre tena anumāna vikalpa ātmanā api prakāśena yadi anāviṣṭaḥ  nīla ādiḥ arthaḥ tad  na anumita eva syāt  atha āviṣṭa eva tarhi prāk iva arthaḥ  aprakāśaḥ syāt  iti nyāyena prakāśa mātra svabhāva eva na bāhyaḥ tena bāhye sādhye yad  kiṃcid  pramāṇam ānīyate tad abāhyatām eva pratyuta sādhayati iti viruddham eva ata eva āha kathaṃcana iti kena api prakāreṇa pratyakṣa ātmanā anumeya ātmanā vā ābhāsanam ābhāsaḥ  bāhyasya anābhāsasya na kadācid  abhūt  iti tasmāt  siddham cit ātmā eva hi deva iti nanu antar sthitam bahis  prakāśayet iti uktam tad  antar sthita tvam upapādanīyam iti āśaṅkya āha bahīrūpatayā ābhāsane api ahantā rūpa tā na truṭyati pramātra aikātmyam āntaryam iti hi vakṣyate tad ca sadā eva prakāśasya pramātṛ tvāt tad ātma tayā ca vinā aprakāśamānasya avastu tvāt  kim tu tatra aham iti ucite parāmarśe yaḥ  ayam idantā parāmarśaḥ sā eva bāhya tā tad ca iha antar sthita tvam aham iti etāvatā cit samucitena eva bapuṣā parāmarśanam eva tad ca iha nīla ādīnām asti eva na tu na asti iti yadi hi na syāt  kumbha kṛtaḥ  ghaṭam karavāṇi iti ya uttara kriyām apekṣya icchā śabda vācyaḥ parāmarśaḥ eṣaṇīyena sa parāmṛśyena aniyantritaḥ ced  tatas  paṭa icchā api sā na kasmāt  iti saṃkīryeran vyavahārāḥ atha tatra api ca eṣaṇīyaḥ tadānīm eva nirmitaḥ san tathā jātaḥ tarhi tad nirmāṇam cit ātmani vinā icchayā na upapannam iti tiṣṭhāsoḥ evam icchā eva hetu tā iti atra varṇayiṣyate tad ca icchā antaram api viṣaya niyantritam na vā iti vikalpe anavasthā viṣaya niyantritam ced  syāt  ātma tā eva jātā na ced  ghaṭe paṭa icchā syāt  atha tatra api tadānīm eva iti kṛtvā anavasthā tasmāt  sarvaḥ  ayam bhāva rāśiḥ cit ātmani aham iti eva vapuṣā satata avabhāsura vapuḥ aiśvarya rūpāt ca svātantrya lakṣaṇāt  svāmi bhāvāt  vicitreṇa vapuṣā krama ākrama ādinā saṃvid  enam bahis karoti pramātṛ prathana pūrvakam tatra api kvacid  ābhāse pramātḥn ekīkaroti nitamba nīnṛtta iva prekṣakān tāvati hi teṣām ābhāse aikyam śarīra prāṇa buddhi sukha ādi ābhāsa aṃśeṣu tu bhedasya avigalanāt  na sarvathā aikyam ata eva pratikṣaṇam pramātṛ saṃyojana viyojana vaicitryeṇa parameśvaraḥ  viśvam sṛṣṭi saṃhāra ādinā prapañcayati tad uktam ācāryeṇa sadā sṛṣṭi vinodāya sadā sthiti sukha asine sadā tribhuvana āhāra tṛptāya bhavate namaḥ ityādi śrī bhaṭṭa nārāyaṇena api muhur muhur aviśrāntaḥ trailokyam kalpanā śataiḥ kalpayan  api kaḥ  api ekaḥ nirvikalpaḥ  jayati ajaḥ iti tasmāt  sthitam antar sthitam bhāva jātam tena vinā tad viṣayasya parāmarśa ayogāt iti nanu parāmarśaḥ  nāma vikalpaḥ sa ca avikalpa śuddha saṃvid vapuṣi bhagavati katham syāt  iti āśaṅkya āha iha avabhāvasya prakāśasya anavabhāsasya ca aprakāśasya ghaṭa ādeḥ paraspara parihāreṇa dvayoḥ sva ātmani ced  vyavasthānam tad  ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva idamjaḍam idam jaḍam iti durupapādam vailakṣaṇyam atha avabhāsaḥ  yatas  arthasya saṃbamdhī tatas  na jaḍaḥ tarhi saṃbandha mātreṇa mṛt api ghaṭasya iti ajaḍā syāt  atha na sva saṃbandha mātram api tu avabhāsaḥ  arthasya prakāśaḥ tarhi artha ātmanā sa prakāśa iti samāpatitam na ca anya ātmanā anyasya prakāśa upapannaḥ atha anya svabhāvaḥ  api ghaṭaḥ avabhāsasya kāraṇam tarhi avabhāsaḥ api ghaṭasya kāraṇam iti ghaṭaḥ api ajaḍaḥ syāt  atha anyena satā api ghaṭena yatas  avabhāsasya pratibimba rūpā cchāyā dattā tām asau adabhāsaḥ  bibhrat  ghaṭasya iti ucyate tatas ca ajaḍaḥ tarhi sphaṭika salilam akurādiḥ api evaṃbhūta eva iti ajaḍa eva syāt  atha tathābhūtam api ātmānam tam ca ghaṭa ādikam sphaṭika ādiḥ na parāmraṣṭum samartha iti jad aḥ tathā aparāmarśanam eva ajāḍya jīvitam antar bahiṣkaraṇa svātantrya rūpam svābhāvikam avabhāsasya sva ātma viśrānti lakṣaṇam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam nāma aham evam prakāśa ātmā prakāśe iti hi vimarśa udaye sva saṃvid eva pramātṛ prameya pramāṇa ādi kṛtārtham abhimanyate na tu atiriktam kāṅkṣati sphaṭika ādi hi gṛhīta pratibimbam api tathā abhāvena siddhau pramātṛ antaram apekṣate iti nirvimarśa tvāt  jaḍam sarvatra vastu tas  vimarśa ātmaka pramātṛ svabhāva tādātmya ahaṃpara āmarśa viśrānteḥ ajaḍa tvam eva pūrva apara koṭyoḥ yad uktam idam iti asya vicchinna vimarśasya kṛtārtha tā yā sva svarūpe viśrāntiḥ vimarśaḥ saḥ  aham iti ayam iti madhya avasthā eva tu idantā vimṛśyamāna ūrvā para koṭiḥ vimūḍhānām māyā padam saṃsāraḥ iti vimarśa eva pradhānam bhagavata iti sthitam na kevalam saṃvid tattvasya asmābhiḥ eva vimarśa prādhānyam uktam yāvat  āgama antaraiḥ api iti darśayati yatas  vimarśa eva pradhānam ātmanaḥ  rūpam amum eva hetum prayojana rūpam uddiśya ātmā dharmi svabhāvaḥ  dravya bhūtaḥ  api caitantyam iti dharma vācinā śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam āśritya uditaḥ kathitaḥ bhagavatā śivasūtreṣu caitanyam ātmā iti paṭhitam caitanyam iti hi dharma vācakopa lakṣaṇam citi śaktiḥ apariṇāminī tad dṛśeḥ kaivalyam draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ iti ādau api hi dharma śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam ātmanaḥ  darśitam guruṇā anantena dravyam hi tad  ucyate yad viśrāntaḥ padārtha vargaḥ sarvaḥ  bhāti ca arthyate ca artha kriyāyai tad  yadi na tad  sakalaḥ  ayam tattva bhūta bhāva bhuvana saṃbhāraḥ saṃvidi viśrāntaḥ tathā bhavati iti sa eva guṇa karma ādi dharma āśraya bhūta padārtha antara svabhāvaḥ tām eva mukhya dravya svarūpam āśrayate iti sā eva dravyam tad  ananta dharma rāśi viśrama bhitti bhūtāyāḥ tasyāḥ sa eva dharmaḥ caitanyam iti kartṛ kṛt antāt  utpannena bhāva pratyayena saṃbandha abhidhāyinā api prādhānyena darśitaḥ tathā hi saṃbandha viśrāntasya pratīteḥ dravyta rūpasya ca saṃbandhinaḥ prakṛtyā ukta tvāt  citi kriyā rūpam dhramam saṃbaddham avagamayatā ṣyañā niṣkṛṣṭa aṃśaḥ pratyāyitaḥ  bhavati citi kriyā ca cittau kartṛ tā svātaṃtryam saṃyojana viyojana anusaṃdhāna ādi rūpam ātma mātra tāyām eva jaḍavat  aviśrānta tvam aparicchinna prakāśa sāra tvam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam iti tad eva anātma rūpāt  jaḍāt  saṃyojana viyojana ādi svātaṃtri avikalāt vailakṣaṇya ādāyi iti tad evam paratvena pradhāna tayā abhisaṃdhāya ātmā cetana iti vaktavye dharma antara adharīkaraṇāya vimarśa dharma uddhurīkaraṇāya ca ātmā caitanyam iti uktam cit kriyā citi kartṛ tātāt paryeṇa iti samāsaḥ ardha yuj  pāda viśrāntiḥ iti hi kāvye samayaḥ na śāstre yadi vā cit kriyā ātmā ucitaḥ citi kartṛ tā ca iti pṛthak eva evam tu na kvacid  paṭhitam nanu yathā prakāśaḥ  aprakāśaḥ ca iti ybhayam api sva ātmani tatas ca prakāśa iti ukte jaḍāt  na vailakṣaṇyam uditam syāt  tadvat  vimarśaḥ  api avimarśaḥ  api ca sva ātmani iti tena api katham vailakṣaṇyam jaḍa ajaḍayoḥ iti āśaṅkya āha cetayati iti atra yā citiḥ citi kriyā tasyāḥ pratyavamarśaḥ sva ātma camatkāra lakṣaṇa ātmā svabhāvaḥ tathā hi ghaṭena sva ātmani na camatkriyate sva ātmā na parāmṛśyate na sva ātmani tena prakāśyate na aparicchinna tayā bhāsyate tatas  ca cetyata iti ucyate caitreṇa tu sva ātmani aham iti saṃrambha udyoya ullāsa vibhūti yogāt camatkriyate sva ātmā parāmṛśyate sva ātmani eva prakāśyate idam iti yaḥ pariccheda etāvat rūpa tayā tad vilakṣaṇī bhāvena nīla pīta sukha duḥkha tad śūnyatā ādi asaṃkhyā avabhāsa yogena avabhāsyate tatas  caitreṇa cetyate iti ucyate evam ca vimarśaḥ sva ātmani avimarśaḥ  api sva ātmani iti asiddam etad vimarśaḥ  hi sarvaṃsahaḥ param api ātmīkaroti ātmānam ca parīkaroti ubhayam ekīkaroti ekīkṛtam dvayam api nyagbhāvayati iti evaṃsvabhāvaḥ pratyavamarśāḥ ca āntara abhilāpa ātmaka śabdana svabhāvaḥ tad ca śabdanam saṅketa nirapekṣam eva avicchinna camatkāra ātmakam antarmukha śiraḥ nirdeśa prakhyam akāra ādi māyīyasa aṅketika śabda jīvita bhūta  nīlam idaṃcaitraḥ  aham ityādi pratyavamarśa antara bhitti bhūta tvāt  pūrṇa tvāt  parā vakti viśvam abhilapati pratyavamarśena iti ca vāc  ata eva sā svarasena cit rūpa tayā sva ātma viśrānti vapuṣā uditā sadāna stamitā nityā aham iti eva etad eva paramātmanaḥ  mukhyam svātantryam aiśvaryam īśitṛ tvam ananya apekṣi tvam ucyate para aparam tu idaṃbhāva rūpasya pratyavamarśasya akhyāti prāṇasya udbodha mātre api ahaṃbhāva eva viśrānteḥ śrī sadāśiva ādi bhūmau paśyantī daśāyām aparam tu idaṃbhāvasya eva nirūḍhau māyā garbha adhikṛtānām eva viṣṇu viriñca indra ādīnām tad tu teṣām parameśvara prasāda jam eva iti anya nirapekṣa tā eva paramārtha ta ānandaḥ aiśvaryam svāta nryam caitanyam tasmāt  yuktam uktam tena jaḍāt sa hi vilakṣaṇaḥ iti pradhāna āgameṣu api etad  pradarśitam eva iti nirūpayati iha ghaṭaḥ kasmāt  asti sva puṣpam kasmāt  na asti iti ukta iti vaktāraḥ  bhavanti ghaṭaḥ  hi sphurati mama na tu itarat  iti tad etad ghaṭa tvam eva yadi sphurat tvam sphuraṇa saṃbandhaḥ tad  sarvadā sarvasya sphuret  na kasyacid vā tasmāt  mama sphurati iti kaḥ arthaḥ madīyam sphuraṇam spandanam ādiṣṭam iti spandanañca kiñcid calanam eṣā eva ca kiñcid rūpa tā yad  acalam api calam ābhāsate iti prakāśa svarūpam hi manāk api na atiricyate atiricyate iva iti tad  acalam eva ābhāsa bheda yuktam iva ca bhāti tatas  uktam ātmā eva sarva bhāveṣu sphurat nirvṛta cit vapuḥ aniruddha icchā prasaraḥ prasarat dṛkkriyaḥ śivaḥ iti yathā ati kruddhaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ  vā kim karomi iti vā mṛśan dhāvanvā yad padam gacchet tatra spandaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti spanda tattva viviktaye iti guṇa ādi spanda niḥṣyandāḥ iti ca loke api vividha vaicitrya yogena spandavat tvam sattā ca bhavana kartṛtā sarva kriyāṣu svātantryam sā ca sva puṣpa ādikam api vyāpnoti iti mahatī deśa kālau nīla ādivat  sā eva sṛjati iti tābhyām viśeṣaṇīyā na bhavati yad  kila yena tulya kakṣya tayā bhāti tad  tasya viśeṣaṇam kaṭaka iva caitrasya na ca deśa kālau vimarśena tulya kakṣyau bhātaḥ tayoḥ idantayā tasya ca ahantayā prakāśe tulya kakṣyatva anupapatteḥ evam deśa kāla asparśāt  vibhu tvam nitya tvam ca sakala deśa kāla sparśaḥ  pi tad nirmāṇa yogāt  iti tatas  api vyāpakatva nitya tve tad uktam mahāsattā mahādevī viśva jīvanam ucyate iti sāram iti yad  atuccham rūpam tad  iyam eva vimarśa śaktiḥ grāhya grāhakāṇām yad  prakāśa ātmakam rūpam tasya api aprakāśa vailakṣaṇya ākṣepikā iyam eva iti śrī sāraśāstre api nirūpitam yad sāram asya jagataḥ sā śaktiḥ mālinī parā iti sā eṣā iti śakti pratyabhijñānam darśitam hṛdayam ca nāma pratiṣṭhā sthānam ucyate tad ca uktanītyā jaḍānām cetanam tasya api prakāśāt prakatvam tasya api vimarśa śaktiḥ iti viśvasya parame pade tiṣṭhataḥ  viśrāntasya tasya idam eva hṛdayam vimarśa rūpam para mantra ātmakam yatra tatra abhidhīyate sarvasya hi mantra eva hṛdayam mantraḥ ca vimarśana ātmā vimarśanam ca parāvāc śakti mayam tatas  eva uktam na taiḥ vinā bhavet śabdaḥ  na arthaḥ  na api citeḥ gatiḥ iti tatra tāvat samāpannā mātṛ bhāvam ityādi ca iti āgameṣu tatrabhavat bhartṛ hariṇā api na saḥ  asti pratyayaḥ loke yaḥ śabda anugamāt ṛte anuviddham iva jñānam sarvam śabdena gamyate vāc rūpa tā ced utkrāmet avabodhasya śāśvatī na prakāśaḥ prakāśeta sā hi pratyavamarśinī iti sā eṣā saṃsāriṇām saṃjñā bahis antar ca vartate yad utkrāntau visaṃjñaḥ  ayam dṛśyate kāṣṭha kuṅyavat  ityādi ca tad  etena viduḥ iti etad  nirvāhitam bauddhaiḥ api adhyavasāya apekṣam prakāśasya prāmāṇyam vadadbhiḥ upagata prāya eva ayam arthaḥ abhilāpa ātmaka tvāt  adhyavasāyasya iti nanu asaṃkhya śakti śreṇa uśobhita vapuṣi parama śive vimarśa śaktiḥ eva iyam itthaṃkāram abhiṣicyate kasmāt  iti āśaṅkya āha sarvāḥ śaktoḥ kartṛtva śaktiḥ aiśvarya ātmā samākṣipati sā ca vimarśa rūpā iti yuktam asyāḥ  eva prādhānyam iti tātparyeṇa uttaram uktam śabda arthasya ayam prakāśa ātmā parameśvaraḥ sva ātmānam jñātṛ eka rūpa tvāt ajñeyam api jñeyīkaroti iti yad  saṃbhāvyate kāraṇa antarasya anupapatteḥ darśita tvāt  dṛḍhena saṃbhāvanā anumānena tadata eva vimarśa śakti lakṣaṇāt  kartṛ tvāt hetoḥ bhavati yatas  hi ayam ātmānam parāmṛśati tatas  viśva nirbhara tvāt  tathā nīla ādi tvena cakāsti nanu eṣā eva kutas  saṃbhāvanā ātmānam jñeyīkaroti iti āha pṛthak  prakāśāt  bahis bhūtā sthitiḥ yasya tādṛś  jñeyam na eva bhavati tuḥ avadhāreṇa tatra ca uktā yuktayaḥ abhyuccaya yuktim api āha yadi vyatiriktam jñeyam syāt  tad  jñātṛ rūpasya ātmanaḥ  yad  etad  jñeya viṣayam aunmukhyam sva saṃvedana siddham dṛśyate tad  na asya syāt  tena vyatirikta viṣaya aunmukhyena anya adhīna tvam nāma pāratantryam asya ānīyate pāratantryam ca svātantryasya viruddham svātantryam eva ca ananya mukha prekṣi tvam ātmanaḥ svarūpam iti vyatirikta unmukha ātmā anātmā eva syāt  anātmā ca jaḍaḥ  jñeyam prati na unmukhībhavati iti prasaṅgaḥ tatas  prasaṅga viparyayāt  idam āyātam avyatirikta unmukhaḥ svatantraḥ san ātmānam eva jñeyīkaroti iti na ca kevalam nīla ādi rūpam eva jñeyam yāvat  atyakta kartṛ svabhāvam svātantryeṇa aparityaktam eva santam ātmānam nirmāya vyavahāreṇa dhyāna upāsana arcana upadeśa ādinā yojayati iti yad  saṃbhāvyate tad api ata eva iti saṃbandhaḥ nanu svātantrya yuktam ca nirmīyate ca iti viruddham idam atra āha advaya ātmanaḥ saṃvid eka rūpasya svātantryāt  hetoḥ idam na na yujyate yad  kila māyā pade ati durghaṭam pratibhāti tad saṃpādane yad  apratihatam svātantryam tad eva punar  svātantrya śabdena darśitam ata eva iti anena tu vimarśa śakti rūpam iti apunaruktam atha vā ata eva svātantryāt  iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena śloka dvayena saṃbandhanīyam udāharaṇam atra arthe darśayati nīla ādi nirmāṇavat  asya svatrantra nirmāṇasya aprasiddha tvāt  īśvaraḥ  bhagavān ātmā nityaḥ  vibhuḥ svatantraḥ iti evamādau hi pramātuḥ pūjayituḥ dhyātuḥ vā apṛthak bhūtam tad  prameyam pūjyam dhyeyam ca bhāti iti tad  tāvat  nirmitam na ca anīśvaram evam hi īśvara iti anīśvara iti saṃkalpa dhyāna ādeḥ tulya tvam syāt  na ca evam phala bhedasya upalabdheḥ iti tasmāt  svātantrya śūnyatā ābhāsanena svātantrya yukta tā ābhāsanena ca yad  idam ubhayam jñeyam ātma rūpam eva parameśvaraḥ  bhāsayati tad  vimarśa śakti balāt  eva iti sā eva pradhānam iti nanu prakāśa balāt  bhāva vyavasthā sa ca prakāśaḥ  vimarśa sāra iti vimarśa abhede tad eva tad  iti vaktum yuktam īśvara ātmā ityādi saṃkalpeṣu ca nirmitasya idantayā parāmarśaḥ svātantryam tu ahaṃparāmarśa rūpam iti nirmitasya tad rūpatva abhāve katham svātantrya āmukta tvam iti tad  etad  parihartum āha svarūpe bhāva pratyayaḥ ādi grahaṇāt  ātma īśvara ādi parāmarśaḥ tiṅgrahaṇam kriyā vāci pratyaya upalakṣaṇam karma grahaṇam asattva bhūta śakti rūpa upalakṣaṇam tad  ayam arthaḥ aham iti evam svarūpaḥ  yaḥ parāmarśaḥ  yaḥ ca īśvaraḥ pramātā ātmā śiva ityādiḥ ananta prakāraḥ parāmarśaḥ tasya yadi api bhedaḥ  anyonya rūpa tā tathā api tad bhedāt hetoḥ asya ātmanaḥ  nirmātṛ rūpasya ahaṃparāmarśa mayasya nirmeya rūpasya ca īśvara ādi parāmarśa āspadasya yaḥ  bhedaḥ śaṅkitaḥ sa na yuktaḥ yata īśvara iti api yaḥ parāmarśaḥ sa īśana śīle jñātṛtva kartṛtva tattve viśrānyati jñātṛtva ādi ca jñāna ādau svātantryam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam avicchinna jñāna yogaḥ avicchedaḥ ca jānāmi karomi iti asmad artha viśrāntiḥ iti asya īśvarasya ātmanaḥ sṛṣṭeḥ sṛjyamānasya ahaṃvimarśanīya tvam eva sṛṣṭeḥ iti vā hetau pañcamī asya īśvarasya yatas  īśvara ādi saṃkalpeṣu api ahaṃpara āmarśana yogyasya eva sṛṣṭiḥ arhe kṛtyaḥ yathā kriyā kāraka samuccaya vikalpa ādi śaktayaḥ yathāsvam tiṅtṛtīya ādi cava ādi prayoga avaseya parāmarśa parama arthāḥ pākaḥ kartā samuccayaḥ  vikalpaḥ ityādi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyamānāḥ sattva bhāvam āpāditā api pacati caitreṇa ca vā iti evaṃrūpe mūla parāmarśe viśrāmyanti anyathā tu tāḥ pratītā na eva bhaveyuḥ tadvat  atra api etad uktam bhavati parāmarśe nāma viśrānti sthānam tad ca pāryantikam eva pāramārthikam tad ca aham iti evaṃrūpam eva madhya viśrānti padam tu yad  vṛkṣa mūla sthānīyam grāma gamane tasya tad apekṣayā sṛṣṭa tvam ucyate iti kaḥ  virodhaḥ anena nīla ādeḥ api idam nīlam iti madhya parāmarśe api mūla parāmarśe aham iti eva viśrānteḥ ātma maya tvam upapāditam eva nīlam idam vedmi iti api hi aham prakāśe iti iyat tattvam yathā uktam idam iti asya ityādi mūḍhaḥ tu nīla ādi vimarśāt eva artha kriyā ādi paritoṣa abhimānī iti nīla ādeḥ svātantrya nirmukta tvam uktam ātma ādau tu tad mūla parāmarśa viśrāntim antareṇa pratīti parisamāptim artha kriyām ca mūḍhaḥ api na abhimanyata iti tasya nirmitau api anujjhita svātantryam uktam nanu evam viśva parāmarśanām aham iti eva viśuddha eka parāmarśa viśrāntiḥ eva tattvam tad  katham idam ucyate jñāna smṛti ādikā asya śaktaya iti jñānasya ca saṃśaya nirṇaya ādi bhedaḥ nīla ādīnām ca vaicitryam iti āśaṅkāyām parihāram āha anupapannam avabhāsanam māyā iti ucyate tatas ca bhinnam prakāśāt  sarvam avabhāsa jātam māyā tatra ca cit tattvasya eva svātantryam māyā śaktiḥ tayā bhinnam yad  saṃvedyam pramātuḥ ca anyonyataḥ ca māyā śaktyā bhinnena pramātuḥ anyonyataḥ  vedyāt ca karaṇa vargeṇa yad  saṃvedyam sa eva gocaraḥ  viśrānti padam yasyāḥ tādṛśī satī sā eva pratyavamarśa ātmā citiḥ parāvāc rūpā jñānam iti saṃkalpa iti adhyavasāya iti ca ucyate ādi grahaṇāt  saṃśayaḥ smṛtiḥ ityādi tathā hi indtriyeṇa sphuṭa grāhiṇā bāhyena viṣayeṇa sphuṭena ca niyantritam saṃvid tattvam tad  jñānam manasā viṣayeṇa ca apshuṭena saṃkalpaḥ buddhyā viṣayeṇa ca viṣayatva paryanta bhājā adhyavasāyaḥ  niścayaḥ viṣayasya ca yad  bhinna tvam bahis antaḥkaraṇānām ca tad prakāśa abhedāt  anupapannam cit tattvena bhāsyate iti bhede yatas  viśrāntiḥ na tu bhedasya abhede īśvara sadāśiva ādivat  tatas  jñāna saṃkalpādayaḥ  bhinnāḥ tasya apradhvasta sva svabhāva abhedasya saṃvid tattvasya anusaṃdhātuḥ śaktaya iti uktāḥ saṃśaya ādayaḥ ca bhinnā nīla ādi vaicitryam ca iti sarvam akhaṇḍitam nanu pratyavamarśa ātma tvam citi śakteḥ saṅkalpa smaraṇa ādi śaktiṣu sacikalpa ātmikāsu bhavatu yā tu nirvikalpa rūpā sākṣātkaraṇa lakṣaṇā anubahva śaktiḥ tatra katham pratyabam arśaḥ  hi abhilāpa viśeṣa yojana āmayaḥ abhilāpa viśeṣa yojanā ca saṅketa smaraṇam apekṣate tad ca saṃskāra prabodham saḥ  api tādṛśdṛśam iti evam prathama samaye katham abhilāpa yogaḥ iti parasya vyāmoham apohitum āha iha tāvat  caitanyasya ātma bhūtaḥ  aṅguli nirdeśa ādi prakhyaḥ abhilāpa yogaḥ anyathā bālasya prathamam vyavahāre dṛśyamāne vyutpattiḥ eva na syāt  nirvikalpaka jñāna paraṃparayā hi tam śabdam śṛṇoti tatas  tam artham puras  paśyati punar tad viviktam bhū talam paśyati iti ghaṭam ānaya naya iti vyavahārāt  katham asya ayam artha iti hṛdi parisphuret  idam ghaṭa iti idam ānaya iti idam naya iti iti yojana aprāṇaḥ  hi ayam arthaḥ yojanā ca vikalpa vyāpāraḥ atra bālā asya prāc janma anubhūta saṅketa smṛteḥ evam tathā api saṅketa kāle sa śabdaḥ  viṣaya tvena idaṃbhāvena pratyavamṛśyamāna tvāt  bhedāt  pracyutya nirbhāsamānaḥ  vijñāna śarīre viśrāntaḥ san vācaka iti bhavati tad  vijñānasya savarūpam ced  bhāti tad  abhilāpa mayam eva iti yathā viṣayasya sukha rūpatva abhāve api jñānam sukha ātmakam bhāti tathā mā bhūt  abhilāpa ātmā rūpa ādiḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api vijñānam tad ātmakam avabhāsiṣyate atra tu darśane viṣayasya api vimarśa maya tvāt  abhilāpa maya tvam eva vastutas  staimitya ādi avasthā api yadi na parāmarśa mayī tarhi asyām vikalpa ātmaka pramātṛ vyāpāra anulāsāt saṃbhavaḥ śapatha parama artha eva smaraṇam ca na syāt  rūpa viṣaya adhyavasāyī hi yadi vikalpa udiyāt  kim anyat  sarva cintā saṃharaṇena staimityam nāma na syāt  iti tatra api asti antar  parāmarśaḥ sakalena ca śabda grāmeṇa śabdanam hi sahante vastūni tatra ca niyata śabda yojanam kriyate tathā hi bālasya puras  puṇḍe sahajaḥ  yaḥ parāmarśaḥ aham iti avicchedena idam iti vicchedena vā tad pṛṣṭhe eva gaura iti gauḥ iti vā śabda āropyate saḥ  api abhyāsāt  pramātṛ mayaḥ  bhavati tad pṛṣṭhe ca anyaḥ śukla iti anyat  balīvarda iti iti evam saṅketa tattvam tasmāt  asti sākṣātkāre pratyavamarśaḥ api śabdasya ayam āśayaḥ iha sākṣātkāraḥ  vastutas  paśyāmi iti evaṃbhūta vikalpana vyāpāra paryanta eva vikalpaḥ  hi pratyakṣasya vyāpāra iti paraḥ  api manyate na ca vyapāraḥ tadvataḥ  bhinnaḥ yuktaḥ tad svarūpa bhūtaḥ  hi saḥ bhavatu vā kṣaṇa mātra svabhāvaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ tatra api asti vimarśaḥ avaśyam ca etad  katham anyathā iti yadi sa na syāt  tad  eka abhisaṃdhānena javāt  gacchan tvaritam ca varkṣān paṭhan drutam ca mantra pustakam vācayan na abhimatam eva gacchet  uccārayet  vācayet  vā tathā hi tasmin deśe jñānam ācikramiṣā ākramaṇam ākrānta tā jñānam prayojana antara anusaṃdhānam tityakṣā deśa antara anusaṃdhiḥ tatra api ācikramiṣā ityādinā yojana viyojana rūpeṇa pratyavamarśena vinā abhimata deśa avāptiḥ katham bhavet  evam tvarita udgrahaṇa vācana ādau mantavyam tatra viśe atas  sthāna karaṇa ākramaṇa ādi yogaḥ atra ca yatas  paścāt bhāvi sthūla vikalpa kalpanā na saṃvedyate tatas  eva tvarita tvam iti sūkṣmeṇa pratyavamarśena saṃvartita śabda bhāvanāmayena bhāvyam eva saṃvartitā hi śabda bhāvanā prasāraṇena vivartyamānā sthūlaḥ  vikalpaḥ yathā idam iti asya prasāraṇā ghaṭaḥ śkla ityādiḥ tasya api pṛthu budhnā udara ākāraḥ śuklatva jāti yukta guṇa samavāyī ityādiḥ dhāvu gati śuddhau iti pāṭhāt  dhāviḥ tvarita gatau sva śakti vaśāt vartata iti bhavatu evam sūkṣmaḥ  vimarśaḥ prakāśa śarīra āveśī yatra tu sthūla tvena vikalpa rūpa tā sphuṭā tatra śabdaḥ  nīla ādivat  eva pṛthak  pratibhāsate nīlam idam iti sa katham prakāśa svarūpāt  apṛthak bhūtaḥ syāt  śabda ātmā ca vimarśaḥ sa ca atra māyā ātmakam bheda pade api prakāśa apṛthak bhūtaḥ  bhavadbhiḥ iṣṭaḥ tad  etad  katham pratipattavyam iti āśaṅkya āha kena etad  uktam ghaṭa iti yaḥ sthūlaḥ śabdaḥ sa prakāśa jīvita svabhāvaḥ  vimarśa iti saḥ api hi sthūlaḥ śabdaḥ  arthavat  pṛthak bhūta eva bhāti tau nāmaka rūpa lakṣaṇau śabda arthau eka rūpa tayā saḥ  ayam iti evaṃrūpa tvena parāmṛśantī adhyavasā yā sā parameśvara śaktiḥ vimarśa rūpā ātmavat eva aham iti anavacchinna tvena bhāti na tu kadācid  idantayā vicchinna tvena bhāti vicchinna tvena avabhāse para pratiṣṭha tvāt  punar vimarśa antareṇa bhāvyam tatra api evam iti anavasthātaḥ  nīlasya prakāśanam eva na syāt  pratiṣṭhā lābha abhāvāt tasmāt  sarva eva vimarśaḥ prakāśāt  avicchinna eva iti adhyavasā iti ātaḥ ca upasarge iti aṅantaḥ striyām nanu evam sarvasya eva jñāna kalāpasya aham iti eva pratiṣṭhāne vedya bhūmi sparśaḥ  na asti vedya bhuvi ca deśa kāla yogaḥ na tu vedaka aṃśe deśa kāla yoga abhāve ca yad  idam jñānām deśa apekṣayā pramātṛ ādi aṃśa apekṣayā ca sa krama tvam lakṣyate tad  katham syāt  krama abhāve ca eka tvam eva vastu tas  bhavet  tatas ca jñāna smṛti ādibhiḥ tadvān parameśvaraḥ iti yad  uktam tad  katham nirvahet  iti āśaṅkām śamayan pūrva uktam upasaṃharati satyam evam akramam eva saṃvid tattvam kintu sva śakti vaśāt bhinna tvena bhāsitāni yāni vedyāni teṣām mūrti bheda kṛtaḥ  yaḥ  dūrādūrava etatyāvaitatyādiḥ deśaḥ kriyā bheda kṛtaḥ ca yaḥ cira śīghra krama ādi rūpaḥ kālaḥ tau anurudhya chāyā mātreṇa abalambya jñāna smaraṇa adhyavasāyānām sva aṃśā iva bhānti niraṃśānām api tad bhāsamāna aṃśa kṛtaḥ ca sa kramatva avabhāsaḥ paraspara apekṣayā sva aṃśa apekṣayā ca yadi api kāla krama eva sphuṭaḥ  vijñāneṣu bhāti na deśa kramaḥ tathā api vimūḍhasya parvata saṃvedanam vitatam iva vadara saṃvedanam ca sūkṣmam iva bhāti iti deśa kramaḥ  api darśitaḥ tena vedya gata krama svīkāra ābhāsāt sa krama tvam ābhāsamānam api na apāramārthikam ābhāsamānasya para artha tvāt  tatas ca yuktam uktam jñānāt ayaḥ  asya bhagavataḥ śaktayaḥ iti māyā śaktyā vibhoḥ iti ślokena svarūpa vaicitryam jñānām darśitam anena tu deśa kāla vaicitryam iti viśeṣaḥ iti śivam iti śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta viracitāyāṃīśvara pratyabhijñā sūtra vimarśinyām prathame jñāna adhikāre jñānaśakti nirūpaṇam nāma pañcama āhnikam atha ṣaṣṭham āhnikam sva ātma abheda dhanān bhāvān  tad apohana ṭaṅkataḥ vhindanyaḥ sva icchayā citra rūpa kṛtam stumaḥ śivaḥ evam smṛti śaktiḥ jñānaśaktiḥ ca nirūpitā atha tad ubhaya anuprāhiṇī apohana śaktiḥ vitatya śloka ekādaśakena aham pratyavam arśaḥ  yaḥ prakāśa ātmā ityādinā siddhe sarvasya jīvataḥ iti antena nirṇīyate tatra ślokena pratyavamarśe avikalpaḥ  viśeṣaḥ iti sūcyate tatas  ślokena śuddhe ahaṃpratyavamarśe apohana vyāpāra asaṃbhavaḥ ucyate tatas  sva dṛṣṭau  eva tad upapattiḥ iti ślokena tatas  api dvayena aśuddhasya aham iti avamarśasya vikalpa rūpa tā tatas  ślokena anusaṃdhānasva api vikalpa rūpa tā evaṃrūpa anusaṃdhāna ādi rūpam eva parameśvarasya sraṣṭṭa tvam iti ślokena tatas  prakṛte cit ātmani artha avabhāsasya sattā upasaṃhiyate ślokena tatas  dvayena tasma eva artha avabhāsasya anubhava smaraṇa ādau vaicitryam ucyate tad uktiḥ ca prakṛtāyām īśvara rūpasva ātma pratyabhijñāyām upayujyate iti ślokena iti āhnikasya tātparya arthaḥ atha grantha arthaḥ  vyākhyāyate uktim idam savabhāvam avabhāsasya vimarśam iti tatra vimarśaḥ  abhilāpa ātmanā śabdena yojita eva tad yojana akṛtam ca vikalpa rūpa tvam śuddhe api parameśvare prāptam na ca etad iṣṭam tasya saṃsāra pade mātha ātmani upapatteḥ iti āśaṅkya āha prakāśasya śuddha saṃvid rūpasya deha ādi saṃsparśaiḥ anāvilībhūtasya yaḥ ātmā jīvita bhūtaḥ sāra svabhāvaḥ  viccheda śūnyaḥ antarabhyupagama kalpaḥ  ananya mukha prekṣitva rūpa svātantrya viśrānti rūpaḥ aham iti pratyavamarśaḥ asau vikalpaḥ  na bhavati vikalpatva āśaṅkāyām bījam darśayati vāc vapuḥ api iti viṣaya rūpāt  śrotra grāhyāt  śabdāt anya eva antar avabhāsamānaḥ saṃvid rūpa āveśī śabdana ātma abhilāpaḥ  vāc iti anena uktaḥ vakti artham svādhyāsena saḥ  ayam iti abhisaṃdhānena yadi vāc vapuḥ kasmāt na vikalpaḥ āha na hi asya vikalpa lakṣaṇam asti tathā hi vividhā kalpanā vividha tvena ca śaṅkitasya kalpaḥ  anvavyavacchedanam vikalpaḥ vividha tvam ca bahnau  anagni saṃbhāvanā samāropanirāse asati bhavat  dvayam vahni avahni rūpam samākṣipati tena vikalpe avaśyam tad ca niścetavyam atat ca apohitavyam bhavati tathā ca ghaṭe hi dṛṣṭe ghaṭa sthāna eva aghaṭe api yogya deśa abhimata sthāna ākramaṇa śīlaḥ  vijñāna janakaḥ sva kāraṇa upanītaḥ saṃbhāvyate paṭa ādi svabhāvaḥ atas  ghaṭāghaṭayoḥ dvaya urava bhāva sasya saṃbhāvanāt  samāropaḥ sa avakāśaḥ  bhavati aghaṭasya sati ārope niṣedhana lakṣaṇa upohana vyāpāraḥ iti tad anuprāṇitā vikalpa rūpa tā ghaṭa iti etasya niścayasya liṅ saṃbhāvanāyām yaḥ tu ayam prakāśaḥ  nāma tasya sthāne yaḥ saṃbhāvyate sa tāvat aprakāśa rūpaḥ  na bhavati tulya kakṣasya hi saṃbhāvanam bhavati na ca yad prakāśena kartavyam tad aprakāśasya kadācid  dṛṣṭam saṃbhāvanā āropaṇa ādi balāt eva ca asya aprakāśa rūpa tvam vighaṭeta atas  prakāśa tulyasya anyasya aprakāśa rūpasya bhedinaḥ tad tulya kakṣyasya apohana ātmaka bhedana vyāpārāsāhiṣṇoḥ avabhāsanam eva na asti tad abhāve kasya apoṣṭhanam avabhāsa saṃbhave api prakāśa rūpa tvam eva na ca prakāśasya sva rūpa deśa kāla bhedaḥ  yena dvitīyaḥ prakāśa ekasmāt apohyeta iti hi iti yasmāt evam tatas  dvaya abhāvāt poha asaṃbhave vikalpa rūpatva abhāvāt cit mātre parāmarśa ātmani aham iti pratyavamarśa eva na tu vikalpaḥ nanu ghaṭe pariniṣthita rūpe dṛṣṭe tad darśanam upajīvatā vikalpena katham aghaṭasya niṣedhanam kriyate na hi aghaṭasya kenacid nāma api gṛhītam aghaṭa vāsanā api ghaṭe dṛṣṭe kathaṃkāram prabudhyatām satyam evam śākyaḥ paryanuyojyaḥ  na tu vayam yatas  iha pramātā nāma pramāṇāt atiriktaḥ pramāsu svatantraḥ saṃyojana viyojana ādi ādhāna vaśāt  kartā darśitaḥ tasya ca pramātuḥ antar  sarva artha avabhāsaḥ cit mātra śarīraḥ  api tad sāmāna adhikaraṇya vṛttiḥ api darpaṇa nagara nyāyena asti iti api uktam evam ca tad pratibhām ghaṭa ābhāsam atad pratibhām ca aghaṭa ābhāsam pramātā bhajate sevate tāvat  tad avikalpa daśāyām cit svabhāvaḥ  asau ghaṭaḥ cidvat eva viśva śarīraḥ pūrṇaḥ na ca tena kaścid vyavahāraḥ tad  māyā vyāpāram ukkāsayan pūrṇam api khaṇḍayati bhāvam tena aghaṭasya ātmanaḥ paṭādeḥ ca apohanam kriyate niṣedhana rūpam tad eva vyapohanam āśritya tasma ghaṭasya niścayanam ucyate ghaṭa eva iti eva arthasya saṃbhāvyamāna apara vastu niṣedha rūpa tvāt eṣa eva paritas chedāt takṣaṇa kalpāt  paricchedaḥ hi iti yata evam tasmāt  yuktam dvayākṣepī vikalpaḥ iti pūrva śloka ultena vastu dvayena hetū krameṇa uktau yasmāt evam vikalpaḥ tatas  aham iti śuddhaḥ  vimarśaḥ na vikalpaḥ iti śloka traye mahā vākya arthaḥ śākyaiḥ api pramātuḥ eva ayam vyāpāra uktaḥ ekaḥ pratyavamarśa ākhyaḥ iti atra prapattā iti svayam iti ca vadadbhiḥ sa tu etaiḥ katham samarthyaḥ iti āḥ tām etad  nanu evam aham iti api pratyavamarśe anahaṃrūpasya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratiyoginaḥ  pohanīyasya apohe vikalpa rūpa tā katham na syāt  iti āśayena āha aham iti avamarśaḥ  dvidhā śuddhaḥ  māyīyaḥ ca tatra śuddhaḥ  yaḥ saṃvid mātre viśva abhinne viśva  chāyā ācchuritāt chā ātmani vā aśuddhaḥ tu vedya rūpe śarīra ādau tatra śuddhe ahaṃpratyavamarśe pratiyogī na kaścid apohitavyaḥ saṃbhavati ghaṭa ādeḥ api prakāśa sāra tvena apratiyogi tvena anapohya tvāt  iti apohya abhāve katham tatra vikalpa rūpa tā aśuddhaḥ tu vedya rūpe śarīra ādau anyasmāt  deha ādeḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ ca vyavacchedena bhavan vikalpa eva iti vākya arthaḥ akṣara arthaḥ tu cit tattvam prakāśa mātra rūpam hitvā sat api apahastanayā apradhānīkṛtya bhinne dehāt ā  aham eva deha ādiḥ nīla ādau prameye pramātā iti abhimānena yaḥ  aham sthūlaḥ ityādi vimarśaḥ sa vikalpa eva na tu śuddham pratyavamarśa mātram atra hetuḥ paraḥ  dvitīyaḥ  deha ādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ ca yaḥ pratiyogī tulya kakṣyaḥ  anyonya parihārāt ca viruddhaḥ tasya yaḥ  avabhāsaḥ samāropaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt yatas  asau  atat niṣedha anuprāṇitaḥ  ham iti avamarśaḥ  jātaḥ aham sthūlaḥ na kṛśaḥ na ghaṭa ādiḥ iti śuddha prakāśa rūpasya apahastana eva deha ādeḥ bheda hetuḥ tad apahastane tu parameśvarasya sva ātma pracchādana icchā rūpā abheda aprakāśanam bhrānti rūpam prati svātantrya rūpā māyā śaktiḥ hetuḥ cit rūpasya cāpahastanam deha ādeḥ eva atyakta vedya bhāvasya bhinnasya eva upapatti śūnyatayā eva pramātṛtva abhimānaḥ tathā ca deha abhimāna bhūmikāyām sthitāḥ cārvākāḥ caitanya viśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ iti kāyam eva prādhānyena āhuḥ strī bāla mūrkhāṇām tathā abhimānāt tatas  api viveka yuktāḥ pākaja utpatti pariṇāma ādi balāt asthiram śarīram manvānāḥ prāṇa śakti samadhiṣṭhānena ca vinā vikāra śata āveśam śarīrasya paśyantaḥ  bubhukṣā pipāsā yoga yogyam prāṇam eva ātmānam kecana śruti anta vidaḥ  manyante tatas  api samadhika viveka bhājaḥ prāṇasya api anitya tvāt anusaṃdhāna yogya tām apaśyantaḥ  jñāna sukha ādi āśraya bhūtām buddhim eva kāṇāda prabhṛtaya ātmānam āhuḥ apare tasyāḥ  api yogidśāyām vedya bhāvāt apara tvam manyamānāḥ asaṃvedya parva rūpam yad na kiṃcid rūpam sakala vedya rāśi vinirmuktam śūnya tvāt nabhaḥ tulyam na tu mahābhūta ākāśa svabhāvam tad  pramātṛ tattvam śūnya brahma vādinaḥ sāṃkhya prabhṛtaya āhuḥ tasmin  api vedye śunyā antaram tatra api śūnya antram iti yāvat bhedaḥ tāvat kalpanā na truṭyati iti tad artham āha kalpite iti na ca anavasthā parama artha prakāśa balena yatas  sarvasya prakāśaḥ  na tu deha ādi vaśāt tayā tu abhimāna mātram dehaḥ pramātā iti saṅkoca mātra rūpam cit tattvam śūnyam bhū talam yathā ghaṭa abhāvaḥ saṅkoca upari vedya aṃśa  chāyā ācchuritam tu cit tattvam eva buddhi prāṇa deha ādi iti amī eva bhūmikā viśeṣā uttarottaram ārohatām yoginām jāgrat āditayā piṇḍa stha ādi tayā ca āgameṣu bhaṇyante apahastanam ca vyākhyāsyateḥ kalā udvalitam etad ca cit tattvam kartṛ tā mayam acit rūpasya śūnya ādeḥ mitam guṇa tayā sthitam iti tad sthitam aśuddhaḥ aham iti avamarśaḥ  vikalpa eva dvividhaḥ  api ca ayam aham pratyayaḥ dvidhā anubhava mātra rūpaḥ ca anusaṃdhāna ātmā ca śiva ātmani aham iti sadāśiva ātmani aham idam iti śuddhaḥ  dvidhā aśuddhaḥ  api aham sthūla iti yaḥ  aham sthūlaḥ  abhavam saḥ  aham kṛśa bālaḥ  yuvā sthaviraḥ sa eva aham iti ca aśuddhaḥ  dvividhaḥ tatra śuddhe vikalpa rūpa tvam apratiṣṭham eva iti uktam aśuddhe tu anubhava rūpe vikalpa tvam upapāditam aśuddhe api tu anusaṃdhāna ātmaka tayā abhedasya prasphuraṇāt  kaścid avikalpaka tvam śaṅketa tasya vyāmoham vyapohitum āha dehe ityādi vartate kādācid kaḥ kadācid bhavaḥ  niyata deśa kāla ākāraḥ  avabhāsaḥ  yasya deha ādeḥ sva lakṣaṇa rūpasya tatra yā pūrva ābhāsena bāla ādi śarīra avabhāsena yojanā yaḥ  aham bālaḥ sa eva adya yuvā iti anusaṃdhānam ādi grahaṇāt uttareṇa bhāvinā ābhāsena saha yojanā sthaviraḥ  bhavitāsmi iti sā yojanā sarvā kalpanā vikalpa eva na tu śuddhaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ atra deha ādeḥ viśeṣaṇam hetutva āśayena yatas  bhinna tā avabhāsi tvam eva deha ādeḥ tadānīm api avichinnam yadi hi tasya deha ādeḥ sarvatas  pūrṇa tvam avaccheda hīna tvam paśyan anusaṃdhānam aham idam iti vidadhyāt  tad iyam sadāśiva bhūḥ kena vikalpāt pada tvena bhaṇyeta yāvatā avicchinne eva saḥ  anusaṃdhiḥ bhinnepi katham anusaṃdhānam iti ced āha saṃskārāt  prāktana anubhava kṛta vāsanā prabodha ja smṛti vaśāt iti yāvat  prāṇe bala abala vaśāt anusaṃdhiḥ buddhau jñāna sukha ādi tāratamyāt  śūnye vaitatya avaitatya yogāt  ayam api vikalpa eva evam sa eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti ghaṭa ādi anusaṃdhāne api vikalpa tvam mantavyam kintu etāsu anusaṃdhāna bhūmiṣu vidyā śaktiḥ ādhikyena acira dyutivat dīpyate iti tāsām para pada pariśīlana prathama kalpa abhyupāya tvam abhyupāgaman guravaḥ na ca deha ādīnām pūrva pūrva pramātṛ vedya tā yena pramātuḥ aprakāśe prameyam na bhāti tad prakāśaḥ ca na pūrva prakāśam vinā saḥ  api na pramātṛ antara prakāśam vinā iti anavasthā syāt  api tu śuddha prakāśa eva viśvasya prakāśa iti nirūpayan ukta yuktyā sadā eva sṛṣṭi ādi śakti aviyogaḥ  bhagavata uktaḥ  bhavati iti darśayati yad  pūrvam darśitam dehe buddhau ityādi tad  evam upapadyate katham yadi vyavahāre māyā pade deha prāṇa ādim api prabhuḥ eva prakāśa parama artha icchayā māyā śakti rūpayā āviśan deha prāṇa ādi prādhānyena svarūpam pradarśayan antar  saṃbinmātre bhāntam aham iti evaṃrūpam artha ogham icchayā eva bahis  idam iti bhāsayati tatas  etad upapadyate anyathā tu anavasthā syāt  hetau liṅ api śabda eva śabdaḥ ca bhinna kramau yad  etāvat  uktam tad iti tasmāt  hetoḥ evam jātam vakṣyamāṇa rūpam kiṃtat  yad  kila prabhuḥ parasparam vyavahāra kāle kraya vikraya prekṣā vyākhyā ādau caitra maitra ādi saṃbandhinaḥ  deha prāṇa ādīn ekatayā tāvati vyavahāre āviśan antar bhāntam eva anujjhita antar prakāśam eva santam bahis  eka ābhāsa tayā bhāsayati iti saṃbhāvyate iti etad jātam iti saṃbhāvanāyām liṅ tena tena pramātrā saha asmin kāle aikyam sṛjyate anyena pramātrā aikyam saṃhriyate ghaṭa ādi mātra rūpe sthitiḥ kriyate pūrṇa svarūpa nimīlanāt  tirobhāva ādhīyate tāvatī ābhāse aikya avabhāsa pūrṇatva vitaraṇāt anugrahaḥ kriyate tena na kevalam mahā sṛṣṭiṣu mahā sthitiṣu mahāpralayeṣu prakopa tirodhāneṣu dīkṣā jñāna ādi anugraheṣu bhagavataḥ krṭya pañcaka yogaḥ yāvat  satatam eva vyavahārepi yad uktam sadā sṛṣṭi vinodāya sadā sthiti sukha asine sadā tribhuvana āhāra tṛptāya svāmine namaḥ iti pratikṣaṇam aviśrāntaḥ trailokyam kalpanā śataiḥ kalpayan  api kaḥ  api ekaḥ nirvikalpaḥ  jayati ajaḥ ityādi ca tathā prākāmyam ātmani yadā prakaṭīkaroṣi vyaktoḥ iti ca iha antar artha abhāva bhāsaḥ sthita eva tad  kim tatra kāraṇa antara cintayā iti prakṛtam prameyam tad siddhaye upapattiḥ uktā tena vinā icchā rūpaḥ pratyavam arśaḥ  na syāt  iti tad prasaṅgāt  pratyavamarśa vikalpa ādi svarūpam upapāditam iti śiṣyāṇām dhiyam samādhātum prakṛtam prameyam upapādayan upasaṃharati prakāśa ātmā parameśvara eva yatas  deha ādi pramātṛ tā abhimāna daśāyām api vastutas  pramātā evam iti atas  hetoḥ idam siddham bhavati smaraṇe apohana jīvite ca vikalpe anubhava jñāne ca antarābhāsaḥ prakāśa viśrāntaḥ sthita eva na atra saṃśayaḥ kaścid  yadi hi deha ādiḥ eva parama artha pramātā syāt  tad  śarīrasya prāṇasya dhiyaḥ śūnyasya vā antar ghaṭa ādi iti na kiṃcid  etad  ghaṭa ādi parihāreṇa deha ādeḥ sthita tvāt  parama artha prakāśaḥ tu sarvaṃsahaḥ iti tatra antar viśvam iti anāyāsa siddham etad  nanu antara ābhāsa vargasya bahis ābhāsanam yadi sarvatra asti kaḥ tarhi smaraṇa ādau ābhāsa bhedaḥ na ca asau na saṃvedyate sphuṭa tā sphuṭa tā ādi prasphuraṇasya anapahnavanīya tvāt  iti āśaṅkya āha anubhava jñānasya idam nīlam iti antar avabhāsam vahirābhāsayataḥ sva antarbhāva ābhāsaḥ  naisargika nisṛṣṭeḥ svātantryāt  āyātaḥ  na tu smaraṇa ādeḥ iva anya jñāna kṛta vāsanā ādi balāt smaraṇe utprekṣaṇe pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvini adhyavasāye ca yaḥ  antar nīla ādi avabhāsaḥ  bāhya tayā adhyavasāyitavyaḥ na asau sva ātmoyaḥ api tu pūrva anubhava saṃskāra jaḥ  asau tatra saṃskāraḥ  nāma anubhavasya kāla antare api anuvartamāna tā atas  asau  anuvartamānaḥ  anubhavaḥ  yatas  nīla ādi ābhāsa saṃbhinnaḥ tatas  tad tādātmya āpannam smaraṇa ādi api tathā nirbhāsate tatas  eva smaraṇa kāla asaṃbhavī ābhāsaḥ tad anubhava pūrva kāla kalita eva iti svayam smaraṇa ādeḥ nirviṣaya tvam gṛhīta grāhi tvam ca uddhoṣyate etad eva asphuṭa tvam iti siddhaḥ  anubhava smaraṇa ādau ābhāsa bhedaḥ antara ābhāsa vargasya bahis ābhāsanam anya avyavadhānena sphuṭa tā vyavadhānena tu tātkālikatva abhāvāt asphuṭa tā iti nanu anubhava jñānāt  aindriyakāt  anyat  sarvam jñānam vyavadhānena bahis ābhāsana rūpam prāptam iti āśaṅkya pravibhāgam āha yaḥ pratyakṣa vyāpāram anupajīvan vyākṣepa sāra tayā manorājya saṅkalpa ādi vikalpaḥ sa svaram kṛtvā sva preraṇena prapreraṇanaiḥ apekṣyeṇa svātantryeṇa carati udeti vyayate ca tatra yaḥ  bahis ābhāsaḥ  nīla ādeḥ antara ābhāsa mayasya sa naisargika eva tathā hi aparidṛṣṭa pūrvam api śvetam daśana śataka lota kara yugala yuktam dantinam antar  pramātṛ bhūmau sthitam bahis  antaḥkaraṇa bhūmau svacchadhī darpaṇa ātmikāyām sa vikalpaḥ tātkālikam eva bhāsayati asmāt ca antara ābhāsa saṃbhava samarthana prasaṅga āgatāt ābhāsa bheda vicārāt śāstre yad  prayoanam mukhya tayā abhisaṃhitam sva ātmani īśvara pratyabhijñāna rūpam tad adhikaraṇa siddhāntanītyā anāyāsa siddham iti darśayati pratibhāti ghaṭaḥ iti yadi api viṣaya upaśliṣṭam eva pratibhānam bhāti tathā api na tad viṣayasya svakam vapuḥ api tu saṃvedanam eva tad  tathā cakāsti mām prati bhāti iti pramātṛ lagna tvāt  tathā ca veda tam eva bhāntam anu bhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti śatrā avirata sphuraṇa tvam karma pravacanīyena tadīya svātantrya upakalpita nirmāṇa kriyā janitaḥ  vedya vedaka bhāva rūpaḥ  lakṣaṇa ātmā saṃbandhaḥ  dyotitaḥ kevalam viṣaya ullekhana balāt bahis  krama avabhāsaḥ samarthitaḥ sa sa krama yaugapadyādi vicitra rūpaḥ  yaḥ padārthānām vakṣyamāṇa īśvara svātantrya rūpa deśa kāla śakti upakalpitaḥ kramaḥ deśa kāla paripāṭī tena rūṣitā pratibimba kalpa tayā uparaktā yā pratibhā uktā kevalam bhinna saṃvedya ityādinā eṣā iti ca sarvasya sva kāśa rūpā paramārthataḥ ca antarmukha tvena prakāśa mātra parama artha tayā bheda abhāvāt akramā sā eva maheśvaraḥ avidyamānaḥ  antar  paricchedaḥ  deśataḥ kālataḥ sva rūpataḥ ca yasyāḥ cittaḥ saṃvidaḥ tad eva rūpam yasya iti ata eva bahirmukha prakāśa ātmaka vijñāna svabhāvasya pramāṇa vargasya yaḥ  antar  pratyābhāsam idam idam iti ananta kalpaḥ vikalpam ayaḥ  vimarśa ātmā pramāsam ūhaḥ tatra saṃyojana viyojana viśrama ādi rūpa aneka prakāra svātantrya paripūrṇaḥ śuddha ahaṃpratyavamarśa mayaḥ pramātā sa bhaṇyate atas ca bahis ghaṭa prakāśaḥ ayam ghaṭaḥ iti antar vikalpaḥ svīkṛta pūrvarūpaḥ aham iti tad ubhaya viśrānti sthānam iti iyat  pūrṇam prakāśasya svarūpam atra eva upapattim pradarśayitum anvayam tāvat āha saṃvid niṣṭhā hi viṣaya vyavasthitayaḥ iti yad  ucyate tad  na bhinna rūpa prakā ātmaka saṃvid mātra viśrāntyā siddhyati api tu tāḥ tā vibhinnāḥ saṃvidaḥ  niścaya rūpāḥ pramā ātmānaḥ  yāḥ tāni eva mukhāni dvārāṇi upāyā mārgāḥ taiḥ mukhaiḥ nadī srotaḥ sthānīyaiḥ yadi amī bhāvā nīla sukha ādaya uhyamānā ekasmin aham iti pramātṛ rūpe mahā saṃvid samudre pratitiṣṭhanti ābhimukhyena viśrāntim bhajante tatas  eṣu parasparam samanvaya rūpam tad  jñātā iyam tad  upapattyā ghaṭate jñātīnām bhāvaḥ tad śabda pravṛtti nimittam parasparam jānīyuḥ iti karma ca anyonya yogakṣema udvahana ātmakam jñātā iyam tad ca samanvaya abhiprāyeṇa iha darśitam na jaḍānām svatas  samanvayaḥ kadācid api iti pratipādayitum tathā ca vyatireka mukhena etad eva āha arthānām jaḍānām tad jñānām tad vikalpānām tad niścayānām ca deśa kramam kāla kramam ca atyajatām sva samāpinām sva rūpa mātra pratiṣṭhānām kaḥ samanvayaḥ na kaścid  iti arthaḥ yatas  hi asau samanvayaḥ sakṛt ābhāsena deśa kāla ākāra miśrīkaraṇa ātmanā yojana ābhāsena sādhayitum śakyaḥ na anyathā na hi pṛthak pṛthak  parikṣīṇeṣu srotaḥsu tad uhyamānāḥ tṛṇa ulapa ādayaḥ samanvayam kaṃcid  yānti iti aneka tvena deśa kāla ādi bheda iti āśayena sakṛt śabdaḥ tad niṣedha tātparyeṇa prayuktaḥ tatra kaḥ  asau samanvaya iti āśaṅkya bahutara vyāpakam kārya kāraṇa bhāvam tāvat  darśayati iha anubhūtaḥ  viṣayaḥ prakāśate smṛtau tatra viṣayasya asau smṛtiḥ na nūtanaḥ prakāśaḥ api tu asya sa prakāśaḥ prācyaḥ  anubhava eva sa ca anubhavaḥ  jñāna rūpa tvena jñeya rūpatva abhāvāt  na jñāna antara saṃvedyaḥ api tu sva prakāśaḥ sa ca smṛti kāle yadi asan tad  katham prakāśatām bhavatu vā asau tathā api smṛtiḥ syāt  tasmāt  etad  evam upapadyate yad eva smṛti sva saṃvedanam tad eva anubhavasya sva saṃvedanam na tu aparam sva saṃvedana vyatiriktam pratyakṣam anumāna ādikam vā tatra kramate tatas ca tāvat kālā api avichinnam ekam yad  sva saṃvedanam tad eva pramātṛt tvam iti siddham anyatra anubhavitari smartā anyaḥ  na upapadyate iti anayā chāyayā smṛtyā pramātṛ siddhiḥ pūrvam uktā idānīm tu sva saṃvedana ekībhāvena bhaṅgi antareṇa iti viśeṣaḥ nanu anubhava atirikte api arthe santu vikalpāḥ pramāṇam aprāmāṇyam hi bādha balāt  bhavati bādha abhāve tad  katham syāt  iti āśaṅkya saḥ  api ayam bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ satya asatya pravibhā janayā viśveṣām vyavahārāṇām jīvita bhūtaḥ  na ekena pramātṛ tattvena vinā ghaṭata iti vitatya darśayati bādha abhāve prāmāṇyam iti etad artham avaśya samarthyaḥ  yaḥ  bādha vyavahāraḥ saḥ  api katham iti api śabdasya arthaḥ iha śuktyā tāvat  rajatasya na kācid  bādhā nāma kriyamāṇā dṛśyate śukti jñānena rajata jñānam bādhyate iti api na yuktam svasmin viṣaye ātmani ca svarūpe dvayoḥ jñānayoḥ pariniṣṭhitayoḥ viśr|antayoḥ anyonyam virodhasya abhāvāt  atha ayam paraspara parihāra eva virodhaḥ tarhi sarveṣām jñānānām virodhāt  bādhya bādhaka bhāvasya sva ātmani pariniṣṭhā eva na labhyā iti sutarām vighaṭeta satyetara pravibhāgaḥ nañapi atra tantreṇa vyākhyeyaḥ etad uktam bhavati yadi jñānam svayam naśyati tadā kim jñāna antareṇa asya kṛtam na hi tena tad kāle asaṃbhava tā tasya viṣaya apahāraḥ kartum śakyaḥ na rājatam iti api jñānam svam rajata abhāvam viṣayīkurvat  na viṣayam apaharet  rajata jñānasya atha api jñāna antareṇa na aśyate iti api pakṣaḥ tatra api sarveṣām jñānām iyam eva saraṇiḥ iti kiṃcid eva bādhyam iti katham syāt  yadā tu rajata jñānam śukti jñānam ca ekatra sva saṃvedane viśrānyataḥ tadā etad  upapadyate tathā hi ekatra api pramātṛ tattve viśrāmyatām jñānānām na eka prakārā eva viśrāntiḥ api tu vicitra tayā eva sā saṃvedyate tathā hi nīlam iti utpalam iti jñāne pramātari viśrāmyantī paraspara uparāga ābhāsena viśrāmyataḥ ghaṭa iti paṭa iti parasparānāśkeṣeṇa śuktikā iti na rajatam iti vā jñānam rajatam iti jñānasya unmūlanam tadīya vimarśa ātmaka pramā rūpa vyāpāra anuvartana vidhvaṃsam kurvat  pramātari pratiṣṭhām bhajate evam kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādau viśrānti vaicitryam prameya asaṃbhavi pramātrā svātantryeṇa nirmitam tatas  eva asya pramāsvatantra tā dāyi vācyam evam ekatra pramātari pūrva jñānasya parivarjanena yatas  niścitā sthitiḥ iti bādhya bādhaka vyavahāra upapannaḥ nīla ādivat  kila tān api vyavahārān sa eva parameśvaraḥ svātantryāt  ābhāsayati tad  te api satyā eva iti atra parakīyam matam āśaṅkate dūṣayiṣyāmi iti iha śuktikā jñānam sva ātmānam saṃvidat  sva ātma abhinnam pramāṇa tvam budhyate tad paricchinatti iti nyāyāt  tad paricchedana āntarīyakaḥ ca anya vyavaccheda iti aśukti jñāna rūpasya rajata jñānasya apramāṇatva vedanam tad eva ucyate yad  etad  śuktikā saṃvedanā bhinna pramāṇatva vedanam na ca etad  apūrvam yad  vastu antara jñānam eva vastu antara abhāva jñānam iti śuddha bhū bhāga grahaṇam eva hi ghaṭa abhāva grahaṇam iti prasiddham etad  evam apramāṇatva saṃvedanam eva rajata jñānasya bādhya tvam ucyate atas ca bādhya bādhaka tvam evam siddham iti ced  asmābhiḥ ucyate tad  kim pramātra aikyena iti atra prasaṅgāt  abhāva vyavahārasya siddhau tattvam upapādayiṣyan dṛṣṭāntam eva tāvat  para darśane dūṣayati yaḥ  dṛṣṭānta uktaḥ sa eva na kuta iti ced  ucyate iha bhū talam na ghaṭaḥ iti tādātmyena abhāvaḥ  vyavahartavyaḥ kadācid  kadācid  vyatirekeṇa iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ  na iti tatra śuddha bhū tala jñānāt  ādyaḥ  ayam vyavahāraḥ sidhyati yatra dṛśya tvam na upayogi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ api hi yasya na asti piśāca ādeḥ svabhāva balāt  yasya vā śabda ādeḥ tad gāhaka śrotra ādi sāmagrī sākalyasya tatra eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antara pratipatti abhāvena aniścayāt  tasya api tādātmyena ayam abhāvaḥ  gṛhyate bhū talam na piśācaḥ  na śabdaḥ iti yatra tu dṛśya tvam viśeṣaṇam avaśyam apayogi tatra vyatirekeṇa abhāve vyavahartavye na eṣaḥ  abhyupāyaḥ kuta iti ced  atiaprasaṅgāt iti brūmaḥ tam eva darśayati vidyamāne api ghaṭe bhū talam śuddham eva na hi bhāvā miśrībhavanti tatas ca tadā api śuddha bhū tala jñānam asti iti sati api ghaṭe katham abhāvaḥ  vyatirekeṇa na vyavahriyate atra bhū tale ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti tad jñānam iti vivikta bhū tala bhāga jñānam jātu iti kasyāṃcid eva daśāyām ghaṭa asaṃnidhāna rūpāyām bhinnasya ghaṭasya abhāvam sādhayati na tu sarvadā iti kena prakāreṇa bhavet  etena atra bhū tale piśācaḥ  na asti iti api syāt iti āpatitam mantavyam nanu evam vyatireka abhāva niṣṭhaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  loke tāvat  avigītaḥ asyāṃcid eva daśāyām dṛṣṭaḥ tatra kā gatiḥ iti āśaṅkya cirantanaiḥ aparidṛṣṭam tad siddhi prakāram darśayati iha bhāva eva bhāva antarasya abhāva iti vyavahartavyaḥ iti ayam tāvat  aparityājyaḥ prātītikaḥ panthāḥ tatra bhāvasya bhāva antareṇa ya ādhārya ādhāra bhāvaḥ sa eva bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ tatas ca bhū tale ghaṭa vyatiriktam vastu antaram śilā ādikam āloka puñja ādikam vā yad  cākṣuṣe jñāne bhāti tad eva vyavahriyate bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvaḥ bhū tale ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti vā yatra api na asti cakṣuḥ vyāpāraḥ  netra nimīlana saṃtama sādau tatra api bhū tale ghaṭa ucita kaṭhina sparśa viviktam mṛdum uṣṇam śītam anuṣṇa aśītam vā gṛhṇan tam eva atra ghaṭa abhāva iti vyavaharati vāyu sparśasya sarvagasya avaśyaṃbhāvāt  iti vākya arthaḥ padārthaḥ tu kim tu iti sva mata upakṣepāya sva pratibhā praśna parāmarśaḥ kim punar atra nyāyyam iti tatra āha tatra bhū tale āloka cayaḥ tāvat  asti jñeyaḥ andhasya uṣṇa ādikaḥ sparśaḥ asti tasya āloka cayasya sparśasya vā yad  sva jñānam anya ghaṭa ādi viviktena svena rūpeṇa jñānam tad  kartṛ  tasya āloka ādeḥ aghaṭa rūpa tām ghaṭa abhāva rūpa tām tatra bhū tale sādhayati iti śakyaḥ  yam arthaḥ śaki liṅ ca iti liṅ āntara prāṇa spandana janita sūkṣma śabda ākarṇanāt ca śrotra ādi sākalyam saṃbhavāyamānaḥ tam eva śabdam eka jñāna saṃsargiṇam śṛṇvan śabda antaram niṣedhayati na iha anyaḥ śabdaḥ iti tad sūkṣma śabda abhāvam api sūkṣmatama antar nāda avahita śrotraḥ  vedayate rasa gandha sparśa abhāvaḥ  api danta udaka rasam tri puṭikā gandham kāyīyam ca sparśam saṃvedayamānena eva rasa abhāvaḥ  vedyaḥ na hi eka jñāna saṃsarga yogya vastu antara upalambhena vinā upalabdhi kāraṇa sākalya niścayaḥ  asti iti ekānta eṣaḥ acira pravṛtta tad tad viṣaya anubhava kalpitasya tadā eva dhvaṃsānāśaṅkanāt karaṇasya kāraṇa sākalya niścayaḥ kim eka jñāna saṃsargi tayā iti ced  na tattva bhāva upalipsuḥ hi prayatnena tad tad indriya adhiṣṭhānam vyāpārayan  eva lakṣyate nanu evam adṛśya asya api piśāca ādeḥ niṣedha vyavahāraḥ  vyatirekeṇa api prāpnoti sa hi ālokapuñjaḥ  yathā ghaṭāt  anyaḥ tadvat  piśāca ādeḥ api tad etad āśaṅkya āha ālokapuñjaḥ  yadi api piśācāt  vyatiriktaḥ  yadi api ca ālokaḥ  asti api śāca ātmā iti etāvat  siddhyati tathā api atra piśācaḥ  na asti iti etad  aśakyam adhyavasātum ghaṭaḥ  hi ālokapūra madhye api asaṃbhāvyaḥ ghaṭa saṃnidhau tatra ālokapūrā samarpaṇāt  atas ca siddhi ati idam atra ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti piśācaḥ tu tādṛś svabhāvaḥ  yaḥ  bhū tala madhye āloka madhye api vā bhavan bhū talasya ālokasya vā tām nibiḍa tām na vihanti tatas ca āloka madhye tasya saṃbhāvanāt  katham vyatirekeṇa niṣedha vyavahāraḥ evam rūpa madhye rasa ādeḥ saṃbhāvanāt  tasya api aniṣedhaḥ yadi api anālokaḥ ālokāt  anyaḥ piśācaḥ tathā api asau bhū talasya antar madhye adṛśyaḥ  bhavati iti saṃbhāvyate yathā tadvat eva ālokasya abhyantarepi saḥ asti iti saṃbhāvyata eva tatas ca yadi api ālokaḥ tatas  anyaḥ iti anena pathā niṣiddhaḥ piśācaḥ tathā api sarva prakāreṇa na niṣiddhaḥ iti tad abhāva nibandhanāḥ katham tatra vyavahārāḥ pravartantām iti śloka arthaḥ evam prasaṅgāt  abhāva vyavahārasya tattvam upadarśya prakṛte yojayati yathā ālokaḥ  ghaṭa abhāva iti āloke gṛhīte prāk  gṛhītasya ghaṭasya na kiṃcid  āyātam tathā eva śukti jñānam rūpya jñāna abhāva iti iyat  saṃbhāvyate yathā ghaṭa jñānam ghaṭa jñāna prāmāṇya saṃvid  paṭa jñāna abhāvaḥ paṭa jñāna abhāva prāmāṇya saṃvid  iyatā ca na pūrva pravṛttam paṭa jñānam apramāṇībhavati eṣā hi tasya ghaṭa jñānasya svarūpa cintā sarvā na jñāna antarasya ādyasya kim api atas  jātam evam śuktiḥ iyam iti na rajatam idam iti ca jñānam eva sva ātmanā prakāśatām aham śuktau rajata abhāve ca pramāṇam na tu rajate iti tāvatā tu prāktanasya rajata jñānasya na kiṃcid  vṛttam iti tad viṣayīkṛtam rajatam katham asatyam syāt  nanu idam iti anena tad eva parāmṛśyate yatra rajata jñānam abhūt  tatra eva idānīm na rajatam iti śuktiḥ iti ca jñānam pramāṇa bhūtam jātam tad  atas  anumīyate tad  prācyam rajata jñānam apramāṇam iti na hi etad  saṃbhavati viruddha viṣaya dvaya avagāhi jñāna dvayam pramāṇam ekatra viṣayībhavati iti tad ayam ānumānikaḥ  bādha vyavahāraḥ  bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkya āha na kevalam sva saṃvedanāt  na siddhyati bādhā yāvat  anumānataḥ  api na siddhyati dharmiṇaḥ  asiddheḥ api śabdāt  hetoḥ vyāpteḥ ca apiḥ ubhayatra neyaḥ iha dharmiṇi siddhe siddhena hetunā smaryamāṇa vyāptikena sādhya dharma ayoga vyavacchedaḥ  anumāna vyāpāraḥ iha ca prācye rūpya jñāne dharmiṇi aprāmāṇyam sādhyaḥ  dharmaḥ tatra śuktikā jñānam vā na rajatam iti jñānam vā tad jñāna viṣayī kārya tvam vā viṣaya gatam hetūkriyeta na ca etad  yuktam tad kāle prācya rūpya bodhasya dharmiṇaḥ  abhāvāt  na ca api tasya śukti jñānāt ayaḥ  dharmāḥ na ca apakṣa dharmāt  sādhya siddhiḥ atas  smaryamāṇam tad dharmi syāt  iti api asat  atha śuktiḥ na rajata jñānasya viṣaya iti sādhyate śuktikā jñāna viṣaya tvāt iti tad  yadi idānīm tadā siddha sādhanam atha pūrvam tadā tad pūrva sva saṃvedanena bādhya viṣaya tā kena ca evam vyāptiḥ gṛhītā yatra idānīm anyat  jñānam tatra pūrvam anyat  na bhavati iti anumā anantareṇa iti ced  ananvasthā etena etad  pratyuktam ekasmin viṣaye katham jñāna dvayam syāt  iti kaḥ  hi eka viṣaya tām tayoḥ jñānayoḥ jānīyāt  te hi tāvat  sva ātmani sva viṣaye ca viśrāmyate iti uktam iti anumānataḥ  api na bādhā na ca tathābhūtam api vyavadhānam atra pratītau saṃvedyate sva saṃvedana siddha tayā jhaṭiti bhāsanāt  ata eva etad api aśakyam vaktum mā bhūt  bādhā nāma iti evam para pakṣe anupapattim pradarśya sva pakṣe eka pramātṛ pariniṣṭhiteḥ udiyāt  bādhya bādhaka bhāva iti vākyena pratijñātam nigamayati yuktā sā ekasmāt  pramātuḥ yadi jāyeta iti sa eva hi tathā nirmātā iti vyākhyātam eva sthite ca evam yadi vyavahāra siddhaye anyathā anupapattiḥ api ucyate tad  ucyatām kāmam adhunā sarvam siddhyati iti na kevalam ete kārya kāraṇa bhāva smaraṇa bādhā vyavahārāḥ sakala loka yātrā sāmānya vyavahāra bhūtā eka pramātṛ pratiṣṭhāḥ yāvat  avāntara vyavahārā api ye kraya vikraya ādayaḥ sa malāḥ upadeśya upadeśa bhāva ādayaḥ ca nirmalāḥ tepi eka pramātṛ niṣṭhā eva bhavanti vyavahārā hi sarve samanvaya prāṇāḥ iti upasaṃhāra krameṇa darśayati tad tad vibhinna iti śloka dvaya uktena anena upapatti prakāreṇa anvaya vyatireka ātmanā tathā śloka antaraiḥ uktena vyavahāra udāharaṇa prakāreṇa idam api mantavyam yad  vibhau deśa kālān avacchinne ata eva atyartha bhinnaiḥ māyā balāt bheda eka prāṇitaiḥ nīla sukha ādi ābhāsaiḥ pratibimba kalpaiḥ anatirikta tayā vartamānaiḥ khacite svarūpa ananyathā bhāvena uparakte viśrāntaḥ sarvaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  anubhūyate anubhava eva atra dṛḍhatamam pramāṇam iti yāvat  anubhūyate ca sa upadeśaiḥ avadhāna paraiḥ yena eṣām yā eva saṃsāra daśāsaṃmatā vyavahāra daśā sā eva pramātṛ tattva prakhyā ātmikā śiva bhūmiḥ yad uktam saṃbandhe sāvadhāna tā iti apratyabhijñāta ātma parama arthānām samalaḥ  vyavahāraḥ anyeṣām sa eva nirmalaḥ iti śivam āditas  iti śrīmat māheśvara ācārya varya utpala deva pāda virati tāyām īśvara pratyabhijñāyām śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta kṛta vimarśinī ākhya vyākhyā upetāyām prathame jñāna adhikāre eka āśraya nirūpaṇam nāma saptamam āhnikam atha jñāna adhikāre māheśvarya nirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭamam āhnikam prārabhyate sva saṃvedana saṃsiddha vyavahāra vaśena yaḥ nityam maheśvaraḥ siddhaḥ siddhānām tam stumaḥ śivam evam jñāna smaraṇa apohanāni vyutpādya eṣām ekam āśrayam vinā vyavahāraḥ  na yuktaḥ iti nirūpitam etāvatā na ced antar  kṛtā iti atra yad  uktam ekaḥ iti tad  parighaṭitam antara ābhāsa samarthanena antar kṛta ananta viśva rūpaḥ iti api nirūpitam yad atra eva maheśvaraḥ iti uktam tad māheśvaryam svātantrya rūpam upapādayitavyam tad ca jñāna viṣayam kriyā viṣayam ca iti ubhaya prakāram tatra yatas  bhagavān jñātā kartā ca yadi api ca prakāśa vimarśa ātmakam cit eka ghanam ekam eva saṃvid rūpam tathā api vyutpādanāya tad parighaṭita eva ayam vibhāgaḥ tena jñāna ātmaka kriyā viṣayam svātantryam yadi api kriyāśakti rūpam tathā api tad  jñāna adhikāra eva nirṇetavyam tad viṣaya tvāt evam ca jñātṛ śabda arthaḥ prakṛtitaḥ pratyayataḥ ca saṃpūrṇa tayā nirṇītaḥ  bhavati tatra jñānam nāma svayaṃbhedita ābhāsa bheda upāśraya niyantraṇa asaṃkucitam aham iti saṃvedanam tatra ābhāseṣu yad  svātantryam tad eva jñāna śakti viṣayam svātantryam saṃpadyate iti tātkālikā akṣasāmakṣya ityādinā śuddhe jñāna kriye yatas  iti antena śloka ekādaśakena tad  nirūpyate tatra abhāsa antara apekṣī ca ābhāsaḥ  anyathā vā iti ślokena uktvā sa eva ābhāsa eka iti śloka antareṇa ucyate artha kriyā ābhāsaḥ  api tathā eva ābhāsa niyata iti śloka dvayena uktvā kasmin ābhāse sā artha kriyā iti punar  śloka dvayena ābhāsa antara vicitrita ābhāsa bhitti sthānīyam āntara tvam iti ślokena tatas  bāhya tvam svarūpataḥ  vibhāgataśva iti śloka yugmena tatas  ślokena jñāna ādi śakti āśrayasya ekasya upasaṃhāraḥ śloka antareṇa maheśvara tvam upasaṃhara tā bhāvinaḥ kriyā adhikārasya upakṣepa iti saṅkṣepa artha āhnikasya atha śloka arthaḥ  nirūpyate nanu yadi parameśvara niṣṭhatayā eva samastaḥ  ayam vyavahāraḥ tad  asya sphuṭatva asphuṭatva prāya prasiddha vaicitrya anupapattiḥ yena kila ayam anuprāṇitaḥ sa eka eva bhagavān na ca tad vyatirekeṇa vyavahārasya nijam kiṃcana tattvam utpaśyāma iti āśaṅkya āha kevalam etāvatā ābhāsānām bhedaḥ  na punar artha avabhāsasya sva ātma gataḥ kvacid api bheda iti śloka dvayasya saṃmelitasya saṃbandhaḥ yasmin  eva kāle sa ābhāsa ābhāti tad kāle eva bhavati yad  akṣa sāmakṣyam bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvam nāma ābhāsa antaram paśyāmi iti evaṃrūpam tad sāpekṣāḥ tad vyāmiśrāḥ kvacid  ābhāsā bhavanti yatra sphuṭa tā vyavahāraḥ andha viṣayaḥ andhakāra stha pramātṛ viṣayaḥ punar  yaḥ  anyaḥ  vyavahāraḥ sphuṭa tāmayaḥ tatra te ābhāsā anyathā tathā hi jāti andhasya bāhya indriya pratyakṣatva lakṣaṇam ābhāsa antaram na eva asti dṛṣṭavataḥ tu andhībhūtasya saṃtamasa shtitasya ca tātkālikam tad  na asti api tu prāktanam eva bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvam anusaṃdhatte tasmāt  artha avabhāsasya keṣucid api vikalpeṣu sattāyām svarūpe viśeṣaḥ  asti iti saṃbhāvanā na kartavyā te hi vikalpā bhāvivaḥ tu gāminaḥ  vā bhaviṣyat niṣṭhā vā bhavantu avrtamāna niṣṭhā vā atīta vastu viśrāntā vā etad uktam bhavati nīlam idam paśyāmi saṅkalpayāmi utprekṣe smarāmi karomi vacmi iti ādau nīla ābhāsaḥ  asau svarūpataḥ  anūna adhikaḥ evam paśyāmi iti api yaḥ pīta ādiṣu te punar ābhāsāḥ svātantryeṇa yadā bhagavatā saṃyojyante viyojyante ca tadā ayam sphuṭatva ādiḥ vyavahāraḥ nīlam iti ābhāsasya utprekṣe iti ādi ābhāsa antara vyavacchedanena paśyāmi iti ābhāsa vyāmiśraṇāyām sphuṭa tā vyavahāraḥ evam traikālika vyavahāra vaicitrya upapattiḥ parameśvara svarūpa antarbhūta tve punar ābhāsānām na kutaścid  vyavacchedaḥ na kenacid  vyāmiśraṇā iti nanu etad  nīla ādiṣu upapadyatām yatra bāhya indriya vyāpāraḥ  asti sukha ādau tu tad abhāvāt katham vaicitryam iti āśaṅkya āha sukhe sraj candana ādike ca tad kāraṇe duḥkhe ahikaṇṭaka ādau ca tad hetau atīte anāgate vā yadi api ābhāsaḥ sa eva tathā api atītam idam anāgatam idam iti ābhāsa antareṇa yatas  vyāmiśraṇā anubhavāmi iti ābhāsāt ca yatas  vyavacchedaḥ tena vidyamāneṣu api teṣu tasya pramātuḥ tena prakāreṇa sthitiḥ na bhavati yathā pūrvan abhūt  aham adhunā sukhaḥ  duḥkhī iti samarjita tad tad nimita sāmagrīkaḥ  vā iti yadā tu vikalpena tāni vastūni bāḍham ullikhati tadā paunaḥpunya viśiṣṭa sukha tad hetu ullekhana abhidhāna kāraṇa ābhāsa anupraveśāt ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇa ātmanā tena eva asmad uktena prakāreṇa na punar anyena tathā iti sukhī aham iti ādikena sthitiḥ bhavati iti saṃbhāvyam ucitam etad  yatas tadānīm sphuṭatva ābhāsa miśram sukha ābhāsam upalakṣayati asau atīta grahaṇam bhāvinaḥ  api upalakṣaṇam nanu iyatā kim uktam bhavati bāhya rūpāḥ sraj ādayaḥ sukha ādi hetavaḥ  bāhya janitāḥ ca sukha ādayaḥ sukhī aham iti abhimāna hetavaḥ iti tatas ca bāhyatva abhāve tad janyatva abhāve ca na tathā uktam syāt  tatra ca ta eva na kecid  tatas ca katham uktam artha avabhāsasya sattāyām na kvāpi viśeṣa iti sattāyā eva abhāvāt  iti āśaṅkya āha iha sukham asti mama duḥkham na asti mama iti ye bhāva ābhāsā abhāva ābhāsāḥ ca teṣām bāhya tvam nāma ātmā svarūpam na bhavati na hi sukham iti asya svarūpam bāhyam iti vapuṣā bhāti sukhasya hi sukham eva svarūpam kevalam bāhya tvam nāma abhāsa antaram īśvareṇa svātantrya balāt eva yadā tatra sukha ābhāse miśratayā bhāsyate tadā tad  tasya upādhi rūpa tām uparañcaka tām viśeṣaṇa tvam gacchati tatas ca yathā nīla ābhāsa abhāve utpala ābhāsasya na kiṃcid  vṛttam svarūpataḥ  rāja ābhāsa abhāve vā puruṣa ābhāsasya tathā bāhyatva ābhāsa abhāve api sukha ābhāsasya duḥkha abhāva ābhāsasya kānta ābhāsasya ca na svarūpataḥ kācana mlānatā iti āntarāṇām sadā eva sthitiḥ eṣām iha antaḥkaraṇe buddhi darpaṇa ātmani nīla ādīnām avabhāsānām āntara tvam api asti antaḥkaraṇa madhyebhava tvāt  bāhya tvam api grāhyatā rūpam pramātuḥ vicchedena avabhāsāt  bāhya tvam ca kevalam bāhya pratyakṣa tā atra ca avasthā dvaye api arthakriyām amī kurvanti eva antatas  jñānam sva viṣayam yad  punar  pramātṛ tādātmya lakṣaṇam āntara tvam tatra amī katham na kāṃcid  artha kriyām vidadhīran iti āśaṅkya āha pramātṛ aikye iti tad nimittakam yad  ānantara tvam tasmāt hetoḥ eṣām ābhāsānām artha kriyā na kācid  asti sā hi artha kriyā bhede sati bhavati sa hi nīla ābhāsaḥ pīta ābhāsāt yatas  bhidyate yatas ca pramātuḥ bhidyate tatas  svena sādhyām bhinnam artha kriyām tasya pramātuḥ kuryāt  na ca eṣa tadā bhede asti pramātra aikyāt  sā hi artha kriyā ābhāsa bheda niyatā tathā ca kānta ābhāsasya bāhya tve api sati ābhāsa antarasya āliṅgana lakṣaṇasya vyapagame dūrībhavati iyam iti ca ābhāsa antarasya upagame anyā eva prāktana āhlāda viparītā dṛśyate artha kriyā ata ābhāsa bheda abhāvaḥ yatas  pramātra aikya kṛte āntara tve tasmāt  na artha kriyā iti artha kriyā ābhāsaḥ  api ca ābhāsa antaram eva iti artha kriyā kāritvam api na bhāvānām sattvam yena tad abhāve svarūpataḥ  abhāvaḥ syāt  nanu ca bāhya ābhāsa vyatibhedana kāle āntara ābhāsaḥ  virodhāt  vicchinna iti katham idam uktam āntarāṇām ya ābhāsaḥ sa sadā iti etad  pariharati iha avabhāsānām sadā eva bāhya tā ābhāsa tada bhāvayoḥ api antar ā iva pramātṛ prakāśa eva sthitiḥ yata ete cit mayāḥ anyathā na eva prakāśeran iti uktam yatas  yadā tu māyā śaktyā viccheda avabhāsana svātantrya rūpayā bāhya tvam eṣām ābhāsyate tadā tad  avalambya avabhāsamānānām asau sthitiḥ bahis api antar api na ayam antarābhāsaḥ  bāhya tvasya virodhaḥ  pratyuta sarva ābhāsa bhitti bhūtaḥ  asau tad  katham virodhaḥ iti yuktam uktam sadā eva āntarāṇām sattā iti nanu bāhya tve sati artha kriyā tad ca bāhya indriya gamya tvam na ca vikalpa ullikhitānām tad  saṃbhavati tad  katham amīṣām artha kriyā syāt  dṛśyate ca vikalpa ullikhitaḥ piśāca ādiḥ trāsa ādi vidhāyī iti āśaṅkya āha vimarśa viśeṣa rūpe vikalpa jñāne ya ullikhyamānaḥ kāntā caura ādiḥ arthaḥ sā upi bāhyaḥ na kevalam bahis avalokyamānaḥ yasmāt  saḥ  api pramātuḥ sakāśāt  pṛthak eva prathate ayam iti yad ca pramātari aham iti eva viśrānta tvam tad  āntara tvam antar iti nikaṭam tad ca kiṃcid  apekṣya apekṣaṇīyaḥ ca sarvatra pramātā eva apekṣaṇīya antaraa abhāve tatas ca pramātari nikaṭam tādātmya prāptam eva iti tatas  yad  bhinnam tad  bāhyam eva iti yuktā ullekhasya api artha kriyā nanu kumbhakāra ādi vyāpāreṇa ghaṭa ādeḥ astu bāhya tvam antaḥkaraṇa gocarasya tu kim kṛtam tad  iti āśaṅkya āha antar vikalpa pratibimbatasya nīla ādeḥ yaḥ  bahis ātmanā pramātṛ vicchinnena svabhāvena prakāśaḥ sa bhartuḥ antara ābhāsān bibhrataḥ  bahis  sṛṣṭim ca puṣṇataḥ īśvarasya eva icchayā yathā eva cakṣuḥ ādi viṣaya bhūtānām pratyakṣa jñāna śabda vācyaḥ  bāhya ātmanā prakāśaḥ  nīla ādīnām etad uktam bhavati kumbhakāra vyāpāraḥ  nāma paramārthataḥ īśvara icchā eva tad abhāsita kāya spanda paryantā na punar anyaḥ kaścana saḥ tatas ca tathā īśvara icchayā prakāśāt  avahiḥ bhūtā api nīla ādyā bāhya karaṇa gocarībhūtāḥ kalpitāt  pramātuḥ vicchinna rūpa tvena bāhya tvena bhāsante tathā antaḥkaraṇa gocarībhūtā api iti kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sukha duḥkha prāyāḥ tu bharata ādi ukta rūpāḥ sthāyi vī abhicāri rūpā riti nirvedāt ayaḥ  antaḥkaraṇa eka gocarībhūtā bahis ātmanā bhānti saṅkalpeṣu yadi api kṣetra jhñasya eva svātantryam tathā api cit param ārtha tāyā nyagbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt  īśvarasya eva tad  vastutas  yathā uktam grantha kṛtā eva yadi api artha sthitiḥ prāṇa puryaṣṭaka niyantrite jīve niruddhā tatra api parama ātmani sā sthitā tad ātmanā eva tasya syāt katham prāṇena yantraṇā iti yatra tu anicchoḥ eva kṣetrajñasya svarasa vāhi vyākṣepa sārā sāṅkalpikī sṛṣṭiḥ tatra sphuṭaḥ īśvarasya eva vyāpāraḥ tasmāt  sa aṅkalpikānām api bahis bhāve parameśvara it chiava hetuḥ iti siddhāntaḥ adhunā pūrva uktam aikyam māheśvaryam ca nigamayati yad  etad  pūrva uktena granthena upapāditam tad  iti tasmāt  hetoḥ saṃvidām jñānām aikyena vinā loka paddhatiḥ loka mārgaḥ sarvaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  na saṃbhavet  saṃbhavati ca ayam tasmāt  aikyam āsām na ca etad  durghaṭam yatas  viṣaya prakāśa eva saṃvid  ucyate kevalam viṣaya uparāga mahmnā bahirmukha tayā nīla prakāśaḥ  anyaḥ pīta prakāśaḥ ca anyaḥ pramārthataḥ tu prakāśasya deśa kāla ākāra saṅkoca vaikalyāt eka tvam eva iti eka eva prakāśaḥ antar viśrāntaḥ sa eva ca pramātā ucyate iti sthitam idānīm upapattitaḥ na ca asya asau prakāśa lakṣaṇaḥ sva ātmā nīla ādi uparāgaḥ ca parāmarśan śūnya eva āste sphaṭikrama eḥ iva api tu sadā eva vimṛśyamāna rūpaḥ iti vimṛśat rūpa tvam anavacchinna vimarśatā ananya unmukha tvam ānanda eka ghana tvam tad eva asya māheśvaryam sa eva hi ahaṃbhāva ātmā vimarśaḥ  devasya krīḍā ādi mayasya śuddhe pāramārthikyau jñāna kriye prakāśa rūpa tā jñānam tatra eva svātantrya ātmā vimarśaḥ kriyā vimarśaḥ ca antar kṛta prakāśaḥ iti vimarśa eva para avasthāyām jñāna kriye parāpara avasthāyām tu bhagavat sadāśiva bhuvi idantā sāmāna adhikaraṇyā āpanna āhatā vimarśa svabhāve apara avasthāyām ca māyā pade idaṃbhāva prādhānyena vartamāne iti viśeṣaḥ sarvathā tu vimarśa eva jñānam tena vinā hi jaḍa bhāvaḥ  asya syāt  iti uktam sa eva ca kriyā iti bhāvinaḥ kriyā adhikārasya upakṣepam karoti iti śivam āditas  iti śrīmat māheśvara ācārya varya utpala deva pāda viracitāyām īśvara pratyabhijñāyām śrīmat ācārya abhinavagupta kṛta vimarśinī ākhya vyākhyā upetāyām māheśvaryanirūpaṇa ākhyam aṣṭamam āhnikam prathamaḥ  jñāna adhikāraḥ ca samāptaḥ atha īśvara pratyabhijñāyāḥ kriyā adhikāra ākhyaḥ dvitīyaḥ adhikāraḥ vitata viśadasva ātma ādarśe sva śakti rasa ujjvalām prakaṭayati yaḥ  mātṛ sva aṃśa prameya taṭa dvaye bahutara bhavat bhaṅgī bhūmim kriyā saritam parām prakaṭayatu naḥ śrīmān gaurīpatiḥ sa ṛtam param yatra viśrāntim āsādya citram krīḍā vijṛmbhitam kriyā śaktiḥ iyā atyantam darśayet tam stumaḥ śivam atha kriyā śakti svarūpam vitasya nirṇetum adhikāra antaram ārabhyate tatra śloka aṣṭakena ata eva ityādinā yad avabhāsyate iti antena parameśvare paramārthataḥ akramā kriyā parimita sāṃsārika pramātṛ krama avabhāsana yogāt  sa kramā api ca iti upapādyate tathā hi ślokena ukta pūrva pakṣa pratikṣepaḥ tatas  ślokena sa kramatva akramatva vivekaḥ tatas  śloka trayeṇa krama svarūpa nirūpaṇam tatas  śloka dvayena sakramatva ākrama tvayoḥ viṣaya vibhāgaḥ viṣaya vibhāge ca sati vastutas  ekatra eva tayoḥ viśrāntiḥ iti ślokena nirūpyate iti tātparyam āhnikasya atha śloka arthaḥ  vibhajyate tatra pūrva ukte jñāna śakti samarthana upayoga nimeye siddhe prameya antaram api ayatnataḥ siddham iti adhikaraṇa siddhānta diśā darśayati yad  tāvat  uktam jñānāni eva anubhava vikalpa rūpa ādi bhinnāni na teṣām āśrayaḥ  asti kaścid  saṃskārāt ca smṛtiḥ siddhā jñānam ca jaḍam ced  na arthasya prakāśaḥ ajaḍam ced  deśa kāla saṃkoca vaikalyāt  ātma tattvāt  abhinnam iti tad  tāvat  pratikṣiptam bhinnānām anubhava ādīnām anupapatteḥ vitatya darśita tvāt  na ca saṃskāra mātrāt smṛtiḥ iti etad api uktam ajaḍam eva ca asaṃkucita rūpam jñānam tad svātantrya avabhāsita jñeya uparāga vaśāt  tu tasya saṃkoca avabhāsa iti api darśitam yatas  na kevalam atas  hetu kalāpāt  jñāna śakti codyāni nidāritāni yāvat  kriyāśakti viṣayāṇi api dūṣaṇāni ata eva hetu kalāpāt  apasāritāni iti api śabdaḥ ekā kriyā kramikā katham āśrayasya eka svabhāva tve sati ghaṭate iti yuktam tathā tatra tatra sthite iti dviṣṭhasya aneka rūpa tvāt iti ca yad uktam tad api pratikṣiptam eva yatas  iyati pūrva pakṣe iyat eva jīvitam ekam aneka svabhāvam katham syāt  iti atra ca uktam cit svabhāvasya darpaṇasya iva ekatā anapabādhanena ābhāsa bheda saṃbhave ka iva dhirodha iti tasmāt  pratyabhijñāna balāt  ekaḥ  api asau padārtha ātmā svabhāva bhedān viruddhān yāvat  aṅgīkurute tāvat  te virodhāt eva krama rūpa tayā nirbhāsamānāḥ tam ekam kriyā āśrayam saṃpādayanti iti tatas ca saṃbandha ādīnām api upapattiḥ iti nanu ca kramika tvam eva kriyāyāḥ svarūpam kramaḥ ca kāla kalanā hīne cit maye bhagavati na asti iti katham asya sā bhavet iti āśaṅkya āha utkṣipati apakṣipati hastam iti ye pūrva uttare kṣaṇāḥ te kramavantaḥ tatra yeṣām ta eva kriyā kāṇāt ādīnām iva teṣām sā sa kramā pratyakṣeṇa eva bhāti ye tu manyante tathābhūta pratyakṣa paridṛśyamāna rūpa bheda saṃpādikā yā asau kācid  atīntriyā hasta gatā śaktiḥ vyāpāra udbodha rūpā nitya anumeyā tasyāḥ kevalam pūrva aparībhūta tvam anumīyate iti laukikyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sa krama tvam kāla śakteḥ ābhāsa vi  chedana pradarśana sāmārthya rūpāt  pārameśvarāt  śakti viśeṣāt  ghaṭate upapadyate yā tu prabhoḥ saṃbandhinī tad avyatiriktā kriyāśaktiḥ śāśvatī kālena aspṛṣṭā tasyāḥ sa krama tvam asti iti saṃbhāvanā api na asti yathā prabhoḥ sa krama tvam asaṃbhāvyam tathā asyāḥ  api uktam hi hastasya sa krama tve tad gatā api kriyā tathā syāt  iti nanu kālaḥ  viśeṣa bhāvam upagacchan bhāvam svena rūpeṇa avacchinatti tatra kaḥ asau kālaḥ  nāma iti āśaṅkya āha ye iyat tayā pariniṣṭhitā ābhāsāḥ siddhāḥ tad yathā candra sūrya ādīnām sahakāra mallikā kuṭaja ādīnām śīta uṣṇa ādeḥ parabhṛta mada vilāsa ādeḥ ta eva kālaḥ yatas apariniṣṭhitam gamana paṭhana ādi taiḥ iyat tayā pariniṣṭhīyate parivartakaiḥ iva kanakam sa eva ca sūrya ādīnām svabhāva viśeṣaḥ tattvataḥ paramāśrataḥ kramaḥ  na anyaḥ kaścid  kramaḥ  nāma krama eva ca kālaḥ  na anyaḥ asau kaścid  iti eva kāraḥ  bhinna abhinna kramaḥ  yojyaḥ yaugapadyam api dvayoḥ ābhāsayoḥ apara ābhāsā apekṣayā krama eva cira kṣipra ādidhīḥ api vitata anyatva vaśāt  ābhāsa bhede krama eva paratva aparatva buddhiḥ api sphuṭatva ādinā tatra eva iti tena tena pratimāna vartaka tulyena sūrya saṃcāra ādinā saha mīyamānaḥ  hema sthānīyaḥ  devadatta ābhāsasya vaicitrya bheda ittham ucyate divasam gacchati iti nanu evam kālaḥ  nāma bhāva svabhāva eva astu kā asau kāla śaktiḥ iti āśaṅkya āha iha svabhāva bheda mātram yadi krama ātmā kālaḥ tadā aṅgulī catuṣṭayam bhonna svabhāvam iti bhinna kālam bhavet  tasmāt  aruṇa ābhāsasya sadbhāvaḥ sphuṭa prabhā puñjasya ca asadbhāvaḥ iti evaṃbhūtaḥ  yaḥ  bheda ābhāsa sadbhāva asadbhāva abhyanuprāṇitaḥ tad kṛtaḥ kramaḥ kāla ātmā tau ca ābhāsānām bhāva abhāvau na bāhya hetu kṛtau iti vistārya upapāditam iti ya eva saṃvid svabhāva ātmā sva prasaṃkalpa ādau ābhāsava citrya nirmāṇe prabhuḥ prabhaviṣṇuḥ iti sva saṃviditaḥ tata eva tau bhavataḥ sa hi ātmani nīla ādīn ābhāsān ābhāsayan citra tayā aparimeyayā bhāsayati tathā hi lohita ābhāsam ghaṭa ābhāsam unnata ābhāsam dṛḍha ābhāsam ca sāmānādhikaraṇyena ghaṭa ābhāsam paṭa ābhāsam ca pṛthaktvā avabhāsena anyonya tra ābhāsā bhāvena sva ātmani tu eka rasena ābhāsena iyati ca na kramasya udayaḥ yadā tu śarad ābhāsam hemanta ābhāsena ca sarvathā eva śūnyam ābhāsayati hemanta ābhāsam ca śārada ābhāsena tadā kāla ātmā krama uttiṣṭhati iti sā iyam itthaṃbhūtā bhāva vaicitrya prathana śaktiḥ bhagavataḥ kāla śaktiḥ iti ucyate citra ābhāsa kṛt tvam eva sphuṭayati padārthasya svam rūpam mūrtiḥ tasyāḥ yad  vaicitryam vibhedaḥ tad yathā gṛham iti anyat  svarūpam prāṅgaṇam iti anyat  vipaṇiḥ iti anyat  devakulam iti aparam udyānam iti anyat  araṇyam iti tad anyatarat  tasmāt  vaicitryāt  ābhāsyamānāt  deśa rūpaḥ  dūrādūra vitatatva avitatatva ādiḥ kramaḥ  bhagavatā avabhāsyate yadā tu gāḍha pratyabhijñā prakāśa balāt  tad eva idam hasta svarūpam iti pratipattau mūrteḥ na bhedaḥ atha ca anya anya rūpa tvam bhāti tadā ekasmin svarūpe yad anyat  anyat  rūpam tad virodha vaśāt asahabhavat kriyā ucyate tasyāḥ  yad  vaicitryam parimita aparimita ātmakam tad eka anusandhānena phala siddhi ādi nibandhana vaśāt yathāruci carcitena nirbhāsayan kāla rūpam kramam eva avabhāsayati na ca etad  vācyam eka svarūpasya katham anyat  anyat rūpam iti yatas  na asau kaścid  bhāvaḥ ya evam kalpyate saṃvid eva hi tathā bhāti tathā bhānam eva ca tasyāḥ  aiśvaryam na hi bhāsane virodhaḥ kaścid  prabhavati sa hi sukha duḥkha ādeḥ bhāsana kṛta eva tathā bhāsana abhāva eva hi virodha tattvam etad  api śabdena īśvara śabdena ca darśitam nanu evam ābhāsa viṣayābhyām eva deśa kāla kramābhyām bhavitavyam anābhāsaḥ ca pramātā sa hi na kasyacid  ābhāsate tasya sarvam ābhāti yatas  tatas ca tau pramātari katham dṛśyete ca abhavam aham bhavāmi bhavitāsmi iti gṛhe tiṣṭhāmi araṇye devagṛhe iti ca kim ca svayam deśa kāla krama śūnyasya kim dūram kim antikam kim vartamānam kim atītam kim bhāvi iti pramātrāśrayaḥ  bhāveṣu api kramaḥ  na yuktaḥ na ca pramātṛ nirapekṣeṣu api teṣu sva ātmani dūratva ādi bhūtatva ādi vā tad etad samarthayitum āha sarveṣu vastuṣu eka aneka rūpeṣu yaḥ kāla ātmā kramaḥ tasya ya ākaraḥ utpatti nibandhanam iti vyākhyātaḥ ābhāsasya bhāva abhāva kṛtaḥ  bhedaḥ sa śūnya prāṇa buddhi deha ādeḥ bhavati iti saṃbhāvyati yatas  sa śūnya ādiḥ vicchinna bhāḥ na hi tasya bhāsanam svarūpam nīla ādivat  jaḍa tvāt  api tu saṃvid sphuraṇam asya bhāsanam tad  yadā asya na asti yathā suptaḥ  dehasya saṃsāra yātrā patita tve śūnyasya prāṇa ādeḥ tadā asya bhāsanam vicchidyate iti ābhāsa sadbhāva asadbhāva kṛtaḥ kāla kramaḥ  asti atītaḥ  aham bāla deha ābhāsa rūpaḥ bhavāmi yuva deha ābhāsa rūpaḥ iti sa ca yatas  pramātā ahaṃbhāva samāveśanāt  aparipūrṇāt  ata eva udrikta kāla kramavat tvāt  bhāveṣu api kāla kramam ābhāsayati yaḥ  aham bālaḥ  abhavam tad sahabhāvī vaṭa ābhāsaḥ  api abhavat  iti na tu yaḥ sakṛt  vibhātaḥ iti anayā vācoyuktyā avicchinna bhāsanaḥ pramātā saṃvid rūpaḥ tasya sva ātmani kāla kramaḥ na api tad apekṣayā vedye bhāva jāte tad hi tatra abhedena bhāti iti evam deśa kramaḥ api mita ātmanaḥ paricchinna svarūpasya śūnya ādeḥ dehāntasya sva ātmani bhāti iha tiṣṭhāmi iti sva apekṣayā ca bhāveṣu api yad  mama saṃyoga pārimityena vartate tad antikam itarat  dūram iti amitasya svarūpeyattā śūnyasya tu saṃvid tattvasya bhāvāḥ sva ātmanā ahaṃbhāvena yatas  bhānti tatas  pūrṇāḥ aparicchinna svarūpeyattākāḥ yatas  sva ātmā tasya tathābhūta eva iti samuccaya upamā tad uktam apūrva aparam hi idam mūrtitaḥ kriyātaḥ ca sarvam sarvatas  pūrṇam iti kriyā prasaṅgāt  iha kāla kramaḥ prākarṇikaḥ  dṛṣṭānta tvena tad prasaṅgāt  deśa kramaḥ  nirūpitaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca pūrvam vācya iti vaicitrya nirūpaṇa avasare deśa kramasya ādau abhidhānam nyāyyam upasaṃhāre tu prākaraṇikasya kāla kramasya eva ādau nirdeśaḥ paścāt tu prāsaṅgikasya deśa kramasya iti nanu evam satya pramātari bhagavati na asti eva kriyā iti āyātam kāla krama abhāvāt krama āśrayeṇa ca tasyāḥ  avasthānāt  iti āśaṅkya āha iha tattvataḥ parameśvarasya apratihata svātantrya rūpa avicchinnasva ātma parāmarśa mayī ananya unmukha tā rūpā icchā eva kriyā iti upasaṃhariṣyate adhikāra antare evam icchā eva hetu tā kartṛ tā kriyā iti caitra maitra ādeḥ api pacāmi iti yā eva antar icchā sā eva kriyā tathā ca adhiśrayaṇa ādi bahutara spandana saṃbandhe api pacāmi iti na asya vicchidyate yad tu pacāmi iti icchā rūpam tad eva tathā spandana ātma tayā bhāti tatra tu na kaḥ api kramaḥ tattvataḥ evam īśvarasya api īśe bhāse sphurāmi dhūrṇe pratyavamṛśām i iti evaṃrūpam yad icchā ātmakam vimarśanam aham iti etāvat mātra tattvam na tatra kaścid  kramaḥ etad eva ca ucyate pramātṛ prameya vaicitrya krama ullasatu iti amunā vākyena tad atra api na kaścid  kramaḥ yathā tu icchā rūpam pacāmi iti spandana ātma tām kāya aparyantām gatam kramā rūpitam ābhāti tadā bhagavat icchā pramātṛ prameya bheda paryavasitā tad krama upaśliṣṭā bhāti darpaṇa talam iva vitata prabahat nadī prabāha krama samāśliṣṭam atra ca kevalam darpaṇasya tathā icchā na asti
